
-----title
河津（龙门） (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='49eb4f9b161041b0a013a64674f9a926_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("49eb4f9b161041b0a013a64674f9a926");'><span id='49eb4f9b161041b0a013a64674f9a926_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=650&endYear=660')">650-660年</a>，1-11岁</div><div id='49eb4f9b161041b0a013a64674f9a926' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=650&endYear=654')">650-654年</a>　居于家乡龙门。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=655&endYear=655')">655年</a>　居于家乡龙门.六岁即善文辞,构思无滞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=656&endYear=657')">656-657年</a>　居于家乡龙门。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=658&endYear=658')">658年</a>　居于家乡龙门.九岁读颜师古注《汉书》,并作《指瑕》以擿其失。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=659&endYear=659')">659年</a>　居于家乡龙门.诵读六经。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=660&endYear=660')">660年</a>　居于家乡龙门。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='217484acce9b4a6280acf98b2ea2354e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("217484acce9b4a6280acf98b2ea2354e");'><span id='217484acce9b4a6280acf98b2ea2354e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>，25岁</div><div id='217484acce9b4a6280acf98b2ea2354e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>　冬,还归龙门家乡,以筹远赴交州之资费。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安（长安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5dd8f772d25d40d49ea3ffa0aef10240_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5dd8f772d25d40d49ea3ffa0aef10240");'><span id='5dd8f772d25d40d49ea3ffa0aef10240_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=661&endYear=667')">661-667年</a>，12-18岁</div><div id='5dd8f772d25d40d49ea3ffa0aef10240' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=661&endYear=661')">661年</a>　从医者曹元学.并依其受《周易章句》、《黄帝素问》、《难经》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=662&endYear=662')">662年</a>　从医者曹元学.并对“上官体”表示不满,且受名流薛元超揄扬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=663&endYear=663')">663年</a>　春,与曹元别.因反对“上官体”而名满长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=664&endYear=664')">664年</a>　秋,上书右相刘祥道.获引荐。作品：《上刘右相书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷5第147页。）</span><div id='poem_1364049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上刘右相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（664年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364049")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364049'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364049'>盖闻圣人以四海为家。英宰与千龄合契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364049_comment'></div>用能不行而至。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>春霆</span>仗天地之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364049_comment'></div>以息相吹。时雨郁山川之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364049_comment'></div>故有元蛟晚集。凭鹤鼎而先鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364049_comment'></div>苍兕晨惊。运龙韬而首出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364049_comment'></div>并能风腾雾跃。指麾成烈士之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364049_comment'></div>蠖屈虬奔。谈笑坐群卿之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364049_comment'></div>未如越苍海。弃行间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364049_comment'></div>排紫微。谒天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364049_comment'></div>于是遭不讳之主。拥非常之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364049_comment'></div>龙章凤黻照其前。锵金鸣玉謺其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364049_comment'></div>三灵叶赞。超然奉天下之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364049_comment'></div>四海承平。高步取寰中之托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364049_comment'></div>君侯之富贵足矣。圣朝之付遇深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364049_comment'></div>故知阳侯息浪。长鲸卧横海之鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364049_comment'></div>风伯停机。大鹏铩垂天之翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364049_comment'></div>及其投形巨壑。触丹浦而雷奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364049_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>假势</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/34/Comments/1")'>灵飙</span>。指青霄而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>电击</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364049_comment'></div>神气洋洋。谓鳞翮使之然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364049_comment'></div>殊不知两仪超忽。动止系于无垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364049_comment'></div>万化纠纷。舒卷存乎非我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364049_comment'></div>是以陈平昔之智士也。俯同降卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364049_comment'></div>百里奚曩之达人也。亲为饿隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364049_comment'></div>当其背强敌。转康衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364049_comment'></div>雄虑耿于风云。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>危途</span>迫于朝夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364049_comment'></div>岂自期荣称相府。西藩开虎据之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364049_comment'></div>宠冠斋坛。东向举<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>熊飞</span>之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364049_comment'></div>顾盼可以荡川岳。咄嗟可以降雷雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364049_comment'></div>遂令用与不用。是非于楚汉之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364049_comment'></div>知与不知。得失于虞秦之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364049_comment'></div>故曰死生有数。审穷达者系于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364049_comment'></div>材运相符。决行藏者定于已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364049_comment'></div>君侯足下可不谓然乎。借如勃者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364049_comment'></div>眇小之一书生耳。曾无击钟鼎食之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364049_comment'></div>非有南邻北阁之援。山野悖其心迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364049_comment'></div>烟雾养其神爽。未尝降身摧气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364049_comment'></div>逡巡于列相之门。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>窃誉</span>干时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364049_comment'></div>匍匐于群公之室。所以慷慨于君侯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364049_comment'></div>有气存乎心耳。实以四海兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364049_comment'></div>齐远契于萧韩。千载风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364049_comment'></div>托<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>神知</span>于管鲍。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364049_comment'></div>则荷裳桂楫。拂衣于东海之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364049_comment'></div>菌阁松楹。高枕于北山之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364049_comment'></div>焉复区区屑屑。践名利之门哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364049_comment'></div>至尊以摇河徙岳之威。当立地开天之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364049_comment'></div>圣人有作。群材毕举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364049_comment'></div>星辰入仕。揖让朱鸟之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364049_comment'></div>风雨称臣。奔走<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>苍龙</span>之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364049_comment'></div>方欲停旒金室。引成康于已往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364049_comment'></div>辟纩瑶林。复尧舜于兹日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364049_comment'></div>可谓明明穆穆。尽天子之容貌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364049_comment'></div>抑尝闻之。丹山九仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364049_comment'></div>烟峰非数篑之功。紫极千门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364049_comment'></div>云台俟万楹之力。故天下至旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364049_comment'></div>神器不可独专。天道无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364049_comment'></div>元勋有待而立。书曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364049_comment'></div>元首明哉。股肱良哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364049_comment'></div>好问则裕。自用则小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364049_comment'></div>况掌万国之权。受一人之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364049_comment'></div>动见臧否。言知利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364049_comment'></div>君侯足下何时易耶。虽国有大命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364049_comment'></div>不资童子之言。而恭此小心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364049_comment'></div>敢进狂夫之说。伏见辽阳未靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364049_comment'></div>大军频进。有识寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364049_comment'></div>群黎破胆。昔明王之制国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364049_comment'></div>自近而及远。先仁而后罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364049_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>徵实</span>则效存。徇名则功浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364049_comment'></div>是以农疏十野。仅踰重石之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364049_comment'></div>禹截九州。不叙流沙之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364049_comment'></div>岂才不及而智有遗哉。将以辨离方而存正功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364049_comment'></div>虽至人无外。甲兵曜天子之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364049_comment'></div>王事有征。金鼓发将军之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364049_comment'></div>而长城在界。秦汉所以失全昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364049_comment'></div>巨海横流。天地所以限殊俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364049_comment'></div>辟土数千里。无益<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/149/Comments/0")'>神封</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364049_comment'></div>勒兵十八万。空疲帝卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364049_comment'></div>惊烽走传。骇秦洛之氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364049_comment'></div>飞刍挽粟。竭淮海之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364049_comment'></div>于是乘奸放命者出绳纆以生威。因公挟私者入闾阎而竞法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364049_comment'></div>虽一物失所。太阶延旰食之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364049_comment'></div>而百战方雄。中国鲜终年之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364049_comment'></div>图得而不图失。知利而不知害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364049_comment'></div>移手足之病。成心腹之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364049_comment'></div>征税屈于东西。威信蹇于表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364049_comment'></div>语曰。胜之不武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364049_comment'></div>不胜为辱。天下之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364049_comment'></div>四面至矣。诚可远凝高策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364049_comment'></div>上荐忠言。决人事于去就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364049_comment'></div>合天情于终始。遂令回麾转檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364049_comment'></div>背青邱而骛。列障分亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364049_comment'></div>巡苍波而守。昔者齐侯以力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364049_comment'></div>方城为楚国之辞。虞帝崇文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364049_comment'></div>苗人失洞庭之险。况乎仗德绥乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364049_comment'></div>以直乘邪。明逆顺之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364049_comment'></div>耸华夷之望。虽复舳舻沸海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364049_comment'></div>旌旗触天。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_95_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/191/Comments/0")'>铁山</span>四面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364049_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_96_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/192/Comments/0")'>金城千里</span>。亦不能为敌人计矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364049_comment'></div>此君侯之未谕一也。盖闻星回日运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364049_comment'></div>御洪荒者贞夫一。电照风行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364049_comment'></div>制寥廓者归乎静。易曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364049_comment'></div>复其见天地之心乎。语曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364049_comment'></div>动之斯和。绥之斯来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364049_comment'></div>是知源洁则流清。形端则影直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364049_comment'></div>大道起而仁义息。神化周而市狱定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364049_comment'></div>虽复体元立教。眚灾耀知远之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364049_comment'></div>顺时宰物。宥罪发精微之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364049_comment'></div>而况浇风易渐。淳化难归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364049_comment'></div>孔明耿介于当朝。子舆殷勤于易箦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364049_comment'></div>盖有由也。伏见边凶尚梗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364049_comment'></div>殊恩屡发。●命山泽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364049_comment'></div>日月相趋。朝脱桎梏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364049_comment'></div>夕还囹圄。奸徒抱袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364049_comment'></div>因时立侥倖之谋。顽夫顿足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364049_comment'></div>中路纡吁嗟之惨。皆由宽胜于猛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364049_comment'></div>人迷所习。劝沮不彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364049_comment'></div>廉耻相冒。亦有公卿失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364049_comment'></div>耻受圭符之任。郎官有衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364049_comment'></div>俯舍铜墨之荣。又焉可以宏长风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364049_comment'></div>抑扬众务者也。且夫朽索<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_118_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/237/Comments/0")'>充羁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364049_comment'></div>不收奔马之逸。轻缗振网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364049_comment'></div>或随吞舟之势。况非常之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364049_comment'></div>方洽于齐人。无妄之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364049_comment'></div>乃及于群小。将恐匡衡管仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364049_comment'></div>复灵诏于下泉矣。古之善为国者不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364049_comment'></div>信赏而必罚。道德而齐礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364049_comment'></div>泽配风雨而无曲惠。威振雷霆而绝私戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364049_comment'></div>交书耸币。伏慈厚之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364049_comment'></div>投金散璧。树仁明之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364049_comment'></div>故虽开衢室。盖明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364049_comment'></div>亦将四三皇而六五帝矣。此君侯之未谕二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364049_comment'></div>盖易曰。天地之大德曰生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364049_comment'></div>圣人之大宝曰位。何以守位曰仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364049_comment'></div>何以聚人曰财。是知发挥地利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364049_comment'></div>农桑启其业。振荡天功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364049_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_134_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/268/Comments/0")'>泉贝</span>流其用。伏睹前制屡扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364049_comment'></div>事非画一。廛市萧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364049_comment'></div>人情怪动。夫烦简并用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364049_comment'></div>未尽交易之宜。轻重齐行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364049_comment'></div>适启兼并之路。于是连阛掩阓者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364049_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_139_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/278/Comments/0")'>闭肆</span>而乘其屈。布衣韦带者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364049_comment'></div>阖门而受其困。五方竞爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364049_comment'></div>务浅术以相雄。百郡争胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364049_comment'></div>驱末技而成弊。田夫织妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364049_comment'></div>衣食鲜终朝之给。巨驵洪商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364049_comment'></div>舆马挟封君之势。盖有由来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364049_comment'></div>故曰国储阙于九载。则公上无所给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364049_comment'></div>家廪乏于三年。则妻子非其有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364049_comment'></div>夫阴阳覆逆。天地之常数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364049_comment'></div>百六运穷。汤尧所不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364049_comment'></div>一旦洪泉决地。大旱焦山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364049_comment'></div>风雨于一岁之间。霜雹于数州之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364049_comment'></div>繁运广役。首尾于中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364049_comment'></div>沓税增徭。日夕于都鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364049_comment'></div>燮阴阳者。将何以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364049_comment'></div>一夫窃议。公之盛德亏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364049_comment'></div>愚谓严程峻法。绝轻陋之货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364049_comment'></div>则奸镕之源塞矣。沿风正典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364049_comment'></div>重耕耘之务。则邪赢之计沮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364049_comment'></div>然后远宏教旨。大变流俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364049_comment'></div>法立有犯而必施。令出唯行而不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364049_comment'></div>违公窃铸者。具五刑之戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364049_comment'></div>因时力田者。悬一命之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364049_comment'></div>不然。则贾生晁错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364049_comment'></div>复流涕而言矣。此君侯之未谕三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364049_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_164_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/328/Comments/0")'>嵩衡</span>不拒细壤。故能崇其峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364049_comment'></div>江海不让纤流。所以存其广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364049_comment'></div>是以星台晓辟。上台忘吐握之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364049_comment'></div>月殿宵兴。中宇轸山林之慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364049_comment'></div>知夫御天下者。必待人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364049_comment'></div>诗曰。济济多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364049_comment'></div>文王以宁。未见君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364049_comment'></div>忧心如醉。伏见皇明远烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364049_comment'></div>帝采遐宣。张乐岱郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364049_comment'></div>腾勋社首。徵廉察孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364049_comment'></div>瑶坛虚不次之阶。署行议年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364049_comment'></div>璿检动非常之诏。天下可谓幸甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364049_comment'></div>于是友月朋霞之客。背<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_176_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/353/Comments/0")'>青皋</span>而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364049_comment'></div>冯唐颜驷之才。排紫阁而集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364049_comment'></div>夫岂知终始异数。泾渭同流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364049_comment'></div>萝薜失图。簪缨解体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364049_comment'></div>惜哉。群英雾散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364049_comment'></div>名侯招蔽善之嫌。天下雷同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364049_comment'></div>君子鲜长鸣之地。而欲招绝足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364049_comment'></div>致真龙。难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364049_comment'></div>此君侯之未谕四也。易曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364049_comment'></div>拔茅连茹。以其汇征吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364049_comment'></div>岂非顺物不若招类。报国不如进贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364049_comment'></div>阳事升而雨露归。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_187_1364049", 1364049, "Clauses/375/Comments/0")'>阴驾</span>凝而风霜厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364049_comment'></div>莫不观时有记。抚气相求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364049_comment'></div>穷则独善其私。达则兼善天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364049_comment'></div>而利已疵物者。以自任为身谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364049_comment'></div>知进忘退者。谓专荣而得计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364049_comment'></div>岂知夫尺波易谢。寸晷难留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364049_comment'></div>陵谷好迁。乾坤忌满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364049_comment'></div>君侯足下出纳王命。升降天衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364049_comment'></div>激扬凤扆之前。趋步麟台之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364049_comment'></div>亦复知天下有遗俊乎。夫心之精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364049_comment'></div>口不能言也。言之微妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364049_comment'></div>书不能文也。伏愿辟东阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364049_comment'></div>开北堂。待之以上宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364049_comment'></div>期之以国士。使得披肝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364049_comment'></div>布腹心。大论古今之利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364049_comment'></div>高谈帝王之纲纪。然后鹰扬豹变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364049_comment'></div>出蓬户而拜青墀。附景抟风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364049_comment'></div>舍薹衣而见绛阙。幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364049_comment'></div>斯不为难矣。庶几乎麑卵不弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364049_comment'></div>终感元枵之精。骏骨时收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364049_comment'></div>或致飞黄之锡。书生王勃死罪死罪再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364049_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_208_1364049_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=665&endYear=665')">665年</a>　经刘祥道表荐,拟应制举。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_1364057_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364057'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364057'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364057_comment'></div>某闻林腾秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364057_comment'></div>羽族知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364057_comment'></div>旸谷流谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364057_comment'></div>波臣有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364057_comment'></div>然则朝光八圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364057_comment'></div>尚欣牧竖之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364057_comment'></div>道济五残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364057_comment'></div>未隔舆人之诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364057_comment'></div>谨凭斯义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364057_comment'></div>辄呈宸游东岳颂一首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364057_comment'></div>当仁不让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364057_comment'></div>下走无惭于自媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364057_comment'></div>闻善若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364057_comment'></div>明公岂难于知我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364057_comment'></div>龙门高远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364057_comment'></div>眇黄道而无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364057_comment'></div>爵里既投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364057_comment'></div>叫丹阍而有地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364057_comment'></div>伏愿暂停左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364057_comment'></div>曲流国士之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364057_comment'></div>广进刍荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364057_comment'></div>俯息樵夫之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364057_comment'></div>轻陈径捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364057_comment'></div>退用彷徨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364057_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　上书皇甫常伯。作品：《上皇甫常伯启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷4第126页。）</span><div id='poem_1364058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上皇甫常伯启</a><span class='authorDate'>（666年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364058")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364058_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364058'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364058'>某启。一昨奉命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364058_comment'></div>令写新对台策及前后旧文。谨凭国士之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364058_comment'></div>敢进舆人之颂。窃以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364058", 1364058, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>龙镳</span>就路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364058_comment'></div>驽骏相悬。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364058", 1364058, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>鹊镜</span>临春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364058_comment'></div>妍媸自远。亦有飞霜匝地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364058_comment'></div>兰萧衔共尽之悲。列火埋冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364058_comment'></div>玉石抱俱焚之惨。然则知音罕嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364058_comment'></div>流水空存。至宝不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364058_comment'></div>荆山有泪。君侯饰扬<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364058", 1364058, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>刍议</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364058_comment'></div>提奖芜词。白圭成再见之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364058_comment'></div>黄金定一言之重。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364058", 1364058, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>鹏飙</span>既接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364058_comment'></div>仰云径而将趋。龙阪可登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364058_comment'></div>指<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364058", 1364058, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>星台</span>而有望。循襟佩德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364058_comment'></div>抚事知恩。山岳有轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364058_comment'></div>河汉无极。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364058_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1364058_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　再上皇甫常伯。作品：《再上皇甫常伯启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷4第127页。）</span><div id='poem_1364059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再上皇甫常伯启</a><span class='authorDate'>（666年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364059")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364059'>某启。自恭陈薄伎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364059_comment'></div>祗奉话言。咳唾成恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364059_comment'></div>盼睐为饰。征夫击节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364059_comment'></div>方思孤竹之风。壮士寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364059_comment'></div>实有长杨之作。谨凭严命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364059_comment'></div>轻呈乾元殿颂一首。将冀导江至海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364059_comment'></div>常以笔札见知。南馆西园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364059_comment'></div>遂与簪缨为伍。德虽无尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364059_comment'></div>攀骥尾而方遥。生也有涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364059_comment'></div>比鸿毛而非重。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364059_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1364059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　为应本年制举,向朝廷投献《宸游东岳颂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　东都造乾元殿,又上《乾元殿颂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷14第383页。）</span><div id='poem_1364042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乾元殿颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（666年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364042")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1364042_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364042'>臣闻鹏霄上廓。琼都开紫帝之庭。鳌纪下清。珍野辟黄灵之馆。兼山配极。照鸾阙于霞标。荐水涵元。湛骊宫于雾壑。斯则神徵语怪。功潜鸟迹之初。理涉非经。道昧鹑居之始。授凤书而稽碧落。仙构罕存。按龟箓而质黄图。金模间起。粤若风移处闇。层巢恢火运之机。业洎向明。上栋括河图之奥。三阶布政。咏匪日于灵台。百堵陈诗。颂斯干于考室。亦有黄轩瞰月。谯门颓九洛之功。璿闼排烟。牧野构三河之酷。御燕台而临北极。缺王度于祈招。列云阁而拒南山。陨皇谟于轵道。然则卑宫丧礼。采椽轻四海之尊。丰屋延灾。柏梁非万乘之有。虽因时立事。奢俭殊流。而宏道在人。兴亡迭运。灵光末造。不窥九室之荣。景福宏规。犹拥三方之衅。瞻风旧史。逮曹马而无讥。观迹故墟。历周隋而未得。自我唐太陵迁构。均五方于鹤几之前。中野凝图。调六气于虬床之下。坐圭台而清俯仰。晷纬齐明。临鼎邑而重威灵。风雷合响。得元功于大壮。其在兹乎。我大唐鸡浑指极。/树神宰而制山河。鹤谶裁仪。辟太虚而有天地。黄精吐瑞。潜龙苞象帝之基。紫气徵祥。鸣凤呈真王之表。高祖太武皇帝虹星湛色。开宝冑于金壶。蛟电凝阴。发皇明于石纽。白蛇宵断。行移海岳之符。苍兕晨驱。坐遘云雷之业。属东邻委驭。扇虐政于丛祠。北拱隳尊。紊皇图于宝极。蜚鸿集野。瞻乌鲜投足之因。青犊啸风。群鹿无择音之所。天街五裂。截鲸浦而飞芒。地纽三分。触鳌山而按节。元虬在御。扫圻甸而廓星都。黄鸟分麾。动扶摇而骇云阵。镳宫仗龯。跨高陌而登元。辔野韬戈。陟圯坛而拥号。皇图不恃。圣人追卷领之风。神器无私。才子奉褰裳之运。太宗皇帝云房揖契。压麟玺于庭轩。雷渚翔英。扰龙钤于周镐。八能亨运。抗鹓邸而仗朱髦。十乱恢基。临鹤州而拥黄龯。唐云秘族。潜开白水之徵。代景回轮。光践丹邱之运。权舆象纬。削茅社而建琼祧。草昧风云。席萝图而创璿历。紫庭合粹。括宇宙于宸襟。丹扆凝尊。运陶钧于宝思。摛碧霄而鍊石。上清耀魄之宫。诏寰海而捐珠。俯睇阳侯之室。功驱偃伯。顿鹗视于华封。道被来王。静龙吟于武库。元枢上运。卜年开累圣之符。丹灶升遐。遗范敞谋孙之画。皇帝陛下椒庭袭庆。曜璿萼于霞庄。兰殿分休。湛珠衡于月馆。道凝琼镇。下苍掖而照重熙。业峻铜楼。凭紫轩而揖群后。环四瀛于舜抱。漏蚁覃津。栖十景于尧衿。巢螟荷照。上元开箓。宝龟定皇邑之模。下武崇基。飞龙锡帝台之构。贞明启运。齐玉镜于鸾门。易简成功。偃铜符于鹤仗。怀降尊于襄野。太阶忘七起之劳。念负重于焦原。中席托三危之险。临翠妫而则道。天孕时成。坐元扈而被图。神超物妙。皇后星浔纵淑。曳珠绂于铜皋。云野疏祥。抗琼枝于桂浦。素蟾登庆。六虚充牝马之贞。丹雀衔休。三雅合关雎之好。璿宫夜静。居龙幰而调元。金屋晨开。御鸳阶而缉化。芝庭揖训。远清和凤之仪。兰佩承风。竞峻当熊之节。皇太子承云紫座。翊八柱于乾维。湛粹青衢。揖三枢于地户。黄离踵曜。太阳分铣树之辉。苍震荐音。少海控银河之色。鹤筌飞奏。想丹驾于琼山。鲍俎捐芳。齿元冠于宝序。彤闱问竖。礼崇监抚之威。黼席兴贤。义极君亲之爱。若乃东门恤允。謺仙构于熊山。西苑承家。导灵波于雁沼。桐圭作瑞。凤毛曜丹穴之英。茅壤分维。麟距冠元邱之俊。巽宫延粹。辟朱柱于娥台。兑野流芬。疏紫兰于别馆。频隈毓范。云扃分戚里之驩。覃屿凝规。星阁绝郎官之请。雕龙命职。纵跳泽而骧鳞。翠鴳调司。顺义飙而抚翼。月轩宵伫。虞溪降璿纬之精。震帐晨披。姜水洞金韬之赜。飞鹤书而抽海状。桂壑于是投纶。转麟旆而揖山容。松涧由其削衽。轩图瑞矞。泛花绶于鸡林。农纪祥炎。濯兰缨于凤水。仙台俶务。三圭铨棘序之风。天秩调邦。六府燮槐衢之典。金门献纳。纵麟笔于苔笺。石馆论思。覈龟章于竹椠。淹中访礼。蹲龙摇璧水之波。稷下谈经。飞兔跃环林之秀。词庭吐凤。玩鸟迹于春黉。书帐翻萤。阅虫文于夏阁。杏花千亩。绀辕照磨蜃之功。桑柘三宫。元绂降亲蚕之礼。圆邱上辟。奉苍璧于灵坛。方泽下凝。列黄琮于宝墠。朱弦翠瓒。履霜怀四飨之尊。复霤重檐。涓日正三纲之首。五灵奔庆。冠蛇泽于黄枢。六祀衔欣。飏麟烟于绀席。遗弓积慕。虔深太庙之仪。执豆推恩。道振明堂之礼。瑶山广乐。备逸调于宫悬。洞庭仙奏。纳遗歌于帝府。九韶分唱。后夔清桂序之音。六变同和。飞凤掌梧轩之律。樽俎折旋之数。苞举阴阳。堂庭节奏之规。弥纶宇宙。灵襟索隐。控风伯于词林。睿想钩深。诏天吴于笔海。神穷独照。傍探赤水之珍。思洽几深。回写丹溪之韵。金坛紫露。映银籀而翻华。瑶林白雪。/藻琼章而吐绚。蝉机撮化。铜浑将九圣齐悬。虬箭司更。银漏与三辰合运。爽鸠分职。素云颓马喙之祥。神獬关司。元水照龙颜之则。黄沙鞠草。刬丛棘而迁讹。丹石滋苔。仰甘棠而息讼。融皋再稔。方闻外户之谣。昧谷千箱。坐溢康衢之奏。百城烟峙。望秋露而乘风。千室云开。合宵霆而组化。彤帏独选。熊轓下芦雁之祥。墨绶分贤。犀检降槐鸾之祉。筠骖伫信。髦士剖竹而相寻。苇杖沾仁。鲐叟攀轮而不暇。龙蛇可践。野人丰荷杖之驩。鸡犬相闻。城尉辍鸣桴之响。五云抽润。湛芳气于璿台。六府咸殷。唱丰歌于铜阙。不戒而东户。恩周动植之津。博施而举南风。化偃胎萌之寓。神谋备预。严七萃于丹枢。邃略防微。肃千庐于紫卫。元戎握节。黄公授犀阙之图。帝座闻鼙。元女荐龙庭之策。赪柯捭刃。中权决胜于两阶。白羽俄麾。善阵推亡于四表。朱匡反景之域。削蛇弭于文㮰。黑山明月之乡。委龙琛于武帐。锦轩星骛。控乾络而观风。绣服霞惊。浃坤纮而问俗。川浮没羽。鲸溪静丹浦之虞。陆荐飞毛。熊巘动青云之侦。银关骤雨。望紫陌而趋恩。铁幌驰风。计彤闱而沥思。赤马文猿之宝。丛积乎郊虞。纨牛露犬之贡。满盈乎储邸。青邱画野。/不踰征赋之乡。苍水奉图。未尽堤封之贯。且夫纬武经文。宏业也。含幽育明。至诚也。混齐六合。大功也。规模百代。昌数也。故能袭九空而宁庶物。划千里而统诸侯。休徵象德而动。嘉符触类而至。风扬晷洽。藻乾庆于芳年。司节河清。蔼坤祯于明渚。瑶枝结庆。泉埃荡玉盖之文。琼液浮甘。天酒缀金茎之色。黄麰紫脱。凑仙颖于中畿。翠箑丹蓂。謺灵株于上序。骈眸候日。漾影蒙池。比翰翻风。栖光理木。祥飞井络。震鳞题瑞朔之元。祉绚新郊。枵兽纪和年之序。具灵篇之绝贶。究仙牒之殊休。天人之际交矣。皇帝之道备矣。由是三灵物睹。扣兰禁而栖诚。九服子来。咏蒿宫而骋力。去奢去甚。不矜黄屋之隆。匪朴匪雕。方顺丹墀之请。宸规相宅。考周旧于灵都。睿览思和。获秦馀于正殿。群臣列陛。奏萧相之遗模。天子临轩。采荀卿之故事。炎洲八桂。簉仙栱于林衡。岱畎五松。委灵材于梓匠。衢宫记范。万机抗九户之尊。海孽移琛。千栾省十家之费。飞廉卷霭。彻烟极而浮薨。屏翳收津。划星墟而置椠。瑶阶百雉。光悬宝露之坛。琼璧万寻。影綷崇霞之阁。拖虹梁而四注。星汉亏于上荣。謺云栋而三休。寒暑隔于中霤。雕楣鹤企。沓势分规。绣桷虬奔。殊形别起。图珰布藻。罄羽璧于狼泉。方镜披莲。孕花机于蜃浦。芝楼对幄。薰传五日之风。芸阁列钱。彩锻三旬之雾。文疏罩迥。阴兔息肩于绮寮。翠幌笼霄。阳乌铩翼于珠网。丰隆按节。下复橑而司阶。列缺施鞭。低丛楹而假道。温房伫幸。煦芳景于佳辰。凉室乘閒。凛徂飙于火序。金铺夕照。若帝圃之耀琼英。宝缀晨悬。类阿房之聚银烛。烟邱碧桂。翊珉陛而披香。雨岫赪筠。夹璿流而飏影。九衢翻翠。杂仙卉于中逵。四照霏红。间灵葩于右墄。神禽率舞。光浮肆夏之轩。瑞鸟相鸣。响叶钧天之乐。钩陈宿列。俨双碣于丹霄。绮徼霞周。辟千门于紫露。尔其左扃嵩镇。申侯降太室之祯。前枕莘郊。伊尹发空桑之秀。揭熊山而北眺。贝阙犹存。睹龟溜而西分。琼台易接。总交中宇。廓川陆而疏畿。竟想善邻。揆风霜而建野。然则因秦构极。祖宗耀金策之符。作洛恢基。我后创璿居之始。援天引圣。隔代重晖。横紫都而可袭。配元宫而非远。故能使神光夜烛。镜麟趾于文除。仙渰晨华。委鸾章于绣础。灵爻密发。八方昭大有之和。宝篆潜开。六合启同人之会。两仪交庆。虚碧墠而翘旌。万宇披欢。指苍车而候跸。虽青蒲颂德。东朝献龙凤之图。而丹极鸣谦。南面动貂羊之诏。百神推策。望璆径而虔诚。三让奉符。顾瑶坛而肃事。龟书吐瑞。按五校而分营。凤策扬辉。翔八鸾而节步。帷宫雾转。列芝盖于中天。帐殿星离。轫蒲轮于大野。紫鳞充馈。若大帝之共临。素鹤翔华。类群仙之广宴。花开瑞雪。委琼馔而调芳。䌽绚祥云。夹珠旗而曳影。功推三祖。银绳勒东岱之威。业峻一人。金筴奉南山之寿。道既成矣。元符集矣。代既贞矣。元勋缉矣。运三辰而虚玉柄。风兑涣其中孚。悬五礼而偃金科。雷坎光其作解。奔烽举爵。溢仙酒于中衢。謺鼓分肴。浃宸辉于下里。吞九皇而上运。控八圣而遐征。翔赤骥而睇风区。吟翠虬而掩霄甸。隐隐轰轰。雷动天惊。回舆斜盼。而降乎乾元之殿。司宫庀职。肃坁堮而神行。掌舍巡方。焕岩廊而洞启。赫若朱螭。负汉而辉横海之鳞。默若苍鹏。架壑而振垂天之翮。千官晓次。傃银榜而端簪。万户宵披。候琼膏而肃带。灵戈列陛。天官具三揖之仪。云辂充庭。宗伯演九宾之礼。瑶鲸戒响。悬猛𥵂于端闱。铜狄分形。肃严扃于左序。排紫微而立极。宸仪冠明后之三。俯黄道而披轩。仙历用乾元之九。荡荡乎何圣人之无外。巍巍乎而神功之不穷也。臣勃席芳十步。企景三冬。虽承宣室之谈。犹窘灵台之影。仙坛远秘。已多谢于祥鹣。大厦初成。复攀荣于贺雀。慨深梁甫。终乖捧日之欢。恩极甘泉。未动凌云之价。神图不测。固流绚于丹縢。微志可存。庶镌芳于翠琬。敢献颂曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364042'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364042'>紫扃垂耀，黄枢镇野。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1364042'>银树霜披，珠台月写。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1364042'>向明立极，横神廓社。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1364042'>大壮摛爻，斯干韵雅<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_3_1364042_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1364042'>鹑居化没，狙讹道长。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1364042'>琼构霞明，璜轩露厂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1364042'>弃人崇欲，违天蠹象。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1364042'>南巢不救，东邻长往<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_7_1364042_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1364042'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364042", 1364042, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>瑶缄</span>考懿，金板藏功。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1364042'>道凝茅屋，业盛蒿宫。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1364042'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364042", 1364042, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>龙阶</span>察祲，鹓阁调风。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1364042'>推访华礼，酌俭思冲<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_11_1364042_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1364042'>悬漦结衅，傅翼生灾。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1364042'>千薨岭接，万栱星开。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1364042'>争图绚侈，福极凶来。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1364042'>风寒碣馆，露惨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364042", 1364042, "Clauses/31/Comments/1")'>苏台</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_15_1364042_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1364042'>十馆营秦，金房<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364042", 1364042, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>砥室</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1364042'>千间架汉，韬云閟日。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1364042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1364042'>济恶承危，同亡异术。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　投文干谒贺兰敏之,有《上武侍极启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷4第120页。）</span><div id='poem_1364055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上武侍极启</a><span class='authorDate'>（666年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364055")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364055'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364055'>某启。某闻元螭掩耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364055_comment'></div>光销赤堇之芒。白鹤摧辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364055_comment'></div>影灭青胡之宝。由是紫氛霄耿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364055_comment'></div>指牛汉而忘归。丹水神迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364055_comment'></div>道骊泉而罔悔。其有龙文已远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364055_comment'></div>轻图剸兕之功。鱼目滥持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364055_comment'></div>自拟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>灵蛇</span>之色。循荣览分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364055_comment'></div>朝闻夕可。君侯缔华椒阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364055_comment'></div>席宠芝扃。粲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>貂冕</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/17/Comments/1")'>金轩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364055_comment'></div>藻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>龟章</span>于玉署。月开鸾镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364055_comment'></div>怀精鉴以分形。霜湛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>虬钟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364055_comment'></div>蕴希声而待物。吞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>九溟</span>于笔海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364055_comment'></div>若控牛涔。抗五岳于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>词峰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364055_comment'></div>如临<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>蚁垤</span>。驰魂雾谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364055_comment'></div>忻逢紫岫之英。驿思霞邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364055_comment'></div>伫接<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>青田</span>之响。某北岩曲艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364055_comment'></div>东皋下节。攀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>翰苑</span>而思齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364055_comment'></div>傃文风而立志。迹疲千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364055_comment'></div>未陪丹毂之游。叶契三英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364055_comment'></div>尚隔黄衣之梦。谨凭洪贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364055_comment'></div>辄录旧文。轻敢上呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364055_comment'></div>列之如右。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364055", 1364055, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>涓波</span>有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364055_comment'></div>望日谷以驰诚。钟鼓无施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364055_comment'></div>伏雷门而假息。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364055_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364055_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　投文干谒贺兰敏之,有《再上武侍极启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷4第123页。）</span><div id='poem_1364056' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364056' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364056?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再上武侍极启</a><span class='authorDate'>（666年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364056")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364056_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364056'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364056'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364056_comment'></div>一昨不缘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364056", 1364056, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>媒绍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364056_comment'></div>轻承盼饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364056_comment'></div>祗宠相惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364056_comment'></div>俯仰无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364056_comment'></div>何则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364056_comment'></div>循方极弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364056_comment'></div>尚亏风雨之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364056_comment'></div>抚翼濡鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364056_comment'></div>犹失江湖之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364056_comment'></div>况乎九天<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364056", 1364056, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>鹏术</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364056_comment'></div>一代龙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364056_comment'></div>荣枯舛致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364056_comment'></div>山川在目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364056_comment'></div>而可以追腾白日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364056_comment'></div>忘言于咫尺之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364056_comment'></div>干突青云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364056_comment'></div>投迹于寻常之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364056_comment'></div>徒以北林增秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364056_comment'></div>弱翰知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364056_comment'></div>东壑流谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364056_comment'></div>纤鳍未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364056_comment'></div>神交道合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364056_comment'></div>君侯昭片善之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364056_comment'></div>千载一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364056_comment'></div>下走得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364056", 1364056, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>长鸣</span>之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364056_comment'></div>是用谬凭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364056", 1364056, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>高奖</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364056_comment'></div>曲撰芜音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364056_comment'></div>游海无际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364056_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364056", 1364056, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>过雷</span>自詟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364056_comment'></div>虽黄金激愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364056_comment'></div>指秦路而方穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364056_comment'></div>苍璧惭恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364056_comment'></div>伏焦原而未远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364056_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1364056_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　应幽素举及第,为朝散郎.沛王李贤征为侍读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>　在沛王府,上《平台钞略》十篇,沛王爱重之,赐帛五十匹。作品：《平台钞略十篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷11第301页;卷15第427页。原作仅存论、赞部分。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='268627c9877046daa39dfa5b39720841_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("268627c9877046daa39dfa5b39720841");'><span id='268627c9877046daa39dfa5b39720841_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=668')">667-668年</a>，18-19岁</div><div id='268627c9877046daa39dfa5b39720841' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>　返京后,注《黄帝八十一难经》完成并作序。作品：《黄帝八十一难经序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷9第266页。）</span><div id='poem_1364064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄帝八十一难经序</a><span class='authorDate'>（667年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364064")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364064'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364064'>黄帝八十一难经。是医经之秘录也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364064_comment'></div>昔者岐伯以授黄帝。黄帝历九师以授伊尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364064_comment'></div>伊尹以授汤。汤历六师以授太公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364064_comment'></div>太公授文王。文王历九师以授医和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364064_comment'></div>医和历六师以授秦越人。秦越人始定立章句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364064_comment'></div>历九师以授华佗。华佗历六师以授黄公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364064_comment'></div>黄公以授曹夫子。曹夫子讳元字真道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364064_comment'></div>自云京兆人也。盖授黄公之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364064_comment'></div>洞明医道。至能遥望气色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364064_comment'></div>彻视腑脏。洗肠刳胸之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364064_comment'></div>往往行焉。浮沈人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364064_comment'></div>莫有知者。勃养于慈父之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364064_comment'></div>每承过庭之训曰。人子不知医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364064_comment'></div>古人以为不孝。因窃求良师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364064_comment'></div>阴访其道。以大唐龙朔元年岁次庚申冬至后甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364064_comment'></div>予遇夫子于长安。抚勃曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364064_comment'></div>无欲也。勃再拜稽首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364064_comment'></div>遂归心焉。虽父伯兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364064_comment'></div>不能知也。盖授周易章句及黄帝素问难经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364064_comment'></div>乃知三才六甲之事。明堂玉匮之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364064_comment'></div>十五月而毕。将别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364064_comment'></div>谓勃曰。阴阳之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364064_comment'></div>不可妄宣也。针石之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364064_comment'></div>不可妄传也。无猖狂以自彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364064_comment'></div>当阴沈以自深也。勃受命伏习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364064_comment'></div>五年于兹矣。有升堂睹奥之心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364064_comment'></div>近复钻仰太虚。导引元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364064_comment'></div>觉滓秽都绝。精明相保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364064_comment'></div>方欲坐守神仙。弃置流俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364064_comment'></div>噫。苍生可以救耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364064_comment'></div>斯文可以存耶。昔太上有立德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364064_comment'></div>其次有立功。其次有言言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364064_comment'></div>非以徇名也。将以济人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364064_comment'></div>谨录师训。编附圣经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364064_comment'></div>庶将来君子。有以得其用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364064_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1364064_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年3月</a>　三月,上《九成宫颂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷13第339页。）</span><div id='poem_1364044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九成宫颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（668年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364044")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1364044_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364044'>臣闻在天垂曜。璿宫列乾象之墟。在地班形。珠阙镇坤灵之野。洎夫三精軿运。即寥廓而为宫。九圣旋游。遍洪荒而可宅。则有瑶房玉室。昆山分大帝之庭。金屋银台。沧海濯元元之宇。岂非神明其道。骋仙辔于无垠。浩荡其居。示清都于不宰。若夫扃牖六合。奔走八神。占日月而揆山川。驾阴阳而法天地。非圣人其孰能与于此乎。至若文开遁甲。仇峰城苍后之躔。乐奏钧天。峒岭驻黄轩之驾。业融环堵。下姑射而寻真。道济岩廊。望衡山而展觌。斯则三阶遍下。唯临布政之宫。六位时乘。未睹巡方之馆。其后两龙齐骛。抗琼闼而同嬉。八骏高骧。指瑶池而结兴。殷风不竞。砂邱雄别馆之娱。秦道无章。云阁绚殊庭之赏。于是功亏大壮。颂阙祈招。丰屋同亡。危辀继及。遂使来年候迹。名山为纵观之场。并海遵河。沃野尽行宫之地。皇天震怒于上苍。黎氓恸哭于下土。其有斟酌千古。文明一代。蒿宫不陋。茨山可仰。祈诚东岳。唐帝复衢室之尊。用飨西岐。天子合钧台之运。得其道也。盖有存焉。国家梯霄架极。罄域裁基。纂高邱白云之裔。郁函都紫气之兆。宸扉既辟。一宇宙而来王。圣箓潜跻。贰乾坤而作帝。高祖天旗夜立。制黄马而先驱。太宗日驭晨飞。骖绿螭而首出。虽立极承祧之业。进烛前文。而重光累洽之符。归功下武。陛下承灵太乙。踵睿登三。星虹沓祉。电虬发庆。丹书碧篆。神符焕河洛之文。玉斗珠衡。天骨挺皇王之表。用能舍桐圭而宣匕鬯。肃玉籍而揖宗祧。写霭九天。腾景万里。御风雷七曜于上。博临之功显。用山川六府而下。辅相之宜得。元宫密运。敷造化于灵襟。黄屋神凝。创经纶于宝思。凤闱宵静。阴灵宣玉阃之华。鹤禁朝趋。离象峻铜楼之景。川分帝子。控鲲壑而疏源。岳动天孙。拥熊山而列镇。其化成也如彼。其强干也如此。犹乃停旒正室。俨纩中轩。玉阶匪泰。金门为险。停虹旃于月涧。岳渎生光。飞鹤盖于烟皋。江湖动色。桃溪逸彦。塞丹井而归风。松磴遗英。斩元关而奉制。位兼河海。九卿参巨济之功。道合星辰。三事郁经天之象。朱轓缉化。泣故老于中溪。墨绶宣风。绕春童于上陌。王化之基已洽。天工之代有序。建铜仪而测曜。象纬齐悬。按璿玑而书云。祯氛謺举。祥嗈十二。紫鹓调夏谷之音。大礼三千。赪蛇应黄钟之曲。蚕功顺令。业著于青裳。蜃磨迎春。恩周于黛耜。黄砂静谳。爽鸠兴顿足之悲。丹石销冤。神獬辍摧锋之计。咏时和于帝壤。动植咸驩。歌道泰于华封。昆虫自乐。星墟列将。辉玉节而长驱。天策神兵。下金坛而决胜。横麾赤坂。葱山成不战之郊。命缴青邱。桃野见其亡之兆。烟驰火徼。励珠产而移琛。雪骛冰洲。驾瑶溪而纳赆。乾坤径复。载遵赤县之封。曦望环周。未出黄图之域。故夫含吐万物。至功也。制乎八表。大业也。一阴一阳。神道也。乃文乃武。圣图也。用能使天不爱宝。地不藏珍。日月五行。风云四序。龙章凤彩。舄奕于郊墟。黄铉紫玉。磊砢于坰圃。集灵风于翠箑。浴甘露于朱英。泽马飞镳。山舆结辙。殊徽狎至。祥书竭东郭之毫。累译同归。朝册尽南山之竹。然后瑶坛备物。陈帝服而展皇仪。后室畴庸。登太山而小天下。功宏事毕。狭广宙而三迁。风举云摇。历神都而一憩。考遗基于汶上。稽故典于淹中。光总章之瑞纪。嗣乾封之宝历。大矣哉。升中作睿。握四海而为尊。则大斯模。肇三宫而配永。凭太室而高视。灵坛八百。坐明堂而恭已。诸侯一万。时既贞矣。襄城辞访道之游。功既成矣。元圃顿寻仙之驾。由是南宫奏议。和元禁而成章。西土讴歌。指皇舆而伫眷。咸以珍台靓穆。阳灵开避暑之宫。清序钧调。景福制追凉之殿。然则高栋深宇。威神之大节也。顺气发生。巡游之大功也。况乎石城金室。偏兴井鬼之区。珠薮瑶池。宛在秦豳之境。应雷軿而出豫。苍帝其时。面炎驭而思和。朱明不远。虽涂吟野忭。黎元忻望幸之符。而屈已从人。天子下劳谦之诏。候离宫而从宴。尚惕三危。清近县而移銮。犹详再驾。以为三十六所。帝刘非舜禹之心。四十二宫。全赵异成康之历。咏荆台而夕厉。思蒲坂而晨凝。方奉后天之期。俯顺观风之请。万灵禔祉。三辰合庆。姬文考筮。容成奏日。千旌凤转。俨镂象而星陈。万骑龙嘶。伐灵鼍而晓彻。静帷宫于绿野。肃帐殿于黄街。奔欃枪而走陆梁。陈浮灵而侯明月。前驱电竦。下列缺于腾鞭。后乘雷惊。起丰隆于骤毂。琼戈昼洒。太阳疲转日之锋。玉剑宵翻。悬象暗冲星之气。天旋雾散。岳运川回。林兵护野。方神启路。黄麾紫盖。杂真气而西浮。云动神行。背封峦而右指。吐雾驰风。以臻夫九成宫。礼也。尔时峰横地乳。景戴天糜。分阆井而图基。荫秦星而耀阯。灵墟宝藏。代兴雍之间。峻阜长岑。謺镇岐梁之域。丹溪碧洞。吐纳虹霓。灌柏丛篁。腾迁雨露。获秦馀于故兆。地拟林光。访周旧于遗风。山连水浒。前趋剑栈。玉垒千寻。傍望斗城。金墉万仞。架阴邱而北走。境瞰鄜祠。分沓嶂而西驰。涂交陇坂。仙都密迩。犹连上苑之扃。灵宫岿然。直透崇冈之曲。即乔基于涧道。利在斯干。固拱木于虞衡。规同匪日。弥峰跨谷。层城万转。庇险乘危。回廊四注。山祇尽石。出徼道而终年。风伯赢粮。半长途而中宿。架千楼而致极。烂若神扶。罗万户而窥天。巍如化立。离堂早照。皦日笼光于绮寮。合殿宵深。归云纳影于重庑。珉房砥室。画栱相望。绿岫红岩。雕栊间出。元熊蚺䗊。俯栋宇而危心。青鸟归飞。仰棂轩而坠翼。转飞檐于秀㟧。上出重冥。荫反宇于回溪。下临无地。红葩紫的。垂倒井而披文。金锁银铺。接重扃而炫色。俨钩陈于汉陌。泰阶非远。设陛戟于烟庄。仙梯可陟。华珰璧散。挂明月于崇朝。密网珠连。落奔星于已曙。丹梁发秀。彩沓虹文。皓壁凝鲜。光涵蜃气。铜龙对霤。接飞泉而瀑流。铁凤连甍。溯还飙而伫立。虽南缠统序。北室开荣。凛劲气于丛楹。起凄风于洞穴。踆乌失辔。出涧户而无光。金兔低轮。下山扉而变色。阴庭阻夏。祝融无窃据之因。邃屋乘春。颛顼定忘归之策。飞廉扣响。超北阙而神寒。屏翳收津。跼南端而股战。苍苍八桂。白露为霜。落落千松。元阴昧景。金人列陛。来危砌而思裘。玉女窥窗。伏曾峦而请纩。阳秋代驾。不凋仙囿之华。天地为炉。未解幽陵之冻。至若气清乾步。景霁山维。栖翠霭于崇荣。列朱霞于复榭。琼枝累道。移缀文㮰。碧树周阿。光瑶镂槛。静帘帷而洞启。穆羽相和。肃坻堮而天临。纤尘不动。宸仪有晬。蓬莱与城阙俱荣。群后多欢。萝薜共簪裾合赏。岩花落砌。缀龙扆而成文。嶂叶交轩。拂鸾旗而追影。炉峰转霭。香传玉几之风。石濑鸣湍。响入铜壶之水。乃有陵阳驾鹤。奉丹墀而称臣。子晋吟鸾。下青蒲而谒帝。箕精失曜。傅说恭命于东厢。昴宿低芒。庭坚奉职于西序。三台九署。云端极目。霓裳凤髻。阙下相寻。张良卧疾。攀赤松而有地。绮季来朝。歌紫芝而忘返。若夫功成旰食。道济宵衣。汉宫追听览之馀。尧殿得巡来之隙。霞登月憩。光睿幸于彤闱。玉振金声。藻宸章于翠掖。洛阳才子。承閒尽宣室之谈。蜀郡词人。还奏动甘泉之赋。复有轩庭十四。出桂阃而乘茵。永巷三千。望椒涂而奉币。翊鸾台之广晏。扈鸳砌之仙游。罗绮芳兮四面春。环佩鸣兮九重暮。风闺夕敞。携少女于歌筵。月幌宵胧。下姮娥于舞席。元房俟宴。云姬辞豹尾之欢。绀幄承颜。星媛入鱼鳞之戏。若乃屯营栉比。对閤道而斜趋。廨寺棋分。混文昌而外属。周朝瑞鸑。声参叶律之宫。陈宝鸣鸡。响杂司晨之序。名都广会。闾阎万室。帝籞仙垣。亭皋千里。山村野塾。家连菌草之园。谷饮川居。户有桃符之水。故夫恩加草树。囿原泽而无私。道被翔行。苑山川而不禁。每至旻天戒序。高风啸律。虞官献秋狝之仪。司马奉梁驺之典。将军布卒。略元灞而东驰。都尉关营。绕黄山而北睇。于是逢蒙列阶。蚩尤并毂。材官发射。期门走仞。杖元麾而直指。鹗视千群。奋朱鬣而横行。龙骧万计。层旗广旆。出宇宙而三驱。謺鼓鸣钟。运雷霆而一呼。前旌逐日。夸父断洪河之流。后骑超山。共伯挟昆崙之柱。近陵吐燄。缛奔电于长锋。灌莽生尘。陨飞霜于劲镞。合戈鋋而照地。猛兕知穷。振罟网而笼天。腾龙失据。崩林磔石。毛群无挺险之资。荫泽风山。羽族落垂云之影。长围躞蹀。得骏马于秦坰。大辂徜徉。载飞熊于渭浦。然后还师振旅。考事陈功。皮轩按节。牙璋复路。祝馀生于大野。誓广校于长陬。班腥于巀㠔之墟。省蜡于长杨之馆。命奔烽而举釂。火照甘泉。总轻骑而行庖。云惊上路。声兼万籥。歌钟空广乐之庭。礼被三雍。玉帛尽涂山之会。龙胎凤卵。入禹膳而调芳。石乳琼浆。委尧樽而湛色。恩沾下帛。宴液仙宫。虽大夫思濯鹢之欢。而天子可回鸾之奏。然后拜釐清庙。考德斋宫。用元功而不有。宅太虚而无迹。勋崇易简。规万祀而化黄金。道贯幽明。徵百灵而飨丹甑。得元珠于舜海。尚警冰危。朗天镜于尧仪。犹勤日昃。虔恭上帝。东朝悬待谏之旌。清问下人。南面听登闻之鼓。则有郊童候跸。敢让天师。野老排阍。唯歌帝力。风行比屋。忠臣收折槛之谋。化溢康衢。良使息埋轮之请。设神规而动俗。庶绩其凝。握元符而发祉。殊方合应。华胥已泰。济群生于不死之庭。阊阖可观。致仙历于无穷之境。荡荡乎发育万物而显诸仁。洋洋乎包举六气而藏诸用。均两仪而得一。耻三皇而不四者矣。臣勃东皋贱节。北阜幽姿。常叨召见之恩。骤玷明扬之列。书生谒相。望阙推轮。下客游梁。荣参赐帛。终童立志。空投函谷之繻。马令同时。未给尚书之笔。虽元机妙键。已寂兆于忘言。而咏德陈功。请追声于匪颂。其词曰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1364044'>望夷有衅，甘泉不祀<span class='inlineComment2'>（其六）</span>。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_23_1364044_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1364044'>宛郊嗣箓，谯乡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364044", 1364044, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>警众</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_24_1364044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1364044'>蜀跨梁岷，吴吞楚梦。<div id='poem_sentence_25_1364044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1364044'>顺时宣节，分戎讲将。<div id='poem_sentence_84_1364044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_1364044'>星骑朝飞，云罗夕张。<div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_1364044'>酆庭未远，涂山有戮。<div id='poem_sentence_88_1364044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_1364044'>襄野迷轩，清都宥穆。<div id='poem_sentence_91_1364044'>光总大猷，允归天禄<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二十三）</span>。<span class='charType'>（二十二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_91_1364044_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1364044'>合宫垂训，灵台韵雅。<div id='poem_sentence_92_1364044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_1364044'>功映寰中，颂流天下。<div id='poem_sentence_93_1364044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_94_1364044'>皇图已泰，鸿笔难假。<div id='poem_sentence_94_1364044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_1364044'>帝有力焉，恶非能者<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二十四）</span>。<span class='charType'>（二十三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_95_1364044_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_1364044'></div><div id='poem_sentence_96_1364044_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年</a>　夏,为东台侍郎张文瓘作《九成宫东台山池赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷1第24页。）</span><div id='poem_1364030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364030?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九成宫东台山池赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（668年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364030")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364030_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364030'>九成宫东台。地接閒旷。面山临水。尔其松峰桂壑。红泉碧磴。金石千声。云霞万色。侍郎张公。雅思沈郁。永怀梓匠。式侔仙造。聿构灵廛。纤波成止水之源。拳石俨干霄之状。虽流波覆篑。俯藉人机。而布叶攒花。妙同天绘。仆因夏日。滥奉清埃。敢抽南亩之才。聊叙东山之事云尔。辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364030'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364030'>若夫金台妙境。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>玉署</span>仙居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364030_comment'></div>酌丹墀之晓暇。候青禁之宵馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364030_comment'></div>骤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>冲情</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>月道</span>。飞峻赏于烟墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364030_comment'></div>指山楹而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>思逸</span>。怀水镜而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>神虚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364030_comment'></div>既而仰瞻赪峤。傍窥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>黛壑</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364030_comment'></div>复嶂烟回。攒溪雾错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364030_comment'></div>伟沈用之兼济。想神功之可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364030_comment'></div>规謺巘于盘龙。宪飞泉于挂鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364030_comment'></div>覆篑而营岩磴。浮芥而环洲堮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364030_comment'></div>采拳石于溪滨。搴纤珠于绮薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364030_comment'></div>萍徙楚江之蒂。花转昆墟之萼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364030_comment'></div>岫蕴玉而虹惊。浦涵珠而星落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364030_comment'></div>美仁智之同归。信高深之纵托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364030_comment'></div>尔其危岑漏影。曲渚留寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364030_comment'></div>高松偃鹤。清筱吟鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364030_comment'></div>被兰邱而结佩。照莲服而披冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364030_comment'></div>激坳堂于别溆。引肤寸于危峦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364030_comment'></div>若乃岭横鸡秀。波连凤液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364030_comment'></div>花鸟萦红。蘋鱼漾碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364030_comment'></div>绿衣元衽。赪鳞翠额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364030_comment'></div>在林薮而同驩。望江湖而齐适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364030_comment'></div>每至景沈西㟧。月下东滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364030_comment'></div>峰深夜久。潭静秋新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364030_comment'></div>荷抽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>水盖</span>。薜引山茵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364030_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>雪芝</span>献液。露菊倾津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364030_comment'></div>嗣南商之逸兴。有东海之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364030", 1364030, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>遐宾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364030_comment'></div>保林泉而肆赏。混簪绂而同尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364030_comment'></div>何濯缨之有地。如攀桂之无因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364030_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1364030_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年7月</a>　七月,作《七夕赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷1第15页。）</span><div id='poem_1364034' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364034?labeling=true' target='_blank'>七夕赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（668年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364034")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364034'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364034'>若夫乾灵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>鹊谶</span>之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364034_comment'></div>地辅龙骖之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364034_comment'></div>凭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>紫都</span>而授历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364034_comment'></div>按元邱而命纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364034_comment'></div>凤毛钟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>桂阃</span>之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364034_comment'></div>麟角灿椒庭之祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364034_comment'></div>驰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>朱轩</span>于九域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364034_comment'></div>振黄麾于万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364034_comment'></div>抗芝馆而星罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364034_comment'></div>擢兰宫而霞起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364034_comment'></div>则有皇慈雾洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364034_comment'></div>圣握天浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364034_comment'></div>庭分<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>玉禁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364034_comment'></div>邸瞰金楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364034_comment'></div>剪凫洲于细柳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364034_comment'></div>披<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>鹤籞</span>于长楸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364034_comment'></div>启<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>鱼钤</span>而分帝术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364034_comment'></div>授虹璧而控神州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364034_comment'></div>拥黄山于石磴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364034_comment'></div>泄元灞于铜沟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364034_comment'></div>列<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>瑶窗</span>而送燠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364034_comment'></div>辟银榜而迎秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364034_comment'></div>君王乃排青幌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364034_comment'></div>摇朱舄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364034_comment'></div>戒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>鹓舆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364034_comment'></div>静<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>鸾掖</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364034_comment'></div>绕震廊而转步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364034_comment'></div>傃云阡而纵迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364034_comment'></div>啸陈客于金床。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364034_comment'></div>命淮仙于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>桂席</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364034_comment'></div>翔翠䍐于云甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364034_comment'></div>迎箫吹于凤驿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364034_comment'></div>伫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>灵匹</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/32/Comments/1")'>星期</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364034_comment'></div>眷神姿于月夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364034_comment'></div>于时玉绳湛色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364034_comment'></div>金汉馀光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364034_comment'></div>烟凄碧树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364034_comment'></div>露湿银塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364034_comment'></div>视莲潭之变彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364034_comment'></div>睨松院之生凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364034_comment'></div>引惊蝉于宝瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364034_comment'></div>宿懒燕于瑶筐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364034_comment'></div>绿台兮千仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364034_comment'></div>赩楼兮百常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364034_comment'></div>拂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>花筵</span>而惨恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364034_comment'></div>披叶序而徜徉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364034_comment'></div>结遥情于汉陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364034_comment'></div>飞永睇于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>霞庄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364034_comment'></div>想佳人兮如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364034_comment'></div>怨灵欢兮不扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364034_comment'></div>促遥悲于四运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364034_comment'></div>咏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>遗歌</span>于七襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364034_comment'></div>于是虬檐晚静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364034_comment'></div>鱼扃夜饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364034_comment'></div>忘帝子之光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364034_comment'></div>下君王之颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364034_comment'></div>握<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>犀管</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364034_comment'></div>展<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>鱼笺</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364034_comment'></div>顾执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364034_comment'></div>招仲宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364034_comment'></div>仲宣跪而称曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364034_comment'></div>臣闻九变无津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364034_comment'></div>三灵有作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364034_comment'></div>布元气于浩荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364034_comment'></div>运太虚于寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364034_comment'></div>辨河鼓于西壖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364034_comment'></div>降天孙于东堮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364034_comment'></div>循五纬而清黄道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364034_comment'></div>正<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>三衡</span>而澄紫落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364034_comment'></div>海人支石之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364034_comment'></div>江女<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>穿针</span>之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364034_comment'></div>鄙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>尘情</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/71/Comments/1")'>春念</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364034_comment'></div>拟仙契于秋诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364034_comment'></div>于是光清<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>地岊</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364034_comment'></div>气敛天标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364034_comment'></div>霜凝碧宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364034_comment'></div>水莹丹霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364034_comment'></div>跃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>麟轩</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/77/Comments/1")'>雾术</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364034_comment'></div>褰羽旆于星桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364034_comment'></div>徵赤螭而架渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364034_comment'></div>漾青翰而乘湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364034_comment'></div>停翠梭兮卷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>霜縠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364034_comment'></div>引<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>鸳杼</span>兮割<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/82/Comments/1")'>冰绡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364034_comment'></div>举黄花而乘月艳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364034_comment'></div>笼黛叶而卷云娇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364034_comment'></div>抚今情而恨促。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364034_comment'></div>指来绪而伤遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364034_comment'></div>既而丹轩万栱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364034_comment'></div>紫房千籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364034_comment'></div>仙御逶迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364034_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_90_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>灵徒</span>扰弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364034_comment'></div>风惊雨骤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364034_comment'></div>烟回电烁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364034_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>娲皇</span>召巨野之龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364034_comment'></div>庄叟命雕陵之鹊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364034_comment'></div>驻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_95_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>麟驾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364034_comment'></div>披<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_96_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>鸾幕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364034_comment'></div>奏云和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364034_comment'></div>汛霞酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364034_comment'></div>碧虬玉室之馔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364034_comment'></div>白兔银台之药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364034_comment'></div>荷叶赪鲛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364034_comment'></div>芙蓉青雀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364034_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>上元</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/103/Comments/1")'>锦书</span>传<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/103/Comments/2")'>宝字</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364034_comment'></div>王母琼箱荐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_104_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/104/Comments/0")'>金约</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364034_comment'></div>䌽襻鱼头比目缝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364034_comment'></div>香针燕尾同心缚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364034_comment'></div>罗帐五花悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364034_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_108_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>珉砌</span>百枝然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364034_comment'></div>下芸帱而匿枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364034_comment'></div>弛兰服而交筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364034_comment'></div>托新欢而密勿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364034_comment'></div>怀往眷而潺湲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364034_comment'></div>于是羁鸾切镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364034_comment'></div>旅鹤惊弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364034_comment'></div>悲侵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_115_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>玉履</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364034_comment'></div>念起金钿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364034_comment'></div>俨归装而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_117_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/117/Comments/0")'>容曳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364034_comment'></div>整还盖而迁延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364034_comment'></div>洞庭波兮秋水急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364034_comment'></div>关山晦兮夕雾连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364034_comment'></div>谓河汉之无浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364034_comment'></div>似参商之永年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364034_comment'></div>君王乃背彤砌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364034_comment'></div>陟元室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364034_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_125_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>冲想</span>自闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364034_comment'></div>神情如逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364034_comment'></div>痛灵之稀偶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364034_comment'></div>嘉沈思之可毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364034_comment'></div>荆艳齐升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364034_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_130_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>燕佳</span>并出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364034_comment'></div>金声玉韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364034_comment'></div>蕙心兰质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364034_comment'></div>珠栊绮槛北风台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364034_comment'></div>绣户雕窗南向开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364034_comment'></div>响曳红云歌面近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364034_comment'></div>香随白雪舞腰来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364034_comment'></div>掩清琴而独进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364034_comment'></div>凌绛树而轻回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364034_comment'></div>卢女黄金之碗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364034_comment'></div>张家碧玉之杯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364034_comment'></div>奉君王于终夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364034_comment'></div>夫何怨于良媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364034_comment'></div>俄而月还西汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364034_comment'></div>霞临东沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364034_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_145_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/145/Comments/0")'>凫氏</span>鸣秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364034_comment'></div>鸡人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/146/Comments/0")'>唱晓</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364034_comment'></div>玉关控鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364034_comment'></div>琼林飞鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364034_comment'></div>君王乃驭风殿而长怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364034_comment'></div>俯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_150_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/150/Comments/0")'>云台</span>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_150_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/150/Comments/1")'>自矫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364034_comment'></div>矜雅范而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_151_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/151/Comments/0")'>霜厉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364034_comment'></div>穆冲衿而烟渺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364034_comment'></div>迎十客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364034_comment'></div>召三英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364034_comment'></div>香涵蔗酎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364034_comment'></div>吹肃兰旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364034_comment'></div>娃馆疏兮绿草积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364034_comment'></div>欢房寂兮紫苔生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364034_comment'></div>耸词峰于月殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364034_comment'></div>披<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_160_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/160/Comments/0")'>翰薮</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_160_1364034", 1364034, "Clauses/160/Comments/1")'>云扃</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364034_comment'></div>方绝元凯而高视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364034_comment'></div>应与梁楚而骈声。</div><div id='poem_sentence_162_1364034_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9a6ce252b9db4dcaa882786622be5de0_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年9-10月</a>　九、十月间,为归仁县主撰写墓志.归仁县主为齐王李元吉女,嫁于天水人姜谟之第二子.生子姜瑴。作品：《归仁县主墓志并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版第646页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年12月</a>　十二月,上《拜南郊颂表》作品：《上拜南郊颂表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷4第117页。）</span><div id='poem_sentence_1_1364045_comment'></div>将觐南岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364045_comment'></div>甫资元勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364045_comment'></div>旋窥大典。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1364045_comment'></div>用天老之前机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364045_comment'></div>戮防风之后至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364045_comment'></div>为而不恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364045_comment'></div>悬宝位于中宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364045_comment'></div>卑以自居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364045_comment'></div>托<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364045", 1364045, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>灵符</span>于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364045_comment'></div>礼凝苍璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364045_comment'></div>瑞溢元圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364045_comment'></div>紫旻降祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364045_comment'></div>睹郊禋之盛节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364045_comment'></div>时非苟遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364045_comment'></div>怀雅颂而知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364045_comment'></div>道不虚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364045_comment'></div>想讴歌而有志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364045_comment'></div>岂与夫周传考室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364045_comment'></div>裁称栋宇之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364045_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年12月</a>　十二月,上《拜南郊颂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷12第323页。）</span><div id='poem_1364043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拜南郊颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（668年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364043")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1364043_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364043'>微臣上稽龙繇。下阅龟谋。观天地之至道。考皇上之大节。武宣七德。未尝踰息乱之乡。文招大功。未尝出升平之域。并能悬日月而高视。驾雷雨而先鸣。或皮币而践大阶。或干戈而蹑乾步。至于理定创礼。功成作乐。振长策以叙诸侯。设灵机而制群动。犹虞阶已泰。不能息洞庭之诛。夏载克宁。不能罢会稽之戮。故将体刚柔而立本。法震曜而崇威。一戎而宇县平。四罪而华夷服。然后皇旗大辂。诏殊号于圜邱。电转星回。奏元符于孝理。天下黎人。知四海之安乐。寰中殊域。奉三灵之康泰。德兼祥风洒。道与和气游。不言而大宝用贞。无事而元功有立。舍彼代也。其谁与哉。若夫应运而生。继天而作。鼓动千载之下。超腾百王之上。遂能发轩庭之景曜。蹑隋运之颓风。揖让而取文明。指麾而清函夏。则我皇唐得之矣。高祖以黄旗锡瑞。静云火之横氛。太宗以赤羽登期。补星辰之绝缕。授瑶图于新邑。付璿历于钧台。人更三圣。道昭千古。于是俛临睿极。趋四荒于凤阙之前。端委庙堂。调万国于龙轩之下。八鸾徐动。顿汤文于后尘。九骏长驱。伫尧舜于中路。邦家之具得矣。易简之业存矣。犹有朱蒙戾俗。违光蓬艾之间。青徼遗氓。假气陶钧之内。背熊山而搆虐。拥狼潭而稽诛。窃瀛海之风波。弄乾坤之纲纪。汉图西返。惟收五都之名。魏律东穷。未出三韩之险。奸谋蓄于有渐。逆节成于不悔。长蚊蚋之雷霆。附豺狼之羽翼。岂知夫至人无外。抚天下以为家。真数有归。吊群方而罪已。三门遁甲。黄公成不战之师。五垒神兵。元女下先登之策。肃牙璋而按律。耀旄节而分麾。降南宫之元老。裂西营之毅卒。良将首路。偏戎竟野。轴轳万里。旌旗四合。金箱玉匮。司空凭百胜之威。鹗视龙趋。将军仗万全之略。负鳌邱而峻壁。据鼋壑而深沟。一鼓而亭塞无尘。七纵而江山失险。伐罪以明。而不以众。怀远人于绝境。均惠化于殊邻。登若木以照临。折红桃以延伫。然后分州列镇。对明月以收营。返旆旋戈。部元云而振旅。望神都而献捷。仰灵社以书功。辛亥谒于昭陵。癸丑告于太庙。时乘黑帝。月旅元枵。大唐有国之五十一年。皇帝有天下之一十九载也。元恶既殄。万宇清矣。元勋既辑。万宝成矣。以为周郊上帝。裁延肃慎之宾。汉礼甘泉。未拯朝鲜之乱。想元功而反侧。奉先旨以迟回。思答上灵之心。以洽庶黎之望。爰考吉日。遂净行宫。有司具典。乘舆乃出。抚元虬。戴翠凤。鼍鼓按节。鲸钟疏响。千乘岳动。万骑林回。星陈而天行。雷震而雾合。是时未登夫泰坛也。乃斋帷宫。宿帐殿。华盖移影。钩陈从跸。千营夕布。亘苍野而烟凝。万幕宵悬。背黄闉而雾列。既而屏翳清晓。飞廉警旦。孙叔奉辔。王良纵策。云藏星谧。宇旷山明。旌轩具照。箫笳互凝。陟名岳以告成。历神邱而展事。国容象物而动。朝章视令而肃。宸仪有晬。虚徐大帝之庭。列侍无哗。髣髴华胥之国。于是袭衮服。戒俎豆。端瑞班。俨华旒。乐悬六代。礼备三古。奠惟苍壁。藉用白茅。鸣孤竹之箫管。奏空桑之琴瑟。感格以诚不以事。动植咸驩。敬神以道不以华。天人合应。然后驻声名于上邑。反文物于仙宫。因雷雨而作施。法云天而用飨。风行电举。未寸景而浃九埏。野抃途歌。不崇朝而晏六合。我之元极建矣。我之能事异矣。超帝寰而振足。越皇衢以骧首。不其休乎。虽睿化无方。比神图而绝唱。而小臣不佞。抚洪笔而当仁。敢作颂曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364043'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364043'>辽河巨浸，碣石危峰。<div
