ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年</a>　名作《送杜少府之任蜀川》约作于本年。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第84页。此诗蒋注本作《送杜少府之任蜀州》）</span><div id='poem_8822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜少府之任蜀州<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作川）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（668年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8822")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8822'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8822'>城阙辅<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8822", 8822, "Clauses/0/Comments/1")'>三<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作俯西）</span>秦</span>，风烟望<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8822", 8822, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>五津</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8822'>与君离别意，同<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作俱）</span>是宦游人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8822'>海内存<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8822", 8822, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>知己</span>，天涯若比邻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8822'>无为在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8822", 8822, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>岐路</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8822", 8822, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>儿女</span>共沾巾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8822'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_8822'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(8822)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年3月</a>　春,因王室权力争夺而被斥出沛王府。作品：《檄英王鸡》<span class='inlineComment2'>（褚人获《坚瓠集补集》广陵书社1984年版卷5第473页。英王又作周王,名李显,后更名李哲。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年4月</a>　四月,王勃因檄文被斥出沛王府,友人杨炯及沈氏曾前来慰问。作品：《夏日诸公见寻访诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷7第225页。）</span><div id='poem_1364087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏日诸公见寻访诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364087")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364087'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364087'>天地不仁。造化无力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364087_comment'></div>授仆以幽忧孤愤之性。禀仆以耿介不平之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364087_comment'></div>顿忘山岳。坎坷于唐尧之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364087_comment'></div>傲想烟霞。憔悴于圣明之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364087_comment'></div>情可知矣。赖乎神交胜友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364087_comment'></div>得山泽之虬龙。隐路幽居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364087_comment'></div>降云霄之鸾凤。杨公沈公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364087_comment'></div>行之者仁义礼智。用之也乾元亨利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364087_comment'></div>元经苦而白凤翔。素牒开而紫鳞降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364087_comment'></div>金门待诏。谒天子于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364087_comment'></div>石室寻真。访下走于丘壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364087_comment'></div>幽人待士。非无北壁之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364087_comment'></div>隐士迎宾。自有西山之馔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364087_comment'></div>席门蓬巷。伫高士之来游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364087_comment'></div>丛桂幽兰。喜王孙之相对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364087_comment'></div>山南花圃。涧北松林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364087_comment'></div>黄雀至而清风生。白鹤飞而苍云起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364087_comment'></div>停琴绿水。仲长统之欢娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364087_comment'></div>置酒青山。郭子期之宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364087_comment'></div>人探一字。四韵成篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364087_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1364087_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='fb2be3c734694fd19bd410783ce31399_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fb2be3c734694fd19bd410783ce31399");'><span id='fb2be3c734694fd19bd410783ce31399_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=672')">671-672年</a>，22-23岁</div><div id='fb2be3c734694fd19bd410783ce31399' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　晚秋,抵长安.十月,朝廷诏求明礼乐之士.冬,参选.有《上绛州上官司马书》、《上明员外启》等。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷5第164页。）</span>《上明员外启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷4第133页。）</span><div id='poem_1364050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上绛州上官司马书</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364050")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364050'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364050'>月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364050_comment'></div>龙门百姓某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364050_comment'></div>谨再拜奉书于司马上官公足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364050_comment'></div>盖闻灵化出于窈冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364050_comment'></div>帝图寄于寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364050_comment'></div>圣人生而万物睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364050_comment'></div>太阶平而四国会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364050_comment'></div>故曰有非常之后者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364050_comment'></div>必有非常之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364050_comment'></div>有非常之臣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364050_comment'></div>必有非常之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364050_comment'></div>至今雷奔雨啸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364050_comment'></div>风旋电转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364050_comment'></div>拾青紫于俯仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364050_comment'></div>取公卿于朝夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364050_comment'></div>云台迫汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364050_comment'></div>南宫列元宰之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364050_comment'></div>霜戟罗门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364050_comment'></div>北阙据名臣之第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364050_comment'></div>尝见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364050_comment'></div>至若时非我与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364050_comment'></div>雄略顿于穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364050_comment'></div>道不吾行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364050_comment'></div>高材屈于卑势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364050_comment'></div>孔宣父之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>英达</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364050_comment'></div>位未列于陪臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364050_comment'></div>管公明之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>杰秀</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364050_comment'></div>名仅终于郡属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364050_comment'></div>有时无主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364050_comment'></div>贾生献流涕之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364050_comment'></div>有志无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364050_comment'></div>孟子养浩然之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364050_comment'></div>则亦有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364050_comment'></div>岂非妙造无端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364050_comment'></div>盛衰止乎其域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364050_comment'></div>神期有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364050_comment'></div>动静牵乎所遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364050_comment'></div>向使太公失于周伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364050_comment'></div>则旗亭之屠父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364050_comment'></div>韩信屈于萧何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364050_comment'></div>则辕门之饿隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364050_comment'></div>又焉得鹰扬豹变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364050_comment'></div>吐纳风云者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364050_comment'></div>故曰知与不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364050_comment'></div>用与不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364050_comment'></div>观夫得失之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364050_comment'></div>亦穷达之有数乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364050_comment'></div>其有邀时誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364050_comment'></div>忘廉耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364050_comment'></div>徇苟得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364050_comment'></div>设向背于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364050_comment'></div>立纵横于势利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364050_comment'></div>举三寸之舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364050_comment'></div>屈辱豪门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364050_comment'></div>奉咫尺之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364050_comment'></div>逡巡下席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364050_comment'></div>皆自谓材足以动俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364050_comment'></div>智足以济时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364050_comment'></div>钟鼎辉其顾盼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364050_comment'></div>冠盖生其藉甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364050_comment'></div>岂知夫四海君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364050_comment'></div>攘袂而耻之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364050_comment'></div>五尺微童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364050_comment'></div>所以固穷而不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364050_comment'></div>此盖庄周有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364050_comment'></div>所以得意而忘象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364050_comment'></div>得象而忘言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364050_comment'></div>语曰谈何容易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364050_comment'></div>易称书不尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364050_comment'></div>知谈之不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364050_comment'></div>而欲言之尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364050_comment'></div>以是思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364050_comment'></div>良可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364050_comment'></div>下官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364050_comment'></div>康衢之贱耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364050_comment'></div>尝闻阙里之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364050_comment'></div>颇挂平舆之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364050_comment'></div>岂不知尘形俗状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364050_comment'></div>游水镜而多惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364050_comment'></div>抱鼓援鼙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364050_comment'></div>过雷门而自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364050_comment'></div>而欲刻鹄饰凫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364050_comment'></div>唐突扃钥者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364050_comment'></div>徒以登山泛海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364050_comment'></div>庶测高深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364050_comment'></div>执炬传萤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364050_comment'></div>希增日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364050_comment'></div>三奔九合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364050_comment'></div>下官闻管仲之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364050_comment'></div>千载一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364050_comment'></div>君侯受鲍卿之托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364050_comment'></div>是以敢陈其径庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364050_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364050_comment'></div>则秋风明月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364050_comment'></div>西江留独往之因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364050_comment'></div>桂峤松岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364050_comment'></div>南山有不群之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364050_comment'></div>矧区区者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364050_comment'></div>而重高明之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>阃阈</span>哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364050_comment'></div>君侯极天分构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364050_comment'></div>振琼树而韬霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364050_comment'></div>带地疏源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364050_comment'></div>握珠胎而冠月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364050_comment'></div>鳞轩羽殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364050_comment'></div>瑶台降卿相之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364050_comment'></div>鹊印蝉簪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364050_comment'></div>金社发公侯之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364050_comment'></div>青皋独唳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364050_comment'></div>望鸿渐而翻霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364050_comment'></div>丹穴高鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364050_comment'></div>对<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/110/Comments/0")'>鹓池</span>而矫雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364050_comment'></div>严助以贤良待诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364050_comment'></div>未厌承明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364050_comment'></div>汲黯以方正拾遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364050_comment'></div>终荣卧理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364050_comment'></div>藩维克振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364050_comment'></div>既参<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_116_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/116/Comments/0")'>来暮</span>之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364050_comment'></div>邦国不空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364050_comment'></div>自有康沂之相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364050_comment'></div>加以雄材广度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364050_comment'></div>散琬玉于胸怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364050_comment'></div>逸气<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_121_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>遒文</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364050_comment'></div>运风霜于掌握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364050_comment'></div>迫青霄而构舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364050_comment'></div>烟霞之涯涘莫寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364050_comment'></div>振沧渤以流谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364050_comment'></div>江汉之波澜未测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364050_comment'></div>耀灵圭于赵席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364050_comment'></div>垂棘知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364050_comment'></div>辩群籁于庄轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364050_comment'></div>悬匏自托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364050_comment'></div>宾阶夕敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364050_comment'></div>清河销骥絷之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364050_comment'></div>虚榻晨披。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364050_comment'></div>元礼得龙驱之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364050_comment'></div>方当翊赞宸极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364050_comment'></div>羽仪台屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364050_comment'></div>岂徒偃仰州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364050_comment'></div>劳事藩庭而已哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364050_comment'></div>借如仆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364050_comment'></div>言不满于乡党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364050_comment'></div>声不出于堂阈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364050_comment'></div>东海取乐于箪瓢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364050_comment'></div>南山异志于文史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364050_comment'></div>餐花佩叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364050_comment'></div>入兰室而谈元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364050_comment'></div>挹露攀霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364050_comment'></div>坐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_147_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>松扃</span>而啸逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364050_comment'></div>扬子云之澹泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364050_comment'></div>心窃慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364050_comment'></div>嵇叔夜之逍遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364050_comment'></div>真其好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364050_comment'></div>未尝露才扬已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364050_comment'></div>饰小智以惊愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364050_comment'></div>假势凭时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364050_comment'></div>托中人而树迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364050_comment'></div>遍游天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364050_comment'></div>寒心于将相之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364050_comment'></div>独守太元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364050_comment'></div>侧身于名利之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364050_comment'></div>尝谓奉琴卮于北牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364050_comment'></div>咏诗礼于南陔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364050_comment'></div>坐商洛而折云英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364050_comment'></div>临江湖而采烟液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364050_comment'></div>生愿毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364050_comment'></div>而属<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_165_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/165/Comments/0")'>鸾扃</span>停逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364050_comment'></div>频虚不次之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364050_comment'></div>鹤板徵贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364050_comment'></div>累发非常之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364050_comment'></div>天下有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364050_comment'></div>吾岂匏瓜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364050_comment'></div>承达人一顾之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364050_comment'></div>辱公车再辟之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364050_comment'></div>平津侯之博物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364050_comment'></div>终屈奉常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364050_comment'></div>贾大夫之才名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364050_comment'></div>犹逢绛灌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364050_comment'></div>况庸者而可免于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364050_comment'></div>君侯要津先据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364050_comment'></div>图海盛于当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364050_comment'></div>下官覆篑方勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364050_comment'></div>为山始于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364050_comment'></div>虽陵深谷变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364050_comment'></div>终非入室之宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364050_comment'></div>而昼咏宵吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364050_comment'></div>敢预升堂之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364050_comment'></div>夫以幽明不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364050_comment'></div>尺标见天下之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364050_comment'></div>巨细相倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364050_comment'></div>寸管合羲舒之度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364050_comment'></div>岂非道存斯贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364050_comment'></div>理在必亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364050_comment'></div>霸略近发于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_192_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/192/Comments/0")'>舆歌</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364050_comment'></div>皇图不隔于刍议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364050_comment'></div>故有荣枯绝等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364050_comment'></div>奉推毂而欣然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364050_comment'></div>年势不侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364050_comment'></div>受分庭而罔愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364050_comment'></div>风规可接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364050_comment'></div>惟君侯体之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364050_comment'></div>今古未殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364050_comment'></div>则下官愿矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364050_comment'></div>常恨霜松列涧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364050_comment'></div>万寻无罩月之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364050_comment'></div>露草滋山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364050_comment'></div>寸茎有梢云之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364050_comment'></div>斯则声实困于兼济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364050_comment'></div>才位难于俱立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364050_comment'></div>况乎地势不足以誇俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364050_comment'></div>容貌不足以动人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364050_comment'></div>遑遑薮泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364050_comment'></div>安足以奉高明之咳唾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364050_comment'></div>所冀蝇阶贱质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364050_comment'></div>附云足而追飙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364050_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_214_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/214/Comments/0")'>蚋序</span>轻姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364050_comment'></div>托霜毛而绝海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364050_comment'></div>委名励已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364050_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_217_1364050", 1364050, "Clauses/217/Comments/0")'>蛟镡</span>申独断之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364050_comment'></div>偶迹当仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364050_comment'></div>骊珠鲜闇投之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364050_comment'></div>天衢可望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364050_comment'></div>指鹏程而三休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364050_comment'></div>巨壑难游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364050_comment'></div>伏龙门而一息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364050_comment'></div>勃死罪死罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_224_1364050_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上明员外启</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364061")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364061'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364061'>某启。侧闻金乌耸辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364061_comment'></div>俯圆燧而抽光。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>瑶兔</span>浮轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364061_comment'></div>候方诸而吐液。斯则洪纤异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364061_comment'></div>冥符造化之津。高下相悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364061_comment'></div>精契陶钧之表。故知声同义合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364061_comment'></div>存长幼于三州。理隔气殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364061_comment'></div>置山川于一面。神交可托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364061_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>风云</span>于杵臼之间。道不虚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364061_comment'></div>泾渭于簪裾之列。其有迹申知已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364061_comment'></div>投爵里于思齐。事迫当仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364061_comment'></div>抱龙泉而愿割。虽荆山已峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364061_comment'></div>多轻抵鹊之珍。而渤澥方春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364061_comment'></div>敢进归凫之影。伏惟丈人珠躔降德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364061_comment'></div>铣社抽英。河岳纵其神器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364061_comment'></div>烟霞发其符采。江东第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364061_comment'></div>家传正始之音。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>日下无双</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364061_comment'></div>誉重名流之首。三冬文史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364061_comment'></div>先兆迹于青衿。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>百里</span>弦歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364061_comment'></div>即驰芳于墨绶。彭泽陶潜之菊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364061_comment'></div>胜气仍存。河阳潘岳之花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364061_comment'></div>芳风遂远。荣加徙秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364061_comment'></div>上膺兰府之游。宠夺攀轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364061_comment'></div>更掌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>蓬山</span>之务。麟图缉谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364061_comment'></div>定荣辱于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>三泉</span>。鹓閤裁书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364061_comment'></div>考薰莸于四部。既鹤鸣云路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364061_comment'></div>望偃朝端。鸿渐星台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364061_comment'></div>俯谐佥议。廉平誉号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364061_comment'></div>李宣伯之当官。雅操绳时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364061_comment'></div>山巨源之称职。加以文场武库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364061_comment'></div>发挥廊庙之师。琼树瑶林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364061_comment'></div>寥廓风尘之表。一邱一壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364061_comment'></div>同阮籍于西山。一啸一歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364061_comment'></div>列嵇康于北面。词条郁雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364061_comment'></div>遥腾驾日之阴。辨锷横霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364061_comment'></div>直上<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>冲星</span>之气。凫钟蓄韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364061_comment'></div>闻片言而指掌。鸾镜悬心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364061_comment'></div>见一善而明目。情源九派。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364061_comment'></div>士流欣满腹之期。德宇千门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364061_comment'></div>词人有庇身之望。方当坐谈帝席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364061_comment'></div>雄视群公。岂徒比迹天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364061_comment'></div>雌伏郎官而已哉。某崇徽启绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364061_comment'></div>盛德传家。承太子之仙宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364061_comment'></div>析将军之远系。朱轮在汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364061_comment'></div>列高士于三台。青盖浮江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364061_comment'></div>扈平王于七姓。遗风旧烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364061_comment'></div>尚存清白之基。祖德家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364061_comment'></div>代有纵横之目。及金陵东覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364061_comment'></div>玉马西奔。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>髦头</span>杰起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364061_comment'></div>文儒继出。凤鸣朝日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364061_comment'></div>森梢烟雨之标。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>龙跃</span>云津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364061_comment'></div>盘礡江山之气。虽雄名雅誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364061_comment'></div>随朔野而扬声。而华冕雕轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364061_comment'></div>比南风而不竞。陈太邱之积善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364061_comment'></div>羔雁成群。谢车骑之馀芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364061_comment'></div>兰荪不替。趋庭洽训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364061_comment'></div>共歌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1364061", 1364061, "Clauses/110/Comments/0")'>朱萼</span>之篇。避席成欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364061_comment'></div>犹守青箱之业。尝谓酣神北阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364061_comment'></div>藉春渚而忘归。动影南棂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364061_comment'></div>坐秋山而长往。不意兰皋独啸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364061_comment'></div>轻交委鹤之书。芝涧行谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364061_comment'></div>坐辱飞龙之使。年殊贾谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364061_comment'></div>仰宣室而方同。业谢刘繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364061_comment'></div>俯长途而遂恧。塞上浮云之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364061_comment'></div>空倦吴山。隋侯明月之珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364061_comment'></div>终悲暗室。岂不知拂衣长谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364061_comment'></div>林泉多倦俗之因。安枕有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364061_comment'></div>庙堂非养高之所。松楹坐月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364061_comment'></div>临黛壑而遐征。桂席攀风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364061_comment'></div>俯青岩而自足。而欲俯首屈膝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364061_comment'></div>逡巡多士之林。吊影惭魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364061_comment'></div>肮脏文昌之府。徒以牛蹄已倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364061_comment'></div>临大壑而骧鳞。羊角可逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364061_comment'></div>想高衢而抚翼。参名国士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364061_comment'></div>方叨智伯之恩。挥迹奉常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364061_comment'></div>冀雪公孙之耻。识正平于处士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364061_comment'></div>虽在孔融。期仲容于望外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364061_comment'></div>终资许允。犹恐先驰折翮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364061_comment'></div>频惊鹢路之风。再举枯鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364061_comment'></div>空击龙门之水。丈人借以颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364061_comment'></div>资以恩波。垂雅契于长年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364061_comment'></div>叙情交于累代。情加倒屣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364061_comment'></div>知顷步之生光。礼极升堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364061_comment'></div>觉声名之有地。是用俯抽丹思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364061_comment'></div>上渎清颜。镂殊奖于肝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364061_comment'></div>衔德音于咳唾。懦夫增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364061_comment'></div>先歌易水之风。壮士投心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364061_comment'></div>思赴吴门之火。恩崇命浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364061_comment'></div>瞻吕梁而可从。山高海深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364061_comment'></div>陟孟门而何险。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364061_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_89_1364061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　在选曹.李敬玄为之延誉,裴行俭则颇有贬损,勃于是作《上吏部裴侍郎启》以明志显才。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷4第128页。）</span><div class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364060")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364060'>某启。猥承衡镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364060_comment'></div>骤照阶墀。本惭刀笔之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364060_comment'></div>虚荷雕虫之眷。殊恩屡及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364060_comment'></div>严命频加。责光耀于昏冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364060_comment'></div>课宫商于寂寞。进退惟谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364060_comment'></div>忧喜聚门。诚恐下官冒轻进之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364060_comment'></div>使君侯招过听之议。贵贱交失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364060_comment'></div>恩爱两亏。所以战惧盈旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364060_comment'></div>迟回改朔。怀郑璞而增愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364060_comment'></div>捧燕珉而自耻。某性惟懵昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364060_comment'></div>识谢沈冥。蒙父兄训导之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364060_comment'></div>藉朋友琢磨之义。好学近乎智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364060_comment'></div>力行近乎仁。知忠孝为九德之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364060_comment'></div>故造次必于是。审名利为五常之贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364060_comment'></div>故颠沛而思远。虽未之逮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364060_comment'></div>亦有其志焉。孔子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364060_comment'></div>言及之而不言谓之隐。今者接君侯者三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364060_comment'></div>承招延者再矣。抑亦可以言乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364060_comment'></div>夫文章之道。自古称难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364060_comment'></div>圣人以开物成务。君子以立言见志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364060_comment'></div>遗雅背训。孟子不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364060_comment'></div>劝百讽一。扬雄所耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364060_comment'></div>苟非可以甄明大义。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364060", 1364060, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>矫正</span>末流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364060_comment'></div>俗化资以兴衰。国家由其轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364060_comment'></div>古人未尝留心也。自微言既绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364060_comment'></div>斯文不振。屈宋导浇源于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364060_comment'></div>枚马张淫风于后。谈人主者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364060_comment'></div>以宫室苑囿为雄。叙名流者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364060_comment'></div>以沈酗骄奢为达。故魏文用之而中国衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364060_comment'></div>宋武贵之而江东乱。虽沈谢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364060", 1364060, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>争骛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364060_comment'></div>适足兆齐梁之危。徐庾并驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364060_comment'></div>不能止周陈之祸。于是识其道者卷舌而不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364060_comment'></div>明其弊者拂衣而径逝。潜夫昌言之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364060_comment'></div>作之而有逆于时。周公孔氏之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364060_comment'></div>存之而不行于代。天下之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364060_comment'></div>靡不坏矣。国家应千载之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364060_comment'></div>恢百王之业。天地静默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364060_comment'></div>阴阳顺序。方欲激扬正道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364060_comment'></div>大庇生人。黜非圣之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364060_comment'></div>除不稽之论。牧童顿颡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364060_comment'></div>思进皇谋。樵夫拭目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364060_comment'></div>愿谈王道。崇大厦者非一木之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364060_comment'></div>匡弊俗者非一日之卫。众持则力尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364060_comment'></div>真长则伪销。自然之数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364060_comment'></div>君侯受朝廷之寄。掌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364060", 1364060, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>镕范</span>之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364060_comment'></div>至于舞咏浇淳。好尚邪正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364060_comment'></div>宜深以为念者也。伏见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1364060", 1364060, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>铨擢</span>之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364060_comment'></div>每以诗赋为先。诚恐君侯器人于翰墨之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364060_comment'></div>求材于简牍之际。果未足以采取英秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364060_comment'></div>斟酌高贤者也。徒使骏骨长朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364060_comment'></div>真龙不降。衒才饰智者奔驰于末流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364060_comment'></div>怀真蕴璞者栖遑于下列。易不云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364060_comment'></div>言行君子之所以动天地。失之毫釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364060_comment'></div>差以千里。书不云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364060_comment'></div>敝化奢丽。万世同流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364060_comment'></div>馀风未殄。公其念哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364060_comment'></div>嗟乎。盖有识天人之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364060", 1364060, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>幽致</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364060_comment'></div>明国家之大体。辨焉而不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364060_comment'></div>酌焉而不竭。抱膝无闷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364060_comment'></div>盱衡自得。彼悠悠小技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364060_comment'></div>焉足为君侯道矣。自非奉閒宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364060_comment'></div>接清谈。未可一二言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364060_comment'></div>然窃不自揆。尝著文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364060_comment'></div>非敢自媒。聊以恭命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364060_comment'></div>谨录古君臣赞十篇并序。虽不足尘高识之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364060_comment'></div>亦可以见小人之志也。伏愿暂停左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364060_comment'></div>少察胸襟。观述作之所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364060_comment'></div>知用心之有地。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364060_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1364060_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　经裴行俭、李敬玄及虢州司法陆季友举荐,参选后补授虢州参军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>　春,赴友人曲水之宴,作《三月曲水宴得烟字》诗,盖与卢照邻唱和之作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第93页。）</span><div id='poem_8839' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8839")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_8839_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_8839'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(457, "poem_allusion_8839")'>傅岩</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(867, "poem_allusion_8839")'>磻溪入钓</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_8839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8839'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8839'>彭泽官初去，河阳赋始传。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8839'>田园归旧国，诗酒间长筵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8839'>列室窥丹洞，分楼瞰紫烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8839'>萦回亘津渡，出没控<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8839", 8839, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>郊廛</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8839'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_8839", 8839, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>凤琴</span>调上客，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_8839", 8839, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>龙辔</span>俨群仙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_8839'>松石偏宜古，藤萝不记年。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8839'>重檐交密树，复磴拥危泉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_8839'>抗石晞南岭，乘沙眇北川。<div id='poem_sentence_7_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_8839'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(457, "poem_sentence_8_8839")'>傅岩</span>来筑处，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(867, "poem_sentence_8_8839")'>磻溪入钓</span>前。<div id='poem_sentence_8_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_8839'>日斜真趣远，幽思梦凉蝉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_8839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_8839'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_8839_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>　春,送弟劼赴太学,有《送劼赴太学序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷8第251页。）</span><div id='poem_1364074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送劼赴太学序</a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364074")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364074'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364074'>今之游太学者多矣。咸一切欲速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364074_comment'></div>百端进取。故夫肤受末学者因利乘便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364074_comment'></div>经明行修者华存实爽。至于振骨鲠之风标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364074_comment'></div>服贤圣之言。怀远大之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364074_comment'></div>盖有之矣。未之见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364074_comment'></div>可以深慕哉。且吾家以儒辅仁述作存者八代矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364074_comment'></div>未有不久于其道而求苟出者也。故能立经陈训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364074_comment'></div>删书定礼。扬魁梧之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364074_comment'></div>树清白之业。使吾徒子孙有所取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364074_comment'></div>大雅不云无念尔祖。易不云干父之蛊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364074_comment'></div>书不云惟孝友于。诗不云不如友生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364074_comment'></div>四者备矣。加之执德宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364074_comment'></div>信道笃。心则口诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364074_comment'></div>废食忘寝。涣然有所成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364074_comment'></div>望然有所伏。然后可以托教义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364074_comment'></div>编人伦。彰风声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364074_comment'></div>议出处。若意不感慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364074_comment'></div>行不卓绝。轻进苟动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364074_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364074", 1364074, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>见利忘义</span>。虽上一阶履半级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364074_comment'></div>何足恃哉。终见弃于高人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364074_comment'></div>但自溺于下流矣。吾被服家业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364074_comment'></div>沾濡庭训。切磋琢磨战兢惕厉者二十馀载矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364074_comment'></div>幸以薄伎。获蠲戎役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364074_comment'></div>尝耻道未成而受禄。恨不得如古君子四十强而仕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364074_comment'></div>而房族多孤。饘粥不继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364074_comment'></div>逼父兄之命。睹饥寒之切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364074_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364074", 1364074, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>解巾</span>捧檄。扶老携幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364074_comment'></div>今既至于斯矣。不蚕而衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364074_comment'></div>不耕而食。吾何德以当哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364074_comment'></div>至于竭小人之心。申犹子之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364074_comment'></div>饮食衣服。晨昏左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364074_comment'></div>庶几乎令汝无反顾忧也。行矣自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364074_comment'></div>游必有方。离别咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364074_comment'></div>未足耿耿。嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364074_comment'></div>不有居者。谁展色养之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364074_comment'></div>不有行者。孰就扬名之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364074_comment'></div>笾豆有践。菽水尽心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364074_comment'></div>盍各赋诗。叙离道意云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364074_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1364074_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>　春,作《倬彼我系》,陈先人之迹,议自身出处之艰难,其兄王励有序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第65页。）</span><div id='poem_8864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>倬彼我系<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8864")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8864_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_8864'>倬彼我系。舍弟虢州参军勃所作也，伤迫乎家贫，道未成而受禄，不得如古之君子四十强而仕也。故本其性情，原其事业，因陈先人之际，以议出处，只天爵之艰难也。勃兄励序。</div><div id='poem_preface_8864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8864'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8864'>倬彼我系，出自有周。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8864'>分疆锡社，派别支流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8864'>居卫仕宋，臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作匡）</span>嬴相刘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8864'>乃武乃文，或公或侯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8864'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8864_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_8865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8865?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8865'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8865'>晋历<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8865", 8865, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>崩坼</span>，衣冠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8865", 8865, -----title
绍兴（山阴）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='94b10fe8aab447a49fcaf179e3a5c959_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("94b10fe8aab447a49fcaf179e3a5c959");'><span id='94b10fe8aab447a49fcaf179e3a5c959_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>，18岁</div><div id='94b10fe8aab447a49fcaf179e3a5c959' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>　秋,在越州山阴季处士宅赴宴并作诗。作品：《秋日宴季处士宅序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷6第191页。《秋日宴季处士宅序》有云,“季处士者,远游濠上,来游镜中”,“镜中”指山阴南湖,故知勃曾至越州山阴。）</span><div id='poem_1364091' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364091' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364091?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋日宴季处士宅序</a><span class='authorDate'>（667年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364091")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364091_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364091'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364091'>若夫争名于朝廷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364091_comment'></div>则冠盖相趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364091_comment'></div>遁迹于丘园者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364091_comment'></div>则林泉见托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364091_comment'></div>虽语默非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364091_comment'></div>物我不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364091_comment'></div>而逍遥皆得性之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364091_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364091", 1364091, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>动息</span>匪自然之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364091_comment'></div>故有季处士者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364091_comment'></div>远辞濠上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364091_comment'></div>来游境中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364091_comment'></div>披白云以开筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364091_comment'></div>俯青溪而命酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364091_comment'></div>昔时西北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364091_comment'></div>则我地之琳琅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364091_comment'></div>今日东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364091_comment'></div>乃他乡之竹箭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364091_comment'></div>又此夜乘槎之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364091_comment'></div>犹对仙家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364091_comment'></div>坐菊之宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364091_comment'></div>尚临清赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364091_comment'></div>既而依稀旧识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364091_comment'></div>欢吴郑之班荆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364091_comment'></div>乐莫新交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364091_comment'></div>申孔程之倾盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364091_comment'></div>向时朱夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364091_comment'></div>俄涉素秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364091_comment'></div>金风生而景物清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364091_comment'></div>白露下而光阴晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364091_comment'></div>庭前柳叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364091_comment'></div>才听蝉鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364091_comment'></div>野外芦花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364091_comment'></div>行看鸥上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364091_comment'></div>数人之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364091_comment'></div>几度琴樽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364091_comment'></div>百年之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364091_comment'></div>少时风月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364091_comment'></div>兰亭有昔时之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364091_comment'></div>竹林无今日之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364091_comment'></div>丈夫不纵志于生平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364091_comment'></div>何屈节于名利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364091_comment'></div>人之情矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364091_comment'></div>岂曰不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364091_comment'></div>人赋一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364091_comment'></div>各申其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364091_comment'></div>使夫千载之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364091_comment'></div>四海之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364091_comment'></div>后之视今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364091_comment'></div>知我咏怀抱于兹日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1364091_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
萧山（永兴）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6da381ae126e41948b585a66058b44a2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6da381ae126e41948b585a66058b44a2");'><span id='6da381ae126e41948b585a66058b44a2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>，18岁</div><div id='6da381ae126e41948b585a66058b44a2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>　秋,在越州永兴李明府宅为萧三饯行并赋诗。作品：《越州永兴李明府宅送萧三还齐州序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷8第241页。）</span><div id='poem_1364076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>越州永兴李明府宅送萧三还齐州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（667年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364076")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364076_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364076'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364076'>嗟乎。不游天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364076_comment'></div>安知四海之交。不涉河梁者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364076_comment'></div>岂识别离之恨。薜衣松杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364076_comment'></div>琴樽为得意之亲。临远登高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364076_comment'></div>烟霞是赏心之事。有梁孝王之下客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364076_comment'></div>仆是河南之南。孟尝君之上宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364076_comment'></div>子在北山之北。幸属一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364076_comment'></div>作寰中之主。翛然四皓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364076_comment'></div>为方外之臣。俱游万物之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364076_comment'></div>相遇三江之表。许元度之清风朗月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364076_comment'></div>时慰相思。王逸少之修竹茂林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364076_comment'></div>屡陪欢宴。加以惠而好我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364076_comment'></div>携手同行。或登吴会而听越吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364076_comment'></div>或下宛委而观禹穴。良谈落落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364076_comment'></div>金石丝竹之音辉。雅致飘飘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364076_comment'></div>松柏风云之气状。当此时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364076_comment'></div>尝谓连璧无异乡之别。断金有好亲之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364076_comment'></div>生平于张范之年。齐物于惠庄之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364076_comment'></div>三光回薄。未殚投分之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364076_comment'></div>四序循环。讵尽忘言之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364076_comment'></div>岂期我留子往。乐去悲来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364076_comment'></div>横咽水而东西。绪愁云于南北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364076_comment'></div>况乎泣穷途于白首。白首非临别之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364076_comment'></div>嗟歧路于他乡。他乡岂送归之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364076_comment'></div>蓐收戒序。少昊司辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364076_comment'></div>清风起而城阙寒。白露下而江山远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364076_comment'></div>徘徊去鹤。将别盖而同飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364076_comment'></div>断续来鸿。共离舟而俱泛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364076_comment'></div>古人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364076", 1364076, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>道别</span>。动便经年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364076_comment'></div>今我言离。会当何日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364076_comment'></div>山巨源之风猷令望。善佐朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364076_comment'></div>嵇叔夜之潦倒粗疏。甘从草泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364076_comment'></div>行当山中攀桂。往往思仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364076_comment'></div>野外纫兰。时时佩德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364076_comment'></div>人非桃李。岂得无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364076_comment'></div>子是箫韶。当思振响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364076_comment'></div>勉酌伤离之酒。具陈感别之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364076_comment'></div>各赋一言。俱题六韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364076_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1364076_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京（江宁）
-----detail

showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364107?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江宁吴少府宅饯宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（675年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364107")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364107_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364107'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364107'>蒋山南望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364107_comment'></div>长江北流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364107_comment'></div>伍胥用而三吴盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364107_comment'></div>孙权困而九州裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364107_comment'></div>遗墟旧壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364107_comment'></div>数万里之皇城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364107_comment'></div>虎踞龙盘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364107_comment'></div>三百年之帝国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364107_comment'></div>关连石塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364107_comment'></div>地实金陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364107_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364107", 1364107, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>霸气</span>尽而江山空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364107_comment'></div>皇风清而市朝改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364107_comment'></div>昔时地险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364107_comment'></div>实为建业之雄都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364107_comment'></div>今日太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364107_comment'></div>即是江宁之小邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364107_comment'></div>吴生俊寀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364107_comment'></div>辅佐烹鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364107_comment'></div>我辈良游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364107_comment'></div>方驰去鹢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364107_comment'></div>梁伯鸾之远逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364107_comment'></div>自有长谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364107_comment'></div>闵仲叔之遐征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364107_comment'></div>仍逢厚礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364107_comment'></div>临别浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364107_comment'></div>枕离亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364107_comment'></div>阵云四面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364107_comment'></div>洪涛千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364107_comment'></div>帘帷后辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364107_comment'></div>竹树映而秋烟生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364107_comment'></div>栋宇前临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364107_comment'></div>波潮惊而朔风动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364107_comment'></div>嗣宗高啸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364107_comment'></div>绿轸方调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364107_comment'></div>文举清谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364107_comment'></div>芳樽自满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364107_comment'></div>想衣冠于旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364107_comment'></div>便值三秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364107_comment'></div>忆风景于新亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364107_comment'></div>俄伤万古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364107_comment'></div>情穷兴洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364107_comment'></div>乐极悲来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364107_comment'></div>怆零雨于中轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364107_comment'></div>动流波于下席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364107_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364107_comment'></div>九江为别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364107_comment'></div>帝里隔于云端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364107_comment'></div>五岭方踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364107_comment'></div>交州在于天际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364107_comment'></div>方严去舳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364107_comment'></div>且对穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364107_comment'></div>玉露下而苍山空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364107_comment'></div>他乡悲而故人别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364107_comment'></div>请开文囿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364107_comment'></div>共泻词源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364107_comment'></div>人赋一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364107_comment'></div>俱题四韵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1364107_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>道经长江,作《采莲赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷2第42页。）</span><div id='poem_1364037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>采莲赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（675年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364037")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364037_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364037'>昔之赋芙蓉者多矣。虽复曹王潘令之逸曲。孙鲍江萧之妙韵。莫不杂陈丽美。粗举采掇。岂所谓究厥艳态。穷其风谣哉。顷乘暇景。历睹众制。伏玩累日。有不满焉。遂作赋曰。非登高可以赋者。惟采莲而已矣。况洞庭兮紫波。复潇湘兮绿水。或暑雨兮朝霁。乍凉飙兮暮起。黛叶青跗。烟周五湖。红葩绛蘤。电烁千里。尤见重于幽客。信作谣于君子。尔其珍族广茂。淑类博传。藻河渭之空曲。被沮漳之沦涟。烛澄湾而烂烂。亘修涨之田田。岂直水区泽国。江漘海壖。是以吴娃越艳。郑婉秦妍。感灵翘于上节。悦瑞色于中年。锦帆映浦。罗衣塞川。飞木兰之画楫。驾芙蓉之绮船。问子何去。幽潭采莲。已矣哉。诚不知其所以然。赏由物召。兴以情迁。故其游泳一致。悲欣万绪。至若金屋丽。璇宫佚女。伤凤台之寂寞。厌鸾扃之閒处。侍饮南津。陪欢北渚。见矶岸之纡直。觌旌旄之低举。上苑神池。芳林御陂。楼阴架沚。殿彩乘漪。张燕洛之容卫。备横汾之羽仪。箫鼓发兮龙文动。鳞羽喧兮鹢首移。咸靓妆而丽服。各分骛而并驰。蘋萦桨碍。荇触船危。视云霞之沃荡。望林泉之蔽亏。洪川泱泱兮菡萏积。绿水湛湛兮芙蕖披。惜时岁兮易暮。伤君王兮未知。折绀房与缃菂。揽红葩及碧枝。回绡裙兮窃独叹。步罗袜兮私自奇。莫不惊香悼色。畏别伤离。复有泽宫年少。期门公子。翠发蛾眉。赪唇皓齿。傅粉兰堂之上。偷香椒屋之里。亦复衔恩激誓。佩宠缄愁。承好赐之珍席。奉嬉游之彩斿。绣栋曛兮翠羽帐。瑶塘曙兮青翰舟。搴条拾蕊。沿波溯流。池心宽而藻薄。浦口窄而萍稠。和桡姬之卫吹。接榜女之齐讴。去复去兮水色夕。采复采兮荷华秋。愿承欢而卒岁。长接席而寡仇。于时蓟北无事。关西始乐。雾静江垠。气恬海漠。寝怪气于沅湘。照荣光于河洛。殊方异类。舞咏相错。王公卿士。歌吹并作。则有侯家琐第。戚里芳园。穿池灞岸之曲。蓄水河阳之源。堤防谷口。岛屿轘辕。嘉木毕植。灵草具繁。沈桂北之丹藕。播荆南之紫根。郁萋萋而雾合。灿煜煜而霞翻。洎乎气彻都鄙。景华川陆。麦雨微凉。梅飙浅燠。命妖侣于石城。啸娱朋于金谷。乃使绿珠捧棹。青琴理舳。樽芳醪。藉珍餗。汎玉潭之㳽漫。绕金渠之隈隩。石近水而苔浓。岸连山而树复。排芰末而争远。托芦间而竞逐。赴汨凌波。飞袿振罗。风低绿干。水溅黄螺。上客喧兮乐未已。美人醉兮颜将。畏莲色之如脸。愿衣香兮胜荷。徘徊郢调。悽惨燕歌。念穷欢于水涘。誓毕赏于川阿。结汉女。邀湘娥。北溪蕊尚密。南汀花更多。恨光景兮不驻。指芳馨兮谓何。若乃南鄢义妻。东吴信妇。结缡整佩。承筐奉帚。忽君子兮有行。复良人兮远征。南讨九真百越。北戌鸡田雁城。念去魂骇。相视骨惊。临春渚兮一送。见秋潭兮四平。与子之别。烟波望绝。念子之寒。江山路难。水淡淡兮莲叶紫。风飒飒兮荷华丹。剪瑶带而犹欷。折琼英而不欢。既而缘隈逗浦。返枻归橹。眷芳草兮已残。忆离居兮方苦。延素颈于极涨。攘皓腕于神浒。惜佳期兮末由。徒增思兮何补。又若倡姬荡媵。命侣招群。淇上洛表。湘皋汝坟。望洲草兮翡翠色。动浦水兮骊龙文。愿解佩以邀子。思褰裳而从君。悲时暮。愁日曛。鸣镮钏兮响窈窕。艳珠翠兮光缤纷。怜曙野之绛气。爱晴天之碧云。棹巡汀而柳拂。船向渚而菱分。掇翠茎以翳景。袭朱萼以为裙。艇楫凌乱。云流雨散。鸣榔络绎。雾罢烟释。状飞虬之蜿蜿。若惊鸿之奕奕。艇怯奔潮。篙憎浅石。丝著手而偏绕。刺牵衣而屡襞。乃有贵子王孙。乘閒纵观。何平叔之符彩。潘安仁之藻翰。税龙马于金堤。命凫舟于石岸。锦缆翻洒。银樯照烂。日侧光沈。风惊浪深。纡北渚</div><div id='poem_preface_1364037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364037'>之新赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364037_comment'></div>恣东溪之密寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364037_comment'></div>鸳鸯绣彩之文履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364037_comment'></div>玳瑁琼华之宝琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364037_comment'></div>扣舷击榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364037_comment'></div>吴歈越吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364037_comment'></div>溱与洧兮叶覆水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364037_comment'></div>淮与济兮花冒浔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364037_comment'></div>值明月之夕出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364037_comment'></div>逢丹霞之夜临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364037_comment'></div>茱萸歌兮轸妾思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364037_comment'></div>芍药曲兮伤人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364037_comment'></div>伊采莲之贱事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364037_comment'></div>信忘情之盖寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364037_comment'></div>虽迹兆于水乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364037_comment'></div>遂风行于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364037_comment'></div>感极哀乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364037_comment'></div>声参郑雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364037_comment'></div>是以缅察谷底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364037_comment'></div>穷览地维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364037_comment'></div>北尽丰镐劳潏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364037_comment'></div>南究巴沱越沂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364037_comment'></div>莫不候期应节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364037_comment'></div>沿涛汎湄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364037_comment'></div>薄言采之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364037_comment'></div>兴言服之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364037_comment'></div>发文扃之丽什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364037_comment'></div>动幽幌之情诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364037_comment'></div>使人结眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364037_comment'></div>令人相思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364037_comment'></div>宜其色震百草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364037_comment'></div>香夺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364037", 1364037, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>九芝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364037_comment'></div>栖碧羽之神雀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364037_comment'></div>负青𪚮之宝龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364037_comment'></div>紫帙流记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364037_comment'></div>丹经秘词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364037_comment'></div>岂徒加绣柱之光彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364037_comment'></div>煜文井之华滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364037_comment'></div>已焉哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364037_comment'></div>向使时无其族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364037_comment'></div>代乏厥类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364037_comment'></div>独秀上清之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364037_comment'></div>不受中国之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364037_comment'></div>学鸾舞而时来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364037_comment'></div>与鹣鲽而间至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364037_comment'></div>必能使众瑞彩没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364037_comment'></div>群贶色沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364037_comment'></div>汤武斋戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364037_comment'></div>伊皋延伫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364037_comment'></div>岂俾夫楚童赵仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364037_comment'></div>倡姬艳女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364037_comment'></div>狎而玩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364037_comment'></div>撷而采之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364037_comment'></div>时有东鄙幽人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364037_comment'></div>西园旧客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364037_comment'></div>常陪帝子之舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364037_comment'></div>经侍天人之藉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364037_comment'></div>咏绿竹于风晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364037_comment'></div>赋彤管于日夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364037_comment'></div>暑往寒来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364037_comment'></div>忽矣悠哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364037_comment'></div>蓬飘梗逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364037_comment'></div>天涯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364037", 1364037, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>海际</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364037_comment'></div>似还邛之寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364037_comment'></div>同适越之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1364037", 1364037, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>淫滞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364037_comment'></div>萧索穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364037_comment'></div>飘飘一隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364037_comment'></div>昔闻七泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364037_comment'></div>今过五湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364037_comment'></div>听<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1364037", 1364037, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>菱歌</span>兮几曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364037_comment'></div>视莲房兮几珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364037_comment'></div>非邺池之宴语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364037_comment'></div>异睢苑之欢娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364037_comment'></div>况复殊方别域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364037_comment'></div>重瀛复嶂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364037_comment'></div>虞翻则故乡寥落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364037_comment'></div>许靖则生涯惆怅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364037_comment'></div>感芳草之及时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364037_comment'></div>惧修名之或丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364037_comment'></div>誓将刬迹颍上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364037_comment'></div>栖影渭阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364037_comment'></div>枕箕岫之孤石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364037_comment'></div>汎磻溪之小塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364037_comment'></div>餐素实兮吸绛房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364037_comment'></div>荷为衣兮芰为裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364037_comment'></div>永洁已于丘壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364037_comment'></div>长寄心于君王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364037_comment'></div>且为歌曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364037_comment'></div>芳华兮修名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364037_comment'></div>奇秀兮异植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364037_comment'></div>红光兮碧色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364037_comment'></div>禀天地之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1364037", 1364037, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>淑丽</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364037_comment'></div>承雨露之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364037", 1364037, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>沾饰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364037_comment'></div>莲有藕兮藕有枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364037_comment'></div>才有用兮用有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364037_comment'></div>含香婀娜华实移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364037_comment'></div>为君何当藻凤池。</div><div id='poem_sentence_96_1364037_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
淮安（山阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='02e4d5b21b404e029995a0dba9c90e21_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("02e4d5b21b404e029995a0dba9c90e21");'><span id='02e4d5b21b404e029995a0dba9c90e21_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>　冬,沿大运河经扬州、楚州等地北返回京。作品：《冬日送闾丘序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版第633页。）</span><div id='poem_1364106' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364106' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364106?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬日羁游汾阴送韦少府入洛序</a><span class='authorDate'>（667年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364106")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364106_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364106'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364106'>游汾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364106", 1364106, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>胜壤</span>。楼船高汉帝之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364106_comment'></div>卜洛名都。城邑辨周公之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364106_comment'></div>仰天文而窥日月。虽共光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364106_comment'></div>凭地理而考山川。即殊南北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364106_comment'></div>韦少府玉山四照。珠胎一色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364106_comment'></div>纵横振<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364106", 1364106, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>锋颖</span>之才。吐纳积江湖之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364106_comment'></div>子云笔札。拥鸾凤于行间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364106_comment'></div>孙楚文词。列宫商于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364106", 1364106, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>调下</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364106_comment'></div>牵丝一命。披林野而随班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364106_comment'></div>考绩三年。指兰台而赴选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364106_comment'></div>移征驾。背长亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364106_comment'></div>地隔风烟。人离岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364106_comment'></div>寒原冠盖。既同斟桂之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364106_comment'></div>歧路风尘。即断惊蓬之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364106_comment'></div>下官诗书<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364106", 1364106, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>拓落</span>。羽翮摧颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364106_comment'></div>朝廷无立锥之处。丘园有括囊之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364106_comment'></div>山中事业。暂到渔樵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364106_comment'></div>天下栖迟。少留城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364106_comment'></div>忽逢萍水。对云雨以无聊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364106_comment'></div>倍切穷途。抚形骸而何托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364106_comment'></div>于时冰霜裂地。星象回天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364106_comment'></div>朔风动而关塞寒。明月下而楼台曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364106_comment'></div>各题一字。传之两乡云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364106_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1364106_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a1482f967f4a4025b0ecf9e72a9c3a2c_label'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364100'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364100'>上元二载。高秋八月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364100_comment'></div>人多汴北。地实淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364100_comment'></div>海气近而苍山阴。天光秋而白云晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364100_comment'></div>川涂所亘。郢路极于崤潼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364100_comment'></div>风壤所交。荆门洎于吴越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364100_comment'></div>凭胜地。列<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364100", 1364100, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>雄州</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364100_comment'></div>城池当要害之冲。寮寀尽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364100", 1364100, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>鹓鸾</span>之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364100_comment'></div>昌亭旅食。悲下走之穷愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364100_comment'></div>山曲淹留。属群公之宴喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364100_comment'></div>披<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364100", 1364100, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>鹤雾</span>。陟龙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364100_comment'></div>故人握手。新知满目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364100_comment'></div>饮崔公之盛德。果遇攀轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364100_comment'></div>慕郝氏之高风。还逢解榻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364100_comment'></div>接衣簪于坐右。驻旌棨于城隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364100_comment'></div>临风云而解带。盼江山以挥涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364100_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364100", 1364100, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>岩楹</span>左峙。俯映元潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364100_comment'></div>野径斜开。傍连翠渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364100_comment'></div>青萍布叶。乱荷芰而动秋风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364100_comment'></div>朱草<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364100", 1364100, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>垂荣</span>。杂芝兰而涵晚液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364100_comment'></div>舣仙舟于石岸。荐绮席于沙场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364100_comment'></div>宾友盛而芳樽满。林塘清而上筵肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364100_comment'></div>琴歌迭起。俎豆骈罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364100_comment'></div>烟霞充耳目之玩。鱼鸟尽江湖之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364100_comment'></div>情盘乐极。日暮途遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364100_comment'></div>思染翰以淩云。愿麾戈以留景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364100_comment'></div>嗟乎。素交为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364100_comment'></div>觉老幼之同归。朱绂傥来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364100_comment'></div>岂荣枯之足道。且欣风物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364100_comment'></div>共悦濠梁。齐天地于一指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364100_comment'></div>混飞沈于一贯。嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364100_comment'></div>此欢难再。慇勤北海之筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364100_comment'></div>相见何时。惆怅南溟之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364100_comment'></div>请扬文笔。共记良游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364100_comment'></div>人赋一言。俱成四韵云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364100_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1364100_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: -----title
华阴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7b4928f496f249d5b4d3f8da2e6e94c4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7b4928f496f249d5b4d3f8da2e6e94c4");'><span id='7b4928f496f249d5b4d3f8da2e6e94c4_link'
