0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋,在杨炯家乡小住,作《山亭兴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷9第268页。）</span><div id='poem_1364071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山亭兴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（668年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364071")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364071'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364071'>仁者乐山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364071_comment'></div>智者乐水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364071_comment'></div>即云深山大泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364071_comment'></div>龙蛇为得性之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364071_comment'></div>广汉巨川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364071_comment'></div>珠贝是有殊之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364071_comment'></div>岂徒茂林修竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364071_comment'></div>王右军山阴之兰亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364071_comment'></div>流水长堤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364071_comment'></div>石季伦河阳之梓泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364071_comment'></div>下官天性任真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364071_comment'></div>直言淳朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364071_comment'></div>拙容陋质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364071_comment'></div>眇小之丈夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364071_comment'></div>蹇步穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364071_comment'></div>坎𡒄之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364071_comment'></div>文史足用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364071_comment'></div>不读非道之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364071_comment'></div>气调不羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364071_comment'></div>未被可人之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364071_comment'></div>颍川人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364071_comment'></div>有荀家兄弟之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364071_comment'></div>汉代英奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364071_comment'></div>守陈氏门宗之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364071_comment'></div>乐天知命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364071_comment'></div>一十九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364071_comment'></div>负笈从师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364071_comment'></div>二千馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364071_comment'></div>有宏农公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364071_comment'></div>日下无双。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364071_comment'></div>风流第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364071_comment'></div>仁崖知宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364071_comment'></div>照临明日月之辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364071_comment'></div>广度冲襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364071_comment'></div>磊落压乾坤之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364071_comment'></div>王夷甫之瑶林琼树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364071_comment'></div>直出风尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364071_comment'></div>嵇叔夜之龙章凤姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364071_comment'></div>混同<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>人野</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364071_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>雄谈</span>逸辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364071_comment'></div>吐满腹之精神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364071_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>达学</span>奇才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364071_comment'></div>抱填胸之文籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364071_comment'></div>簪裾见屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364071_comment'></div>轻脱履于西阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364071_comment'></div>山水来游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364071_comment'></div>重横琴于南涧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364071_comment'></div>百年奇表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364071_comment'></div>开壮志于高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364071_comment'></div>千里<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>心期</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364071_comment'></div>得神交于下走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364071_comment'></div>山人对兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364071_comment'></div>即是桃花之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364071_comment'></div>隐士相逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364071_comment'></div>不异菖蒲之涧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364071_comment'></div>黄精<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>野馔</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364071_comment'></div>赤石神脂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364071_comment'></div>玉案金盘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364071_comment'></div>徵石髓于蛟龙之窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364071_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>山樽</span>野酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364071_comment'></div>求玉液于蓬莱之峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364071_comment'></div>溪横燕尾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364071_comment'></div>岩竖龙头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364071_comment'></div>锻野老之真珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364071_comment'></div>挂幽人之明镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364071_comment'></div>山腰半折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364071_comment'></div>溜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>王烈</span>之香膏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364071_comment'></div>洞口横开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364071_comment'></div>滴严遵之芳乳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364071_comment'></div>藤牵赤絮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364071_comment'></div>南方之物产可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364071_comment'></div>粉渍青田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364071_comment'></div>外域之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>谣风</span>在即。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364071_comment'></div>人高调远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364071_comment'></div>地爽气清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364071_comment'></div>抱玉策而登高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364071_comment'></div>出琼林而更远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364071_comment'></div>汉家二百所之都郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364071_comment'></div>宫殿平看。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364071_comment'></div>秦树四十郡之封畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364071_comment'></div>山河坐见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364071_comment'></div>班孟坚骋两京雄笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364071_comment'></div>以为天地之奥区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364071_comment'></div>张平子奋一代宏才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364071_comment'></div>以为帝王之神丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364071_comment'></div>珠城隐隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364071_comment'></div>阑干象北斗之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364071_comment'></div>清渭澄澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364071_comment'></div>滉漾即天河之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364071_comment'></div>长松茂柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364071_comment'></div>钻宇宙而顿风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364071_comment'></div>大壑横溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364071_comment'></div>吐江河而悬日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364071_comment'></div>凤凰神岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364071_comment'></div>起烟雾而当轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364071_comment'></div>鹦鹉春泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364071_comment'></div>杂风花而满谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364071_comment'></div>望平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364071_comment'></div>荫丛薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364071_comment'></div>山情放旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364071_comment'></div>即沧浪之水清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364071_comment'></div>野气萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364071_comment'></div>即崆峒之人智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364071_comment'></div>摇头坐唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364071_comment'></div>顿足起舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364071_comment'></div>风尘洒落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364071_comment'></div>直上天池九万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364071_comment'></div>邱墟雄壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364071_comment'></div>傍吞少华五千仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364071_comment'></div>裁二仪为舆盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364071_comment'></div>倚八荒为户牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364071_comment'></div>荣者吾不知其荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364071_comment'></div>美者吾不知其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364071_comment'></div>下官以词峰直上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364071_comment'></div>振笔札而前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364071_comment'></div>高明以翰苑横开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364071_comment'></div>列文章于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_116_1364071", 1364071, "Clauses/116/Comments/0")'>后殿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364071_comment'></div>情兴未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364071_comment'></div>即令樽中酒空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364071_comment'></div>彩笔未穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364071_comment'></div>须使山中兔尽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_120_1364071_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋,在杨炯家乡小住,作《秋日饯别序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷8第237页。）</span><div id='poem_1364101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364101?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋日饯别序</a><span class='authorDate'>（668年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364101")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364101'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364101'>黯然别之销魂。悲哉秋之为气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364101_comment'></div>人之情也。伤如之何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364101_comment'></div>极野苍茫。白露凉风之八月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364101_comment'></div>穷途萧瑟。青山白云之万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364101_comment'></div>奏鸣琴则离鹍别鹤。惊歧路之悲心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364101_comment'></div>来胜地则时雨凉风。助他乡之旅思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364101_comment'></div>琴书人物。冀北关西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364101_comment'></div>去马归轩。云间日下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364101_comment'></div>杨学士天璞自然。地灵无对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364101_comment'></div>二十八宿禀太微之一星。六十四爻受乾坤之两卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364101_comment'></div>论其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364101", 1364101, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>器宇</span>。沧海添江汉之波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364101_comment'></div>序其文章。元圃积烟霞之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364101_comment'></div>几神之外。犹是卿云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364101_comment'></div>陶铸之馀。尚同嵇阮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364101_comment'></div>接光仪于促席。直观明月生天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364101_comment'></div>响词辩于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364101", 1364101, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>中筵</span>。但觉清风满室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364101_comment'></div>悠哉天地。含灵有喜愠之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364101_comment'></div>邱也东西。怅望积别离之恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364101_comment'></div>烟霞直视。蛇龙去而泉石空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364101_comment'></div>文酒求朋。贤俊散而琴歌断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364101_comment'></div>门生饯别。如北海之郡前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364101_comment'></div>高士将归。似东都之门外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364101_comment'></div>研精<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364101", 1364101, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>麝墨</span>。运思龙章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364101_comment'></div>希存宿昔之资。共启相思之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364101_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364101_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋,在杨炯家乡小住,作《山亭思友人序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷9第273页。）</span><div id='poem_1364072' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364072?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山亭思友人序</a><span class='authorDate'>（668年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364072")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364072'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364072'>高兴之后。中宵起观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364072_comment'></div>举目四望。风寒月清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364072_comment'></div>邻人张氏。有山亭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364072_comment'></div>洞壑横分。奇峰直上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364072_comment'></div>郁然有造化之功矣。嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364072_comment'></div>大丈夫荷帝王之雨露。对清平之日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364072_comment'></div>文章可以经纬天地。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364072", 1364072, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>器局</span>可以畜泄江河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364072_comment'></div>七星可以气冲。八风可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364072", 1364072, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>调合</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364072_comment'></div>独行万里。觉天地之崆峒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364072_comment'></div>高枕百年。见生灵之龌龊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364072_comment'></div>虽俗人不识。下士徒轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364072_comment'></div>顾视天下。亦可以蔽寰中之一半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364072_comment'></div>惜乎此山有月。此地无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364072_comment'></div>清风入琴。黄云对酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364072_comment'></div>虽形骸真性。得礼乐于身中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364072_comment'></div>而宇宙神交。卷烟霞于物表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364072_comment'></div>至若开辟翰苑。扫荡文场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364072_comment'></div>得宫商之正律。受山川之杰气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364072_comment'></div>虽陆平原曹子建。足可以车载斗量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364072_comment'></div>谢灵运潘安仁。足可以膝行肘步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364072_comment'></div>思飞情逸。风云坐宅于笔端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364072_comment'></div>兴洽神清。日月自安于调下云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364072_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1364072_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
兴平（始平）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bd1ad521e82b451aa01d600ae4589b27_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bd1ad521e82b451aa01d600ae4589b27");'><span id='bd1ad521e82b451aa01d600ae4589b27_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>，20岁</div><div id='bd1ad521e82b451aa01d600ae4589b27' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年5月26日</a>　五月二十六日,离京西行赴蜀,经过始平（今陕西兴平）,作《始平晚息》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第102页。始平即今陕西兴平.兴平,在咸阳西、武功东,谭图未详,参汪贤度校点《王子安集注》第102页,上海古籍出版社,1995年版。）</span><div id='poem_8789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8789?labeling=true' target='_blank'>始平晚<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作晓）</span>息</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年5月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8789")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8789_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_8789'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1289, "poem_allusion_8789")'>长安近</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_8789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8789'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8789'>观阙<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1289, "poem_sentence_0_8789")'>长安近</span>，江山蜀路<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作道）</span>赊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8789'>客行朝复夕，无处是乡家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8789'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8789_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扶风
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1d1f1202fb224e0db13a78ec3bf58b79_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1d1f1202fb224e0db13a78ec3bf58b79");'><span id='1d1f1202fb224e0db13a78ec3bf58b79_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>，20岁</div><div id='1d1f1202fb224e0db13a78ec3bf58b79' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>　途经扶风（今属陕西）,作《扶见昼届,离京浸远》诗。作品：《扶风昼届离京浸远》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第102页。）</span><div id='poem_8787' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8787' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8787?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扶风昼届离京浸远</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8787")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8787_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8787'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8787'>帝里金茎去，扶风石柱来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8787'>山川殊未已，行路方悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8787'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8787_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
勉县（西县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7a9b4deddf37498a9c3b674d50d25d48_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7a9b4deddf37498a9c3b674d50d25d48");'><span id='7a9b4deddf37498a9c3b674d50d25d48_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>，20岁</div><div id='7a9b4deddf37498a9c3b674d50d25d48' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>　途经长柳（在今陕西勉县附近）,作《长柳》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第89页。据谭图,今勉县在梁州西县东。）</span><div id='poem_8813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长柳</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8813")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8813'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8813'>晨征犯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8813", 8813, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>烟磴</span>，夕憩在云关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8813'>晚风清近壑，新月照澄湾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8813'>郊童樵唱返，津叟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8813", 8813, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>钓歌</span>还。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8813'>客行无与晤<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作旧识）</span>，赖此释愁颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8813'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8813_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title

-----title
绵阳（巴西）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='496680bb35364795ba12df4764c11175_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("496680bb35364795ba12df4764c11175");'><span id='496680bb35364795ba12df4764c11175_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>，20岁</div><div id='496680bb35364795ba12df4764c11175' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>七月,途经绵州（今四川绵阳）,有仲氏于宅设宴款待,作《仲氏宅宴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷7第201页。）</span><div id='poem_1364088' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364088' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364088?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仲氏宅宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364088")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364088_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364088'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364088'>仆不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364088_comment'></div>在流俗而嗜烟霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364088_comment'></div>恨林泉不比德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364088_comment'></div>而嵇阮不同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364088_comment'></div>处良辰而郁怏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364088_comment'></div>仰高风而杼柚者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364088_comment'></div>岂夫司马卿之车骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364088_comment'></div>上客盈门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364088_comment'></div>仲长统之园林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364088_comment'></div>群英在席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364088_comment'></div>坐卧南郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364088_comment'></div>萧条东野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364088_comment'></div>江波浩旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364088_comment'></div>晴山纷积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364088_comment'></div>嘉鸳鸾之接翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364088_comment'></div>曜江汉之多才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364088_comment'></div>顾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364088", 1364088, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>斜景</span>而危心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364088_comment'></div>瞻火云而变色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364088_comment'></div>思传胜饯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364088_comment'></div>敢振文锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364088_comment'></div>盖同席者高人薛曜等耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364088_comment'></div>盍各赋诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364088_comment'></div>放怀叙志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364088_comment'></div>俾山川获申于知已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364088_comment'></div>烟霞受制于吾徒也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364088_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>七月,绵州群官设宴款待,并与薛曜别,作《秋日于绵州群官席别薛升华并序》一文与《秋日别薛升华》诗。作品：《秋夜于绵州群官席别薛升华序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷9第263页。）</span>《别薛华》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第80页。《王子安集注》作《别薛华》）</span><div id='poem_1364102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋夜于绵州群官席别薛升华序</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364102")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364102'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364102'>夫神明所贵者道也。天地所宝者才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364102_comment'></div>故虽阴阳同功。宇宙戮力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364102_comment'></div>山川崩腾以作气。星象磊落以降精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364102_comment'></div>终不能五百年而生两贤也。故曰才难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364102_comment'></div>不其然乎。今之群公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364102_comment'></div>并受奇彩。各仗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364102", 1364102, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>异气</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364102_comment'></div>或江海其量。或林泉其识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364102_comment'></div>或簪裾其迹。或云汉其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364102_comment'></div>不可双得也。今并集此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364102_comment'></div>岂英灵之道长。而造化之功倍乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364102_comment'></div>然仆之区区。常以为人之百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364102_comment'></div>犹如一瞬。非不知风月不足怀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364102_comment'></div>琴樽不足恋也。事有切而未能忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364102_comment'></div>情有深而未能遣。故仆射群公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364102_comment'></div>相知非不深也。相期非不厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364102_comment'></div>然义有四海之重。而无同方之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364102_comment'></div>分有一面之深。而非累叶之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364102_comment'></div>故与夫升华者其异乎。嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364102_comment'></div>积潘杨之远好。同河汾之灵液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364102_comment'></div>目置良友。相依穷路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364102_comment'></div>是月秋也。于时夕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364102_comment'></div>他乡怨而白露寒。故人去而青山迥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364102_comment'></div>不其悲乎。盍各赋诗云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364102_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1364102_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_8821' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8821' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8821?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别薛华<span class='inlineComment2'>（《英华》作《秋日别薛升华》）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（669年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8821")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8821_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8821'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8821'>送送多穷路，遑遑独问津。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8821'>悲凉千里道，悽断百年身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8821'>心事同漂泊，生涯共苦辛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8821'>无论去与住，俱是梦中人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8821'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_8821'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(8821)'>评注</a><span
