DetailSwitch("44eb248d8e14460281ad50c1c7292e29");'><span id='44eb248d8e14460281ad50c1c7292e29_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>，22岁</div><div id='44eb248d8e14460281ad50c1c7292e29' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　于绵州决定离蜀,与绵州众僚宴别,有《绵州北亭群公宴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷7第218页。）</span><div id='poem_1364094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364094?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绵州北亭群公宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364094")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364094'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364094'>下官人间独傲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364094_comment'></div>海内少徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364094_comment'></div>志不屈于王侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364094_comment'></div>身不绝于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364094", 1364094, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>尘俗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364094_comment'></div>孤吟五岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364094_comment'></div>长啸三山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364094_comment'></div>昔往东吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364094_comment'></div>已有梁鸿之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364094_comment'></div>今来西蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364094_comment'></div>非无张载之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364094_comment'></div>况乎践<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364094", 1364094, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>名场</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364094_comment'></div>携胜友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364094_comment'></div>风月无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364094_comment'></div>琴酒俄乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364094_comment'></div>半面十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364094_comment'></div>一别千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364094_comment'></div>何少府故人攀桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364094_comment'></div>抚金石而论心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364094_comment'></div>韩法曹新识班荆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364094_comment'></div>临江湖而执手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364094_comment'></div>离亭北望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364094_comment'></div>烟霞生故国之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364094_comment'></div>别馆南开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364094_comment'></div>风雨积他乡之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364094_comment'></div>于时苍云寡色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364094_comment'></div>白日无光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364094_comment'></div>沙尘起而桂浦昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364094_comment'></div>凫雁下而芦洲晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364094_comment'></div>傍邻苍野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364094_comment'></div>霜风橘柚之园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364094_comment'></div>斜枕碧潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364094_comment'></div>夜月芙蓉之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364094_comment'></div>既而登临惜别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364094_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1364094", 1364094, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>骖驾</span>少留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364094_comment'></div>季札何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364094_comment'></div>亲逢赠缟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364094_comment'></div>子荆不敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364094_comment'></div>思挂倾城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364094_comment'></div>惆怅北梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364094_comment'></div>揖琴台而渐间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364094_comment'></div>徘徊东道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364094_comment'></div>思锦署以行遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364094_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364094_comment'></div>人事乖矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364094_comment'></div>江山远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364094_comment'></div>请命离前之笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364094_comment'></div>为题别后之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364094_comment'></div>五际飞文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364094_comment'></div>想群公之不让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364094_comment'></div>一言有赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364094_comment'></div>知下笔之有神。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1364094_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
三台（郪县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='060e364db1c749d09ac2bccd1a9deaa8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("060e364db1c749d09ac2bccd1a9deaa8");'><span id='060e364db1c749d09ac2bccd1a9deaa8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>，20岁</div><div id='060e364db1c749d09ac2bccd1a9deaa8' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>八月,抵梓州（州治为郪县,在今四川三台县）,作《江曲孤凫赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷1第32页。）</span><div id='poem_1364038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江曲孤凫赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364038")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364038_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364038'>梓州之东南。涪江之所合。有潭焉。周数十步。青壁绝地。绿波澄天。常有孤凫。栖荡其侧。飞沈翻唼。而天性不违。嗟乎。宇宙之容我多矣。造化之资我厚矣。何必处华池之内。而求稻粱之恩哉。遂作赋曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364038'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364038", 1364038, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>灵凤</span>翔兮千仞。大鹏飞兮六月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364038_comment'></div>虽凭力而易举。终候时而难发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364038_comment'></div>不如深泽之鸟焉。顺归潮而出没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364038_comment'></div>迹已存于江汉。心非系于城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364038_comment'></div>吮红藻。翻碧莲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364038_comment'></div>刷雾露。栖云烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364038_comment'></div>迫之则隐。驯之则前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364038_comment'></div>去就无失。浮沈自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364038_comment'></div>尔乃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364038", 1364038, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>忘机</span>绝虑。怀声弄影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364038_comment'></div>乘骇浪而神惊。漾澄澜而趣静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364038_comment'></div>耻园鸡之恋促。悲塞鸿之赴永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364038_comment'></div>知动息而多方。屡沿洄而自省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364038_comment'></div>故其独泛单宿。全真远致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364038_comment'></div>反复幽溪。淹留胜地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364038_comment'></div>伤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364038", 1364038, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>云雁</span>之婴缴。惧泉鱼之受饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364038_comment'></div>甘辞稻粱之惠焉。而全饮啄之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364038_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1364038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>八月,在梓州（州治为郪县,在今四川三台县）作《涧底寒松赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷2第37页。）</span><div id='poem_1364039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>涧底寒松赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364039")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364039_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364039'>岁八月壬子。旅游于蜀。寻茅溪之涧。深溪绝磴。人迹罕到。爰有松焉。冒霜停雪。苍然百丈。虽崇柯峻颖。不能踰其岸。呜呼斯松。托非其所。出群之器。何以别乎。盖物有类而合情。士因感而成兴。遂作赋曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364039'>惟松之植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364039_comment'></div>于涧之幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364039_comment'></div>盘柯跨崄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364039_comment'></div>沓柢凭流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364039_comment'></div>寓天地兮何日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364039_comment'></div>沾雨露兮几秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364039_comment'></div>见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364039", 1364039, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>时华</span>之屡变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364039_comment'></div>知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364039", 1364039, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>俗态</span>之多浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364039_comment'></div>故其磊落殊状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364039_comment'></div>森梢峻节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364039_comment'></div>紫叶吟风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364039_comment'></div>苍条振雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364039_comment'></div>嗟英鉴之希遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364039_comment'></div>保贞容之未缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364039_comment'></div>攀翠崿而形疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364039_comment'></div>指丹霄而望绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364039_comment'></div>已矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364039_comment'></div>盖用轻则资众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364039_comment'></div>器宏则施寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364039_comment'></div>信栋梁之已成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364039_comment'></div>非榱桷之相假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364039_comment'></div>徒志远而心屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364039_comment'></div>遂才高而位下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364039_comment'></div>斯在物而有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364039_comment'></div>余何为而悲者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364039_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>八月,在梓州（州治为郪县,在今四川三台县）作《青苔赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷2第40页。）</span><div id='poem_1364040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青苔赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364040")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364040_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364040'>吾之旅游数月矣。憩乎荒涧。睹青苔焉。缘崖而上。乃喟然而叹曰。嗟乎。苔之生于林塘也。为幽客之赏。苔之生于轩庭也。为居人之怨。斯择地而处。无累于物也。爱憎从而生。遂作赋曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364040'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364040'>若夫桂洲含润。松崖秘液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364040_comment'></div>绕江曲之寒沙。抱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364040", 1364040, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>岩幽</span>之古石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364040_comment'></div>汎回塘而积翠。萦修树而凝碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364040_comment'></div>契山客之奇情。谐野人之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364040", 1364040, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>妙适</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364040_comment'></div>及其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364040", 1364040, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>瑶房</span>有寂。琼室无光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364040_comment'></div>霏微君子之砌。蔓延君侯之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364040_comment'></div>引浮青而泛露。散轻绿而承霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364040_comment'></div>起金钿之旧感。惊玉箸之新行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364040_comment'></div>若夫弱质绵羃。纤滋布濩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364040_comment'></div>措形不用之境。托迹无人之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364040_comment'></div>望夷险而齐归。在高深而委遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364040_comment'></div>惟爱憎之未染。何悲欢之诡赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364040_comment'></div>宜其背阳就阴。违喧处静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364040_comment'></div>不根不蒂。无华无影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364040_comment'></div>耻桃李之暂芳。笑兰桂之非永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364040_comment'></div>故顺时而不竞。每乘幽而自整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364040_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1364040_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c099dcafda59416eb3b71007538aead1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c099dcafda59416eb3b71007538aead1");'><span id='c099dcafda59416eb3b71007538aead1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=670')">669-670年</a>，20-21岁</div><div id='c099dcafda59416eb3b71007538aead1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>　冬,复归梓州郪县（今四川三台）,作《梓州郪县兜率寺浮图碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷17第510页。）</span><div id='poem_1364134' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364134' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364134?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梓州郪县兜率寺浮图碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364134")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364134_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364134'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364134'>若夫仙楼白玉。窈冥昆阆之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364134_comment'></div>神阙黄金。寂寞蓬瀛之浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364134_comment'></div>斯则冈峦髣髴。稽凤册而空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364134_comment'></div>岛屿凭陵。𫇢龙舟而罕迨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364134_comment'></div>至若按皇轩于夏箓。考璿构于殷图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364134_comment'></div>周王北洛之宫。秦帝南山之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364134_comment'></div>西京故事。下听雷霆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364134_comment'></div>东国馀基。俛临风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364134_comment'></div>莫不陵迁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>谷变</span>。共榛灌而邱墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364134_comment'></div>火绝烟沈。与风云而坱莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364134_comment'></div>其有据坤灵之宝位。借神道之冥扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364134_comment'></div>占象纬而图基。揆川原而宅址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364134_comment'></div>蜂台映月。还临舍卫之城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364134_comment'></div>雁塔寻云。即对耆阇之岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364134_comment'></div>成而不毁者。将斯之谓欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364134_comment'></div>兜率寺者。隋开皇中之所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364134_comment'></div>尔其林泉纠合之势。山川表里之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364134_comment'></div>抽紫岩而四绝。謺丹峰而万变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364134_comment'></div>连溪拒壑。所以控引太虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364134_comment'></div>蒸云驾雨。所以荡泄元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364134_comment'></div>涪江千仞。波潮将旭日争光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364134_comment'></div>都城百雉。甍栋与晴霞共色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364134_comment'></div>信造化之奇模。尽登临之妙境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364134_comment'></div>元房雾转。抗金枢于桂岊之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364134_comment'></div>绀殿星开。栖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>玉刹</span>于梅林之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364134_comment'></div>岩花落沼。近拂天衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364134_comment'></div>涧叶低阴。斜笼宝座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364134_comment'></div>宵汀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>鹤警</span>。乘鼓吹而齐鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364134_comment'></div>晓峡猿清。挟霜钟而赴节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364134_comment'></div>若乃巡碧磴。历元阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364134_comment'></div>琐窗澄彩。琼铺洞照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364134_comment'></div>神姿满月。疑临石镜之峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364134_comment'></div>众馥扬烟。似对香炉之岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364134_comment'></div>信可下清人境。上配天都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364134_comment'></div>为胜地之先鸣。执名山之右契者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364134_comment'></div>爰有信弟子某乙等。夙祛尘网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364134_comment'></div>早植慈根。悲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>梵室</span>之未宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364134_comment'></div>悼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>禅居</span>之犹褊。以为上栋下宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364134_comment'></div>河图避风雨之灾。广榭崇台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364134_comment'></div>时令著<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>高明</span>之宅。是以菩提长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364134_comment'></div>竞洁舍卫之坛。天帝人皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364134_comment'></div>争辟仙宫之塔。则知威容下丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364134_comment'></div>群生解瞻仰之因。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>材朴</span>重雕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364134_comment'></div>黎人有子来之地。乃于寺内建浮图一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364134_comment'></div>某年月日。乡望等兆基宏愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364134_comment'></div>继发净因。陵轹中天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364134_comment'></div>规模大壮。高列砌架。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364134_comment'></div>迥浮轾轩。直上千寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364134_comment'></div>周回百步。占氛候景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364134_comment'></div>神祇叶幽赞之功。揆墨端行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364134_comment'></div>班倕逞绝群之思。收岱宗之梓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364134_comment'></div>聚昆山之玉石。土兼五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364134_comment'></div>金逾百鍊。龙蟠万栱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364134_comment'></div>策屏翳而高骧。鹤矫千楣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364134_comment'></div>冠扶摇而独运。重檐霭霭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364134_comment'></div>云将反覆于棂轩。洞宇寥寥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364134_comment'></div>风伯栖遑于户牖。仙娥去月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364134_comment'></div>旅方镜而忘归。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>宝婺</span>辞星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364134_comment'></div>攀圆珰而未返。元甍湛䨴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364134_comment'></div>若鹏飞之戾九天。丹楹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/119/Comments/0")'>联骞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364134_comment'></div>如凤翔之据九仞。每至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>韶光</span>照野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364134_comment'></div>爽霭晴遥。列郊墟于四野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364134_comment'></div>开云气于千里。风恬雨霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364134_comment'></div>烟雾藻天地之容。野旷川明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364134_comment'></div>风景挟江山之助。则有雕帘绣轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364134_comment'></div>排净域而停轮。宝骑银鞍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364134_comment'></div>指珍台而耸辔。于是披岫幌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364134_comment'></div>抵岩扃。攀翠复而三休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364134_comment'></div>步元梁而十憩。廊轩外敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364134_comment'></div>淑气长延。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>阴室</span>中开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364134_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/140/Comments/0")'>鲜飙</span>自激。俯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/141/Comments/0")'>环瀛</span>而极望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364134_comment'></div>积藓非遥。出云汉而高践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364134_comment'></div>灵槎可托。真福地之殊观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364134_comment'></div>香城之巨丽者乎。寺主等沈研二谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364134_comment'></div>振耀三明。抵苍璧于邪山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364134_comment'></div>揽元珠于定水。挹其流者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364134_comment'></div>曲成般若之缘。承其风者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364134_comment'></div>浚发菩提之愿。长史河东裴某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364134_comment'></div>风神<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>朗润</span>。操履<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/157/Comments/0")'>贞勤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364134_comment'></div>萧条江海之心。磊砢冰霜之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364134_comment'></div>下岷关而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_80_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/160/Comments/0")'>叱驭</span>。寄切全都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364134_comment'></div>临蜀野而宣条。功深半剌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364134_comment'></div>县令卫元。海内高流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364134_comment'></div>河东望族。荣高铜墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364134_comment'></div>任屈弦歌。浃辰而风化大行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364134_comment'></div>踰月而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/170/Comments/0")'>奸豪</span>屏气。陶潜彭泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364134_comment'></div>自得高人。王吉临邛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364134_comment'></div>仍延<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/174/Comments/0")'>重客</span>。县丞胡敬仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364134_comment'></div>三河旧族。一代良材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364134_comment'></div>提镆铘而愿割。跼骅骝而待步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364134_comment'></div>江湖秋至。方怀纵壑之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364134_comment'></div>海浪风高。未接垂天之翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364134_comment'></div>乡望等并中和受气。孝友承家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364134_comment'></div>才称江汉之灵。地实岷峨之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364134_comment'></div>或以时良入选。擢迹乡邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364134_comment'></div>或以朝望来仪。升名郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364134_comment'></div>并沐康衢之化。俱承比屋之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364134_comment'></div>瞻彼岸而同归。登春台而共乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364134_comment'></div>咸以垣墉遽覆。犹传路寝之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364134_comment'></div>银鼎俄穷。尚勒灵台之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364134_comment'></div>况乎崇基奕奕。与天地而争工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364134_comment'></div>层构峨峨。配山川而永固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364134_comment'></div>岂可使宏规在我。空存蔽日之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364134_comment'></div>雄笔同时。不借淩云之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364134_comment'></div>谨闻命矣。乃作铭云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364134_comment'></div>二象成纪。三才定位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364134_comment'></div>开剖太虚。导引元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364134_comment'></div>纷纷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/214/Comments/0")'>化迹</span>。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/215/Comments/0")'>飙飙</span>圣致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364134_comment'></div>行杰趣约。归同弃异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364134_comment'></div>法王西眷。教迹东游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364134_comment'></div>功超道茂。义冠儒流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364134_comment'></div>丹青既备。栋宇旋周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364134_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/224/Comments/0")'>梵宫</span>霞积。香阁星浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364134_comment'></div>缅想蓬瀛。金台迥起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364134_comment'></div>旷瞻昆阆。瑶房峻峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364134_comment'></div>壮矣名都。神居攸止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364134_comment'></div>大哉英服。兹峰诞纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364134_comment'></div>金绳对岭。玉榜分岑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364134_comment'></div>松扃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_118_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/236/Comments/0")'>委郁</span>。桂幌深沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364134_comment'></div>云龛树晦。烟洞花深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364134_comment'></div>重峦雾结。复涧泉吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364134_comment'></div>肃肃禅众。遥遥净镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364134_comment'></div>鹿野经文。龙宫佛影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364134_comment'></div>梵臻金室。光来石井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364134_comment'></div>峡晓猿清。池曛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_124_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/249/Comments/0")'>鹤警</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364134_comment'></div>岷峨旧族。江汉英姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364134_comment'></div>争开法愿。重峻崇基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364134_comment'></div>占云接庑。揆景分墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364134_comment'></div>天人合应。幽显呈期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364134_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_129_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/258/Comments/0")'>灵思</span>孤出。神模独涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364134_comment'></div>雾积千楹。霞张万栱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364134_comment'></div>玉牖星罗。璿珰月拥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364134_comment'></div>复榭龙蟠。重甍凤耸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364134_comment'></div>峨峨峻岊。奕奕崇标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364134_comment'></div>雕檐切汉。宝缀淩霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364134_comment'></div>深窗閟景。洞户<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_135_1364134", 1364134, "Clauses/271/Comments/0")'>流飙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364134_comment'></div>银釭夕映。珠铎晨摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364134_comment'></div>我辞秦陇。来游巴蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364134_comment'></div>胜地归心。名都憩足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364134_comment'></div>甫建乡县。频移灰烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364134_comment'></div>聿从良时。仍寻妙躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364134_comment'></div>旷望原陆。周流江汜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364134_comment'></div>桃李春风。芙蓉秋水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364134_comment'></div>烟霞四面。关山千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364134_comment'></div>他乡寓目。兹焉复几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364134_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_145_1364134_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>　冬,复归梓州郪县（今四川三台）,作《梓州郪县灵瑞寺浮图碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷18第547页。）</span><div id='poem_1364139' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364139' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364139?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梓州郪县灵瑞寺浮图碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364139")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364139_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364139'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364139'>辨夫神州<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364139", 1364139, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>括地</span>。寰中分五岳之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364139_comment'></div>巨壑浮天。海上擢三山之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364139_comment'></div>造化之所枢纽。灵仙之所窟宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364139_comment'></div>故得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364139", 1364139, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>昭灼</span>天汉。发挥云气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364139_comment'></div>牛头山者。即广汉之名峰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364139_comment'></div>圆裔几乎数里。直上逾乎百仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364139_comment'></div>若乃岩泉铣石之什。风烟草木之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364139_comment'></div>倾九围而得隽。环四时而竞爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364139_comment'></div>苍岑隐嶙。旁分玉砌之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364139_comment'></div>碧洞逶迤。下掬金陵之苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364139_comment'></div>实群圣之所托也。隋开皇中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364139_comment'></div>王秀作牧益州。来窥胜地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364139_comment'></div>首旌嘉号。仍疏净域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364139_comment'></div>因危裂户。就岭磴之成规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364139_comment'></div>跨险分荣。借冈峦之迥势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364139_comment'></div>工穷雕镂。妙出丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364139_comment'></div>飞栋神行。回甍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364139", 1364139, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>灵构</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364139_comment'></div>又于山顶。别建浮图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364139_comment'></div>隋运告迁。明皇首出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364139_comment'></div>轩疏凋昧。基砋堙芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364139_comment'></div>奄兴宣榭之灾。施及柏梁之烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364139_comment'></div>乡望等驰心妙律。夙契禅居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364139_comment'></div>悲梵宇之摧梁。痛珍台之绝构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364139_comment'></div>思宏法愿。重缉奇功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364139_comment'></div>党集且千。家惟巨万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364139_comment'></div>以为玉楼星峙。稽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364139", 1364139, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>阆苑</span>之全模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364139_comment'></div>金阙霞飞。得瀛洲之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364139_comment'></div>指香城而耸睇。临火宅而危魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364139_comment'></div>参妙范于神明。骋良工于宇宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364139_comment'></div>飞廉按辔。定枢臬于风衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364139_comment'></div>羲和顿策。揆钩绳于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1364139", 1364139, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>日路</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364139_comment'></div>雕檐画栱。龙回紫汉之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364139_comment'></div>复霤重栾。凤举丹霄之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364139_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1364139", 1364139, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>琼扉</span>暮敞。推明月于金铺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364139_comment'></div>绣桷晨开。落繁星于玉砌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364139_comment'></div>每至两江春返。四野晴初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364139_comment'></div>山川霁而风景凉。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364139", 1364139, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>林甸</span>清而云雾绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364139_comment'></div>沙汀送暖。落花与新燕争飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364139_comment'></div>城邑迎寒。凉叶共初鸿竞起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364139_comment'></div>则有都人袭赏。凭紫楹而延衿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364139_comment'></div>野客含情。俯丹棂而极睇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364139_comment'></div>穷百年之后乐。写千里之长怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364139_comment'></div>信可以澡雪神襟。清疏视听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364139_comment'></div>忘机境于纷扰。置怀抱于真寂者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364139_comment'></div>且勃旅游岷徼。漂举涪乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364139_comment'></div>年晷一穷。时灰七变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364139_comment'></div>王阳西上。方惊敛辔之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364139_comment'></div>王粲南征。实动登楼之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364139_comment'></div>我之怀矣。乃作颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364139_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1364139'>大块甄筫。名山作纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364139_comment'></div>登地龙盘。干霄凤峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364139_comment'></div>风雪万邑。冈峦千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364139_comment'></div>绝域天成。珍台地起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364139_comment'></div>揆刹元岭。图基丹峤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364139_comment'></div>层栋峥嵘。重檐𥦖窱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364139_comment'></div>有隋紊历。重明改照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364139_comment'></div>事与时迁。迹从原燎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364139_comment'></div>义均除旧。事切为新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364139_comment'></div>如或继者。代有其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364139_comment'></div>声飞陇蜀。望动州邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364139_comment'></div>争开禅施。竞植<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1364139", 1364139, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>灵因</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364139_comment'></div>控险裁标。循危列搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364139_comment'></div>岩烟接庑。风云对霤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364139_comment'></div>铎运星衢。珰悬月窦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364139_comment'></div>紫轩雾合。丹梁露透。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364139_comment'></div>暮春疏节。新秋戒序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364139_comment'></div>照满暄郊。气销寒渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364139_comment'></div>树浓莺乱。川长雁举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364139_comment'></div>流涕写怀。魂驰意与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364139_comment'></div>伟哉灵宇。壮矣全模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364139_comment'></div>穷高极丽。远览长图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364139_comment'></div>赏因时合。笔为神驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364139_comment'></div>有情君子。谁为舍乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364139_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1364139_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>　冬,复归梓州郪县（今四川三台）,作《唐故河东处士卫某夫人贺拔氏墓志并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版第650页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　春,往来梓州、玄武间,作《梓州通泉县惠普寺碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷17第500页。）</span><div id='poem_1364138' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364138' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364138?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梓州通泉县惠普寺碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364138")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364138_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364138'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364138'>若夫元机默运。披睿烈于三精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364138_comment'></div>素键潜融。肇神功于万汇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364138_comment'></div>则有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>灵期</span>肸蚃。龟龙负河洛之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364138_comment'></div>帝绪氤氲。贤哲举乾坤之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364138_comment'></div>虽功悬日月。终植轨于寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364138_comment'></div>业静云雷。未逃规于象外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364138_comment'></div>尔其译雉林之宝偈。诠鹫岭之真图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364138_comment'></div>抽紫玉于禅山。朗元珠于智水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364138_comment'></div>不生不灭。光临妙物之津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364138_comment'></div>无去无来。璿发乘时之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364138_comment'></div>仗三明而独运。施洽平分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364138_comment'></div>据二谛而同归。功超邃古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364138_comment'></div>故能使三千法界。向风知衽席之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364138_comment'></div>百亿天王。闻道失岩廊之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364138_comment'></div>非释迦之神化。其孰能与于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364138_comment'></div>既而正法将隐。微言不嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364138_comment'></div>应身既没。遗仪间起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364138_comment'></div>恒星夜掩。西天衔风雾之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364138_comment'></div>梦日宵成。东汉肃坛场之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364138_comment'></div>由是鹿园层敞。象教旁流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364138_comment'></div>宣妙奖于希夷。范<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>灵踪</span>于显晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364138_comment'></div>瑶龛宝座。光华震旦之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364138_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>凤刹</span>蜺裳。斧藻阎浮之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364138_comment'></div>其寺盖梁大同中年所建。地分彭蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364138_comment'></div>岭对岷峨。凭广汉之遗墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364138_comment'></div>藉犍为之旧壤。西驰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>峭崿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364138_comment'></div>山连白雉之郊。东赴长川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364138_comment'></div>江走黄牛之峡。崇墉却峙之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364138_comment'></div>庭衢四会。胜里九曲之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364138_comment'></div>闾阎万积。危冠袨服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364138_comment'></div>参差轩盖之前。露渚风畦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364138_comment'></div>隐轸亭皋之望。是惟仙境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364138_comment'></div>实启香城。焕若神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364138_comment'></div>恍同化出。绀坛烟属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364138_comment'></div>疏绝阁而三休。紫殿云深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364138_comment'></div>彻回廊而四注。重栾复栋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364138_comment'></div>雾缉霞张。绣桷雕楣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364138_comment'></div>鸾伸鹤跂。珍台控景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364138_comment'></div>羲和获练辔之因。绮榭裁氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364138_comment'></div>屏翳得停镳之所。连甍积翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364138_comment'></div>交玉琐于星衢。洞户流丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364138_comment'></div>缀金铺于月窦。垂珠网露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364138_comment'></div>傍倾汉浦之琛。列铎吟飙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364138_comment'></div>上合钧天之乐。固以轮奂之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364138_comment'></div>冠真宰以先鸣。雕范之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364138_comment'></div>告<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>灵基</span>而得隽。乃造弥勒下生像一座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364138_comment'></div>相好端足。华姿朗备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364138_comment'></div>贞观末年。灵晖继发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364138_comment'></div>房栊匝曜。疑连不夜之城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364138_comment'></div>户牖皆明。似出重昏之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364138_comment'></div>自非理参幽赞。道叶冥机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364138_comment'></div>宣佛镜于无方。演慈灯于已绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364138_comment'></div>岂能写丹青于实相。妙色长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364138_comment'></div>图铣鋈于真容。神光不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364138_comment'></div>若乃时暄福地。低落照于晴晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364138_comment'></div>候肃禅房。汛初华于霁景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364138_comment'></div>千千宝树。若在双林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364138_comment'></div>一一妙香。仍清八味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364138_comment'></div>山翚傃晚。跂叶屿而相鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364138_comment'></div>野燕迎晨。拂花帘而自乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364138_comment'></div>松楹秀蔓。曲成萝薜之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364138_comment'></div>砌石生莲。直起芙蓉之座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364138_comment'></div>则有施身童子。戾止岩扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364138_comment'></div>忍辱仙人。来仪涧户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364138_comment'></div>都人野彦。希<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>梵席</span>而投裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364138_comment'></div>赵美燕姝。望斋庭而继履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364138_comment'></div>莫不青凫委贯。俱欣不舍之坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364138_comment'></div>紫贝蒹明。共化无缘之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364138_comment'></div>故能使雕形画塔。象设年滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364138_comment'></div>彩帙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/138/Comments/0")'>瑶箱</span>。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>龙编</span>月久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364138_comment'></div>岂西周之道备。南国之风成者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364138_comment'></div>爰有寺主等。覃机色外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364138_comment'></div>练迹尘间。浴甘露于身田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364138_comment'></div>集祥风于性宇。栖情不二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364138_comment'></div>忽起初地之权。援手大千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364138_comment'></div>犹拥弥天之具。县令等或公侯百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364138_comment'></div>元貂列驷之门。或文史三冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364138_comment'></div>吐凤回鸾之客。铜章墨绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364138_comment'></div>任切临人。铁印黄簪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364138_comment'></div>功宣渐陆。局牛烹而待价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364138_comment'></div>肆蠖屈以求伸。挥锋九仞之隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364138_comment'></div>作镜双流之外。录事柳元等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364138_comment'></div>丹轩紫绂。家传<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/165/Comments/0")'>方面</span>之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364138_comment'></div>骥子鱼文。地列膏腴之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364138_comment'></div>昔承隋运。屡委天书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364138_comment'></div>爰自皇初。颛流帝礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364138_comment'></div>等賨渝之奉汉。类微濮之匡周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364138_comment'></div>咸申白马之盟。并受飞龙之托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364138_comment'></div>故能遗风罔坠。代济其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364138_comment'></div>望重西南。功宣法俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364138_comment'></div>咸以为弦歌小政。犹篆德而垂芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364138_comment'></div>钟鼎微荣。尚铭勋而作鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364138_comment'></div>况乎神威自在。方传<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/185/Comments/0")'>宰匠</span>之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364138_comment'></div>岂可栋宇常存。不勒山河之赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364138_comment'></div>爰托幽鄙。奉扬徽猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364138_comment'></div>敢宣此义。而为颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364138_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_1364138'>天地定位。君臣作极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364138_comment'></div>道在岩廊。功沾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_97_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/195/Comments/0")'>寰域</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364138_comment'></div>尚清皇盼。犹歌帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364138_comment'></div>况我能仁。惟神不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364138_comment'></div>诞生迦室。利见王城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364138_comment'></div>机覃有应。业会无生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364138_comment'></div>长驱定境。振旅魔营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364138_comment'></div>恩兼动植。势绝随迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364138_comment'></div>燕山倾仞。鹤林埋景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364138_comment'></div>慧日西沈。慈波东骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364138_comment'></div>竞窥灵相。争参佛影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364138_comment'></div>月殿分城。云龛动岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364138_comment'></div>长江旧域。广汉遗区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364138_comment'></div>川分潼峡。塞接岷渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364138_comment'></div>闾阎四会。亭障<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/221/Comments/0")'>威纡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364138_comment'></div>爰开宝地。实控名都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364138_comment'></div>霞墙百雉。云甍四注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364138_comment'></div>紫阙寻烟。赪楼结雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364138_comment'></div>波流虹起。雷奔蠖步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364138_comment'></div>网罩星鹑。珰栖月兔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364138_comment'></div>灵机藻繂。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_116_1364138", 1364138, "Clauses/233/Comments/0")'>禅室</span>安闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364138_comment'></div>雕金范玉。举翠浮丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364138_comment'></div>神宫不夜。虚室长寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364138_comment'></div>光超有色。贶出无端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364138_comment'></div>清露花径。飞泉业户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364138_comment'></div>涧绿苔秋。山苍树古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364138_comment'></div>茫茫庶类。巍巍净土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364138_comment'></div>鹅鹭同归。华夷共聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364138_comment'></div>第一义谛。寥廓法门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364138_comment'></div>迹离生灭。思举乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364138_comment'></div>情迷则复。道在为尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364138_comment'></div>惟名与器。万古长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364138_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_128_1364138_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　春,往来梓州、玄武间,作《上巳浮江宴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷7第202页。）</span><div id='poem_1364078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上已浮江宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364078")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364078_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364078'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364078'>吾之生也有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364078_comment'></div>时之过也多绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364078_comment'></div>若夫遭主后之圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364078_comment'></div>属天地之贞观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364078_comment'></div>得畎亩之相保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364078_comment'></div>以农桑为业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364078_comment'></div>而托形宇宙者幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364078_comment'></div>况乃偃泊山水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364078_comment'></div>遨游风月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364078_comment'></div>樽酒于其外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364078_comment'></div>文墨于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364078_comment'></div>则造化之于我得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364078_comment'></div>太平之纵我多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364078_comment'></div>兹以上已芳节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364078_comment'></div>云开胜地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364078_comment'></div>大江<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364078", 1364078, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>浩旷</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364078_comment'></div>群山纷纠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364078_comment'></div>出重城而振策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364078_comment'></div>下长浦而方舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364078_comment'></div>林壑清其顾盼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364078_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364078", 1364078, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>风云</span>荡其怀抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364078_comment'></div>于时序躔清律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364078_comment'></div>运启朱明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364078_comment'></div>轻荑秀而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364078", 1364078, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>郊戍</span>青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364078_comment'></div>落花尽而亭皋晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364078_comment'></div>丹莺紫蝶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364078_comment'></div>候芳晷而腾姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364078_comment'></div>早燕归鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364078_comment'></div>俟迅风而弄影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364078_comment'></div>岩暄蕙密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364078_comment'></div>野淑兰滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364078_comment'></div>弱荷抽紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364078_comment'></div>疏萍泛绿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364078_comment'></div>于是俨松舲于石㠗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364078_comment'></div>停桂楫于璇潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364078_comment'></div>指林岸而长怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364078_comment'></div>出河州而极睇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364078_comment'></div>妍妆袨服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364078_comment'></div>香惊北渚之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364078_comment'></div>翠幕元帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364078_comment'></div>彩缀南津之雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364078_comment'></div>若乃寻曲渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364078_comment'></div>历回溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364078_comment'></div>榜讴齐引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364078_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364078", 1364078, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>渔歌</span>互起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364078_comment'></div>飞沙溅石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364078_comment'></div>湍流百势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364078_comment'></div>翠崄丹崖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364078_comment'></div>冈峦万色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364078_comment'></div>亦有银钩犯浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364078_comment'></div>挂赪翼于文竿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364078_comment'></div>琼舸乘波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364078_comment'></div>耀锦鳞于画网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364078_comment'></div>钟期在听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364078_comment'></div>元云白雪之琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364078_comment'></div>阮籍同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364078_comment'></div>紫桂苍梧之醴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364078_comment'></div>既而游盘兴远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364078_comment'></div>景促时淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364078_comment'></div>野日照晴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364078_comment'></div>山烟送晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364078_comment'></div>方披襟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1364078", 1364078, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>朗咏</span>。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364078_comment'></div>客怀既畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364078_comment'></div>游思遄征。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364078_comment'></div>初传曲路之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364078_comment'></div><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_72_1364078_comment'></div>盍遵清辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364078_comment'></div>共抒幽襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364078_comment'></div>俾后之视今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364078_comment'></div>亦犹今之视昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364078_comment'></div>一言均赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364078_comment'></div>六韵齐疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364078_comment'></div>谁知后来者难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364078_comment'></div>辄以先成为次。</div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1364078_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: -----title
中江（玄武）

1364098, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>道记</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364098_comment'></div>知轩冕可以理隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364098_comment'></div>鸾凰可以术待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364098_comment'></div>而事亲多衣食之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364098_comment'></div>登朝有声利之迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364098_comment'></div>清识滞于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364098", 1364098, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>烦城</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364098_comment'></div>仙骨摧于俗境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364098_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364098_comment'></div>阮籍意疏。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1364098_comment'></div>常恐运促风火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364098_comment'></div>身非金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364098_comment'></div>遂令林壑交丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364098_comment'></div>烟霞板荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364098_comment'></div>此仆所以怀泉涂而惴恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364098_comment'></div>相与游于元武西山庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364098_comment'></div>盖蜀郡三灵峰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364098_comment'></div>山东有道君庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364098_comment'></div>古者相传以名焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364098_comment'></div>其丹壑丛倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364098_comment'></div>元崖纠合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364098_comment'></div>俯临万仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364098_comment'></div>平视重元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364098_comment'></div>乘杳冥之绝境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364098_comment'></div>属<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364098_comment'></div>眇眇焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364098_comment'></div>逌逌焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364098_comment'></div>王孙何以不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364098_comment'></div>羽人何以长往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364098_comment'></div>其元都紫微之事耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364098_comment'></div>方敛手钟鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364098_comment'></div>息肩岩石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364098_comment'></div>绝视听于寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364098_comment'></div>置形骸于度外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364098_comment'></div>不其然乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364098_comment'></div>时预乎斯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364098_comment'></div>济阴鹿宏允安阳邵令远耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364098_comment'></div>盖诗以言志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364098_comment'></div>不以韵数裁焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1364098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在玄武,尚作有《游庙山赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷1第28页。）</span><div id='poem_1364035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游庙山赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364035")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364035_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364035'>元武山西有庙山。东有道君庙。盖幽人之别府也。长萝巨树。梢翳云日。王子御风而游。泠然而善。盖怀霄汉之举。而忘城阙之恋矣。思欲攀洪崖于烟道。邀羡门于天路。仙师不存。壮志徒尔。俄而泉石移景。秋阴方积。松柏群吟。背声四起。背乡关者。无复向时之荣焉。鸣乎。有其志。无其时。则知林泉有穷路之嗟。烟霞多后时之叹。不其悲乎。遂作赋曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364035'>陟彼山阿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364035_comment'></div>积石峨峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364035_comment'></div>亭皋千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364035_comment'></div>伤如之何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364035_comment'></div>启松崖之密荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364035_comment'></div>攀桂岊之崇柯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364035_comment'></div>隔浮埃于地络。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364035_comment'></div>披颢气于天罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364035_comment'></div>尔其绿岩分径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364035_comment'></div>苍岑对室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364035_comment'></div>菌轩丹绚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364035_comment'></div>蕙场翠密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364035_comment'></div>俯泉石之清泠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364035_comment'></div>临风飙之䫻瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364035_comment'></div>仰绀台而携手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364035_comment'></div>望元都而容膝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364035_comment'></div>于是蹑霞冈于玉砌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364035_comment'></div>步云岊于金坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364035_comment'></div>怀妙童与真女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364035_comment'></div>想青螭及碧鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364035_comment'></div>情恍恍而将逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364035_comment'></div>心回回而未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364035_comment'></div>见丹房之晚晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364035_comment'></div>忘紫洞之宵寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364035_comment'></div>既而雾昏千嶂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364035_comment'></div>烟浮四野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364035_comment'></div>恨流俗以情多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364035_comment'></div>痛飞仙之术寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364035_comment'></div>驱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364035", 1364035, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>逸思</span>于方外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364035_comment'></div>跼高情于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364035_comment'></div>使蓬瀛可得而宅焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364035_comment'></div>何必怀于此山也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364035_comment'></div>乱曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364035_comment'></div>已矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364035_comment'></div>吾谁欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364035_comment'></div>林壑逢地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364035_comment'></div>烟霞失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364035_comment'></div>托宇宙兮无日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364035_comment'></div>俟虬鸾兮未期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364035_comment'></div>他乡山水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364035_comment'></div>祇令人悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1364035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: href='/Writing/1364140?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梓州元武县福会寺碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364140")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364140_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364140'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364140'>若夫考龙图而括运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364140_comment'></div>抚麟笔以伤时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364140_comment'></div>天地闭而贤人隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364140_comment'></div>周孔逝而微言绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364140_comment'></div>岂非太阶无象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364140_comment'></div>三辰鲜逌叙之因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364140_comment'></div>沧海为陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364140_comment'></div>百川有横流之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364140_comment'></div>况乎法身长往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364140_comment'></div>顾糟粕以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364140_comment'></div>化迹繁流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364140_comment'></div>仰舟航而遂远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364140_comment'></div>虽复功推八正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364140_comment'></div>犹迷鹤树之谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364140_comment'></div>道亚三明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364140_comment'></div>未睹龙宫之籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364140_comment'></div>则有妙音难遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364140_comment'></div>瞻雪岭而投躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364140_comment'></div>真谛希声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364140_comment'></div>仰云山而破骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364140_comment'></div>优昙企景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364140_comment'></div>新雕白玉之龛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364140_comment'></div>般若寻风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364140_comment'></div>旧化黄金之像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364140_comment'></div>三千宝座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364140_comment'></div>迥出天宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364140_comment'></div>八万珍台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364140_comment'></div>遥临净域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364140_comment'></div>非慧图之冥感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364140_comment'></div>孰能臻于兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364140_comment'></div>福慧寺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364140_comment'></div>隋开皇中之所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364140_comment'></div>尔其峰峦雾列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364140_comment'></div>东分井络之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364140_comment'></div>楼雉云横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364140_comment'></div>西睹禺同之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364140_comment'></div>北弥丰邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364140_comment'></div>里闬千甍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364140_comment'></div>南控平江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364140_comment'></div>波潮万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364140_comment'></div>拥亭皋之绝势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364140_comment'></div>升林野之殊形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364140_comment'></div>肇开修竹之园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364140_comment'></div>式揆旃坛之刹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364140_comment'></div>法川<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364140", 1364140, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>高辟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364140_comment'></div>慈宫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1364140", 1364140, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>峻敞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364140_comment'></div>文珰宝缀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364140_comment'></div>环日月于重廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364140_comment'></div>翠栱丹楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364140_comment'></div>起虹蜺于复殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364140_comment'></div>真容俯映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364140_comment'></div>福众爰依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364140_comment'></div>梵筵交烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364140_comment'></div>禅房互启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364140_comment'></div>山神献果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364140_comment'></div>还栖承露之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364140_comment'></div>天女持香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364140_comment'></div>即绕飞花之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364140_comment'></div>轮辉夜满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364140_comment'></div>抽紫焰于金山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364140_comment'></div>毫相晨临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364140_comment'></div>发珠华于玉地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364140_comment'></div>爰有县令柳边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364140_comment'></div>河东<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1364140", 1364140, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>令族</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364140_comment'></div>大业之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364140_comment'></div>来光上邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364140_comment'></div>高人捧檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364140_comment'></div>功为铜墨之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364140_comment'></div>令宰鸣琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364140_comment'></div>课称弦歌之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364140_comment'></div>眷香城而恻念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364140_comment'></div>披道肆而惊魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364140_comment'></div>示怀延奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364140_comment'></div>思宏末教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364140_comment'></div>乃于寺内起重阁一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364140_comment'></div>乘烟置臬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364140_comment'></div>揆日端绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364140_comment'></div>层榭三休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364140_comment'></div>雕檐四注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364140_comment'></div>奔星挂庑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364140_comment'></div>混珠网而同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364140_comment'></div>明月窥轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364140_comment'></div>杂璿珰而共贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364140_comment'></div>仍抽丽笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364140_comment'></div>俯刊贞炎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364140_comment'></div>词源迅委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364140_comment'></div>振<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_86_1364140", 1364140, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>法海</span>之波澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364140_comment'></div>义宇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1364140", 1364140, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>宏深</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364140_comment'></div>接禅宫之阃奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364140_comment'></div>昔者陶潜彭泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364140_comment'></div>罔闻仁慈之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364140_comment'></div>潘岳河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364140_comment'></div>未入菩提之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364140_comment'></div>兼其美者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364140_comment'></div>盖在我柳君乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364140_comment'></div>俄而帝隋方否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364140_comment'></div>三官失龙凤之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364140_comment'></div>皇业未昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364140_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1364140", 1364140, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>九野</span>被豺狼之毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364140_comment'></div>虽复餐砂茹石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364140_comment'></div>窥剑道而回心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364140_comment'></div>蜂聚枭腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364140_comment'></div>指铜梁而革面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364140_comment'></div>自非法云西眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364140_comment'></div>潜消火宅之氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364140_comment'></div>慧日东来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364140_comment'></div>迥朗昏衢之景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364140_comment'></div>则安能冥资福地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364140_comment'></div>显阻魔军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364140_comment'></div>波清于振壑之隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364140_comment'></div>燎息于炎昆之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364140_comment'></div>洎乎大钧无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364140_comment'></div>神器有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364140_comment'></div>清玉户而帝寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364140_comment'></div>转金轮而王天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364140_comment'></div>元场佛境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364140_comment'></div>与天下而惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364140_comment'></div>莺树鸡林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364140_comment'></div>共风云而改旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364140_comment'></div>功既成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364140_comment'></div>时既贞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364140_comment'></div>紫宸有裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364140_comment'></div>苍氓胥悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364140_comment'></div>都人狎至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364140_comment'></div>瞻雁塔而欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364140_comment'></div>野老相趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364140_comment'></div>寻鹿园而顿颡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364140_comment'></div>或至诚冥发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364140_comment'></div>争知不尽之虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364140_comment'></div>或道思旁流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364140_comment'></div>竟委忘缘之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364140_comment'></div>乃于寺内造菩提塑像一座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364140_comment'></div>实彭氏绝群之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364140_comment'></div>洞参<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_133_1364140", 1364140, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>瑶铣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364140_comment'></div>体备丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364140_comment'></div>得埏范之奇模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364140_comment'></div>尽陶甄之能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364140_comment'></div>功分实相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364140_comment'></div>变入冥机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364140_comment'></div>丹果长春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364140_comment'></div>青莲不染。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364140_comment'></div>灵仪若动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364140_comment'></div>似临王舍城中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364140_comment'></div>神足疑行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364140_comment'></div>即坐菩提树下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364140_comment'></div>银床地涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364140_comment'></div>宝帐犹悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364140_comment'></div>珍木天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364140_comment'></div>金花不落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364140_comment'></div>总章元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364140_comment'></div>又奉为皇帝更造八菩萨像。<div class='inline'
