class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1364140_comment'></div>松桂连华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1364140_comment'></div>鸳鸾集彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1364140_comment'></div>禅津有裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1364140_comment'></div>至公无待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1364140_comment'></div>火宅可辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1364140_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_370_1364140'>舟航斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1364140_comment'></div>我之飘寓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1364140_comment'></div>邈矣来游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_372_1364140_comment'></div>山川俯仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_373_1364140_comment'></div>道义淹留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_374_1364140_comment'></div>承风郭外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_375_1364140_comment'></div>撰缀江幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_376_1364140_comment'></div>元机胜笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_377_1364140_comment'></div>天地相周。</div><div id='poem_sentence_378_1364140_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在玄武,尚作有《梓州飞乌县白鹤寺碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷16第474页。）</span><div id='poem_1364137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364137?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梓州飞乌县白鹤寺碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364137")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364137'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364137'>原夫玉都琼室。紫垣光大帝之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364137_comment'></div>金阙银台。元壁壮群仙之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364137_comment'></div>故能使神明有宅。驾日月以长驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364137_comment'></div>鸾凤知归。抚云霓而上出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364137_comment'></div>斯则层巢墐穴。上皇迷栋宇之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364137_comment'></div>考室灵台。中古识岩廊之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364137_comment'></div>然后冕旒前序。提四海以为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364137_comment'></div>登步太阶。列千门而有闶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364137_comment'></div>况乎耆山形见。旁行草昧之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364137_comment'></div>□光宅乾坤之右。虽鹤临西閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364137_comment'></div>龙宫与正法同亡。而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364137", 1364137, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>象化</span>东流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364137_comment'></div>雁塔与遗仪继起。白鹤寺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364137_comment'></div>盖菩提寺之馀址。梁武皇之所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364137_comment'></div>香城福地之旧。三巴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364137", 1364137, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>五蜀</span>之凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364137_comment'></div>裂岷山之奥域。分井络之荣光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364137_comment'></div>西包玉垒之墟。北瞰铜陵之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364137_comment'></div>南扃列第。门庭万家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364137_comment'></div>东户连峰。冈峦千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364137_comment'></div>实伽蓝之胜迹。得迦卫之英模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364137_comment'></div>凭绝磴以图规。俯长溪而作固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364137_comment'></div>自金陵不竞。玉镜无章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364137_comment'></div>城池兴南路之悲。亭障切北风之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364137_comment'></div>崩山斗水。触地网而三分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364137_comment'></div>坠月奔星。划乾纲而五裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364137_comment'></div>中原错戾。慈门为虎豹之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364137_comment'></div>沧海横流。定水穴鲸鲵之浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364137_comment'></div>怀山既荡。法众咸沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364137_comment'></div>林院<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364137", 1364137, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>榛芜</span>。轩堂委寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364137_comment'></div>遂使悲生弃井。堙玉甃于三泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364137_comment'></div>叹积为山。移琼峰于九仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364137_comment'></div>皇上摄千秋之宝运。绪三圣之宏机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364137_comment'></div>挟宇宙而先神。御雷风而首出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364137_comment'></div>灵功不宰。华夷沾共贯之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364137_comment'></div>至道无私。霜露得平分之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364137_comment'></div>考祯图于日慎。寤寐同符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364137_comment'></div>稽妙册于年刀。幽明合贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364137_comment'></div>然后东巡巨镇。追六圣而抚寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364137_comment'></div>南面太坛。朝万方而小天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364137_comment'></div>皇威既畅。宝应齐归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364137_comment'></div>川岳荐灵。风烟动庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364137_comment'></div>丹乌抱日。疑增<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364137", 1364137, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>帝阁</span>之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364137_comment'></div>素鹤低云。若赴仙庭之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364137_comment'></div>昔白鱼黄竹。业未峻于崇封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364137_comment'></div>赤雁芝房。名不登于梵宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364137_comment'></div>爰徵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364137", 1364137, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>瑞典</span>。肇锡嘉名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364137_comment'></div>重兴般若之台。更起招提之院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364137_comment'></div>金绳夕布。绵秀岭以开坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364137_comment'></div>玉榜晨舒。拥回峰而辟户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364137_comment'></div>爰有宏演上人者。法门之秀士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364137_comment'></div>行超常冻。思越恒饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364137_comment'></div>悲净域之为墟。喜皇波之普泛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364137_comment'></div>纵还舟于苦海。惊浪旋夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364137_comment'></div>叱归驭于邪山。灵关非险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364137_comment'></div>于是净财云委。真众烟驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364137_comment'></div>如趋摩竭之宫。似向毗邪之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364137_comment'></div>县令梁宏悦。首加甄缉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364137_comment'></div>县丞梁敬一。亲昭施典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364137_comment'></div>上凭天旨。争开舍利之坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364137_comment'></div>俯会众心。竞起须弥之座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364137_comment'></div>禺同故岭。石鲜坚华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364137_comment'></div>广汉馀坰。地多疏斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364137_comment'></div>事关经始。人怀祗惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364137_comment'></div>重阶不就。空思太室之氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364137_comment'></div>宝像无资。未获黎阳之土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364137_comment'></div>岂非冥期肸蚃。功参造化之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364137_comment'></div>故能果唇间发。莲眸周映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364137_comment'></div>贝齿含滋。璿毫起照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364137_comment'></div>三十二相。临玉座以相辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364137_comment'></div>八十四仪。拥金山而圆立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364137_comment'></div>层甍四合。烁奔电于丹楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364137_comment'></div>复殿三休。络浮烟于翠幌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364137_comment'></div>因高积磴。疑迁倒景之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364137_comment'></div>架险连荣。似立迎风之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364137_comment'></div>雕檐竞注。萦雾道以龙回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364137_comment'></div>绣桷争飞。傃云衢而凤矫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364137_comment'></div>写归禽于宝镜。误接朝鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364137_comment'></div>图走兽于文珰。疑栖夕免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364137_comment'></div>雷霆蓄泄。裁临承霤之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364137_comment'></div>烟雨飞浮。未出层栾之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364137_comment'></div>辉丹青于菌壁。妙迹疑存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364137_comment'></div>炳铣鋈于莲龛。神辉自烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364137_comment'></div>锵锵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1364137", 1364137, "Clauses/162/Comments/0")'>櫩铎</span>。声传<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1364137", 1364137, "Clauses/163/Comments/0")'>桂叶</span>之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364137_comment'></div>焰焰山炉。气结松阴之霭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364137_comment'></div>仰真容于始旦。满月晨昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364137_comment'></div>窥列栋于方宵。长虹夜发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364137_comment'></div>香泉激溜。有符温净之池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364137_comment'></div>珍木成行。无忝祇园之树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364137_comment'></div>信煦尼之别府。实兜率之殊庭者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364137_comment'></div>爱友上座法师等。情机藻莹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364137_comment'></div>戒律圆明。披玉笥以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1364137", 1364137, "Clauses/179/Comments/0")'>研芳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364137_comment'></div>候琼钟而肃虑。禅姿晓映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364137_comment'></div>依稀同鸡岫之前。梵呗晨临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364137_comment'></div>髣髴像鱼山之曲。县令独孤俭等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364137_comment'></div>或鹏垂待运。终燮道于中台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364137_comment'></div>或蠖屈求伸。且毗风于下邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364137_comment'></div>乡望仪曹等。或盐泉锦室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364137_comment'></div>家称三蜀之豪。或抱朴怀仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364137_comment'></div>誉拥双流之美。或以为山川肆践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364137_comment'></div>犹纪石于弇州。陵谷生哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364137_comment'></div>尚沈碑于岘首。况乎德因时盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364137_comment'></div>庆流封拜之辰。名为功登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364137_comment'></div>事属文明之运。岂可使璿猷被物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364137_comment'></div>终昧燮于元机。金字韬华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364137_comment'></div>不题勋于翠炎。敢作颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364137_comment'></div>睿涂菌蔼。灵机翕忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364137_comment'></div>玉架天都。金裁地阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364137_comment'></div>法王利见。香城继发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364137_comment'></div>雁塔齐云。龙宫瘗月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364137_comment'></div>长江近域。广汉遗居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364137_comment'></div>禅扃共往。梵宇全疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364137_comment'></div>迹均梁后。义切秦馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364137_comment'></div>山川牢落。榛莽邱墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364137_comment'></div>有圣聿兴。惟皇降抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364137_comment'></div>因天因地。为云为雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364137_comment'></div>日观龙骧。烟坛鹤举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364137_comment'></div>肇开嘉号。重光净土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364137_comment'></div>猗欤上士。道场真政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364137_comment'></div>物观成章。子来兴咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364137_comment'></div>土石呈彩。人灵合庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364137_comment'></div>宝座晨严。金山夕映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364137_comment'></div>紫微分殿。青岑曜郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364137_comment'></div>复袖萦楼。攒峰跨阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364137_comment'></div>月低璿镜。星连宝铎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364137_comment'></div>彩凤将飞。蟠虹未落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364137_comment'></div>森沈桂宇。肃穆筠坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364137_comment'></div>花明柳砌。叶暗朱栏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364137_comment'></div>溪留夏雪。涧咽秋湍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364137_comment'></div>山虚梵冷。谷静钟寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364137_comment'></div>法众爰依。禅徒戾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364137_comment'></div>望风三蜀。征尘千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364137_comment'></div>顿首元墀。归心翠扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364137_comment'></div>业超有色。功齐无始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364137_comment'></div>伟哉冥化。妙矣能仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364137_comment'></div>去来均迹。前后俱身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364137_comment'></div>寂灭为乐。般若为因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364137_comment'></div>题芳翠珉。敢诣灵津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364137_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_136_1364137_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='971a6b63adaf4daead616d2b113f215a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("971a6b63adaf4daead616d2b113f215a");'><span id='971a6b63adaf4daead616d2b113f215a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>，21岁</div><div id='971a6b63adaf4daead616d2b113f215a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春,往来梓州、玄武间,作《圣泉宴并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第78页。）</span><div id='poem_8814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圣泉宴</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8814")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8814_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_8814'>玄武山有圣泉焉，浸淫历数百千年，垂岩沁涌，接磴分流，下瞰长江，沙堤石岸，咸古人遗迹也。兹乃青蘋绿芰，紫苔苍藓，遂使江湖思远，寤寐寄托。既而崇峦左峙，石壑（一作「壁」）前萦，丹崿万寻，碧潭千顷，松风唱响，竹露熏空。潇潇乎人间之难遇也，方欲以林壑为天属，琴樽为日用。嗟乎！古今同逝（一作「代谢」。）方深川上之悲；少长偕游，且尽山阴之乐。盍题芳什，共写高情。诗得泉字。诗曰：（《古今图书集成坤舆典》三六《泉部》）</div><div id='poem_preface_8814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8814'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8814'>披襟乘石磴，列籍<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作席）</span>俯春泉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8814'>兰气熏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8814", 8814, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>山酌</span>，松声韵野弦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8814'>影飘垂叶外，香度落花前。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8814'>兴洽林塘晚，重岩起夕烟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8814'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_8814'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(8814)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春,往来梓州、玄武间,作《唐故度支员外郎达奚公墓志并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版第644页。）</span><br /></div>
-----end

金堂

-----title
广汉（雒县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6a8065db480e46aaa34e230c1325cdb8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6a8065db480e46aaa34e230c1325cdb8");'><span id='6a8065db480e46aaa34e230c1325cdb8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>，21岁</div><div id='6a8065db480e46aaa34e230c1325cdb8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　居汉州山间,作《慈竹赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷2第38页。）</span><div id='poem_1364041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慈竹赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364041")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364041_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364041'>广汉山谷。有竹名慈。生必向内。示不离本。修茎巨叶。攒根沓柢。丛之大者。或至百千株焉。而萦结踰乎咫步。好事君子。徙为阶庭之玩焉。吁嗟非此土所有。乃有厌流俗之讥。动乡关之思者。盖抚高节而兴叹。览嘉名而思归。遂为赋曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364041'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364041'>有竹猗猗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364041_comment'></div>生于高陂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364041_comment'></div>左连瑶带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364041_comment'></div>右杂琼枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364041_comment'></div>恨幽客之方赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364041_comment'></div>嗟君侯之不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364041_comment'></div>徙蔚丹谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364041_comment'></div>迁荣绿池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364041_comment'></div>气<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364041", 1364041, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>凛凛</span>而犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364041_comment'></div>色苍苍而未离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364041_comment'></div>屈岩壑之容貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364041_comment'></div>充阶庭之羽仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364041_comment'></div>尔其画疆分域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364041_comment'></div>骈阴抗趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364041_comment'></div>謺干龙回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364041_comment'></div>攒根凤峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364041_comment'></div>防<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364041", 1364041, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>碧露</span>于霄末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364041_comment'></div>翳红光于晕始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364041_comment'></div>崇柯振而云霭生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364041_comment'></div>繁叶动而风飙起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364041_comment'></div>拥凉砌之晨肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364041_comment'></div>屏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364041", 1364041, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>炎扃</span>之昼滓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364041_comment'></div>至若白藏载谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364041_comment'></div>元英肇切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364041_comment'></div>塞北河坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364041_comment'></div>关南地裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364041_comment'></div>观众茂之咸悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364041_comment'></div>验贞辉之独洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364041_comment'></div>抽劲绿以垂霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364041_comment'></div>总严青而负雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364041_comment'></div>盖同类之常禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364041_comment'></div>非殊方之异节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364041_comment'></div>若乃宗生族茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364041_comment'></div>天长地久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364041_comment'></div>万柢争盘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364041_comment'></div>千株竞纠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364041_comment'></div>如母子之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364041", 1364041, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>钩带</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364041_comment'></div>似闺门之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364041", 1364041, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>悌友</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364041_comment'></div>恐孤秀而成危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364041_comment'></div>每群居而自守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364041_comment'></div>何美名之天属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364041_comment'></div>而和气之冥受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364041_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364041_comment'></div>道之存矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364041_comment'></div>物亦有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364041_comment'></div>不背仁以贪地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364041_comment'></div>不藏节以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1364041", 1364041, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>遁时</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364041_comment'></div>故其贞不自炫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364041_comment'></div>用不见疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364041_comment'></div>保夷险之无易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364041_comment'></div>哂荣枯之有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364041_comment'></div>俄蓬转于岷徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364041_comment'></div>遂萍流于江汜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364041_comment'></div>分兄弟于两乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364041_comment'></div>隔晨昏于万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364041_comment'></div>抚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1364041", 1364041, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>贞容</span>而骨愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364041_comment'></div>伏嘉号而心死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364041_comment'></div>庶因感而长怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364041_comment'></div>将策情而励已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1364041_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
德阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3eb677f27e694bc081d23038cebefaa0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3eb677f27e694bc081d23038cebefaa0");'><span id='3eb677f27e694bc081d23038cebefaa0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>，21岁</div><div id='3eb677f27e694bc081d23038cebefaa0' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋,在德阳（今属四川）,县令宇文峤设宴款待,作《宇文德阳宅秋夜山亭宴序》,预宴者尚有中山郎馀令。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷7第219页。德阳时属益州,谭图标在汉州,张谱已言系垂拱二年后改。）</span><div id='poem_1364095' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364095' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364095?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宇文德阳宅秋夜山亭宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364095")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364095_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364095'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364095'>若夫龙津宴喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364095_comment'></div>地切登仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364095_comment'></div>凤阁元虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364095_comment'></div>门称好事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364095_comment'></div>亦有登山临水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364095_comment'></div>长想巨源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364095_comment'></div>明月清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364095_comment'></div>每思元度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364095_comment'></div>未有能星驰一介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364095_comment'></div>留美迹于芳亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364095_comment'></div>云委<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364095", 1364095, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>八行</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364095_comment'></div>抒劳思于彩笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364095_comment'></div>遂令启<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364095", 1364095, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>瑶缄</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364095_comment'></div>攀胜集而长怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364095_comment'></div>披<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364095", 1364095, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>琼翰</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364095_comment'></div>仰高筵而不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364095_comment'></div>王子猷之独兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364095_comment'></div>不觉浮舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364095_comment'></div>嵇叔夜之相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364095_comment'></div>欣然命驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364095_comment'></div>琴樽佳赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364095_comment'></div>始诣临邛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364095_comment'></div>口腹良游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364095_comment'></div>未辞安邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364095_comment'></div>乃知两乡投分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364095_comment'></div>林泉可攘袂而游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364095_comment'></div>千里同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364095_comment'></div>烟霞可传檄而定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364095_comment'></div>友人河南宇文峤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364095_comment'></div>清虚君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364095_comment'></div>中山郎馀令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364095_comment'></div>风流名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364095_comment'></div>或三秋意契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364095_comment'></div>辟林院而开襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364095_comment'></div>或一面新交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364095_comment'></div>叙风云而倒屣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364095_comment'></div>彭泽陶潜之菊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364095_comment'></div>影泛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364095", 1364095, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>仙樽</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364095_comment'></div>河阳潘岳之花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364095_comment'></div>光悬妙理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364095_comment'></div>岩岩思壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364095_comment'></div>家藏虹岫之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364095_comment'></div>淼淼言河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364095_comment'></div>各探骊泉之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364095_comment'></div>偶同金碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364095_comment'></div>暂照词场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364095_comment'></div>巴汉英灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364095_comment'></div>潜光<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1364095", 1364095, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>翰院</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364095_comment'></div>亹亹焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364095_comment'></div>萧萧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364095_comment'></div>信天下之奇托也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364095_comment'></div>于时白藏开序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364095_comment'></div>青女御律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364095_comment'></div>金风高而林野动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364095_comment'></div>玉露下而江山清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364095_comment'></div>琴亭酒榭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364095_comment'></div>磊落乘烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364095_comment'></div>竹径松扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364095_comment'></div>参差向月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364095_comment'></div>鱼鳞积磴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364095_comment'></div>还升兰桂之峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364095_comment'></div>鸳翼分桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364095_comment'></div>即映芙蓉之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364095_comment'></div>亦有红蘋绿荇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364095_comment'></div>亘渚连翘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364095_comment'></div>玉带瑶华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364095_comment'></div>分楹间植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364095_comment'></div>池帘夕敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364095_comment'></div>香牵十步之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364095_comment'></div>岫幌宵褰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364095_comment'></div>气袭三危之露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364095_comment'></div>纵冲衿于俗表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364095_comment'></div>留<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364095", 1364095, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>逸契</span>于人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364095_comment'></div>东山之赏在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364095_comment'></div>南涧之情不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364095_comment'></div>夫以中牟驯雉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364095_comment'></div>犹婴触网之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364095_comment'></div>单父歌鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364095_comment'></div>罕继鸣琴之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364095_comment'></div>俾夫一同诗酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364095_comment'></div>不挠于牵丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364095_comment'></div>千载岩溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364095_comment'></div>无惭于景烛云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1364095_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋,在德阳（今属四川）,为宇文峤饯行,作《饯宇文明府序》.预饯宴者,尚有薛曜等人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷8第254页。《王子安集注》作《送宇文明府序》）</span><div id='poem_1364089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饯宇文明府序</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364089")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364089'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364089'>昔者王烈登山。林泉动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364089_comment'></div>嵇康入座。左右生光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364089_comment'></div>岂非仙表足以感神。真姿可以错物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364089_comment'></div>况我巨山之禀孤出。升华之丽清峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364089_comment'></div>群公之好善。下官之恶俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364089_comment'></div>接霓裳于胜席。陪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364089", 1364089, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>鹤辔</span>于中轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364089_comment'></div>俱持拔尘之标。各仗专门之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364089_comment'></div>烟霞用足。江海情多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364089_comment'></div>言泉共秋水同流。词峰与夏云争长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364089_comment'></div>虽扬亭载酒。方趋好事之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364089_comment'></div>而乐肆含毫。请命升仙之笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364089_comment'></div>同抽藻思。共写离怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364089_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1364089_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>应德阳县令宇文峤之请,作《益州德阳县善寂寺碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷17第487页。）</span><div id='poem_1364133' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364133' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364133?labeling=true' target='_blank'>益州德阳县善寂寺碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364133")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364133_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364133'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364133'>若夫玉绳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>高曜</span>。分宝历于皇阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364133_comment'></div>金榜洞开。导<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>瑸晖</span>于帝幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364133_comment'></div>虽复苍梧北望。湖湘盈舜后之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364133_comment'></div>绿荇西浮。江汉积文妃之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364133_comment'></div>未有激扬烦荫。栖妙果于香城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364133_comment'></div>挥发盖缠。树冥基于净域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364133_comment'></div>则紫房<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>丹室</span>。犹居燬室之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364133_comment'></div>朱绂瑶筐。未出尘笼之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364133_comment'></div>我国家凤翔元气。驾黄幄而层飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364133_comment'></div>龙跃太虚。绝苍根而止傃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364133_comment'></div>文皇帝以八才御宇。光升岱野之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364133_comment'></div>文德后以十乱乘时。恭赞涂山之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364133_comment'></div>握<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>仁王</span>之宝镜。日月重光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364133_comment'></div>驱梵帝之金轮。雷霆静祲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364133_comment'></div>涅槃甘露。承眷而宵流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364133_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>般若</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/30/Comments/1")'>灵音</span>。杂祥以昼引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364133_comment'></div>蛟台蜃阁。俄交<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>震旦</span>之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364133_comment'></div>月面星毫。坐照毗邪之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364133_comment'></div>善寂者。盖旧寺之馀趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364133_comment'></div>梁武帝之所建也。尔其碧鸡仙宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364133_comment'></div>分绝障于金堤。石兔遥源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364133_comment'></div>控长江于玉峡。封畿四会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364133_comment'></div>龙坰舍卫之坛。里闬三分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364133_comment'></div>鹿野经行之地。洎苍鹅上击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364133_comment'></div>铜马交驰。祗园兴板荡之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364133_comment'></div>沙界积沦胥之痛。火炎昆岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364133_comment'></div>高台与雁塔同平。水浸天街。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364133_comment'></div>曲岸与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>猴池</span>共尽。山川隐嶙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364133_comment'></div>空传鹫岭之基。灌莽萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364133_comment'></div>非复莺林之树。武德伊始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364133_comment'></div>君子道亨。正皇极而抚寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364133_comment'></div>登太阶而临天下。函关云物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364133_comment'></div>更逢真圣之期。井络星辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364133_comment'></div>重集会昌之运。虽开基拨乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364133_comment'></div>狱讼知归。而继绝兴亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364133_comment'></div>经纶未暇。先皇统业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364133_comment'></div>贞观御宸。奉文物于三天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364133_comment'></div>布声名于十地。参罗上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364133_comment'></div>充橐籥于襟怀。八部神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364133_comment'></div>荐图书于掌握。皇宝降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364133_comment'></div>地符升。含生无昏垫之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364133_comment'></div>法众有来苏之望。俄而后庭搆厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364133_comment'></div>椒房穆卜。六宫震恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364133_comment'></div>三灵愕眙。驰瑶展币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364133_comment'></div>有事于群宗。碧剂元针。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364133_comment'></div>无徵于众术。帝乃降监回虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364133_comment'></div>屏璧与圭。追胜迹于灵关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364133_comment'></div>事良缘于福地。爰纡圣綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364133_comment'></div>重启禅宫。峙璇刹于将倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364133_comment'></div>镇银绳于巳绝。丝纶既洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364133_comment'></div>栋宇行周。坤德用宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364133_comment'></div>阴仪载朗。于是林衡授矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364133_comment'></div>周官诠揆日之工。梓匠挥斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364133_comment'></div>荆客鍊成风之巧。重楹画栱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364133_comment'></div>坐出天霄。复树文闺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364133_comment'></div>俛临霓宇。显庆中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364133_comment'></div>县令萧君道宏。理<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>钩绳</span>于日用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364133_comment'></div>凭藻缋于天成。仙宫之妙匠可寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364133_comment'></div>卢舍之神模不坠。雕甍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/117/Comments/0")'>鹤翥</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364133_comment'></div>曳珠网于星津。绣桷虬伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364133_comment'></div>吐璿珰于月径。绿房丹锁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364133_comment'></div>彩缀晴霞。紫阁青疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364133_comment'></div>光含薄雾。春风琼树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364133_comment'></div>香飘席上之兰。秋水银塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364133_comment'></div>影数轩中之芰。晨光转卉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364133_comment'></div>翻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>宝宇</span>之龙花。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>溽露</span>低枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364133_comment'></div>荡真文于贝叶。天童润色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364133_comment'></div>黄珉碧玉之坛。海圣弥缝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364133_comment'></div>师子龙王之会。建<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>灵幢</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/137/Comments/1")'>厚夜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364133_comment'></div>珠饰年深。悬法鼓于迷津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364133_comment'></div>规模岁远。时又于佛堂东壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364133_comment'></div>画二圣僧。丹青未毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364133_comment'></div>大启神光。邻玉尘之崇辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364133_comment'></div>发金龛之实相。朱轩夕朗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364133_comment'></div>似游明月之宫。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/149/Comments/0")'>绀宇</span>晨融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364133_comment'></div>若对流霞之阙。由是岷英蜀秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364133_comment'></div>攀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>讲序</span>以云趋。带燕裙鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364133_comment'></div>仰齐庭而雾合。贪机大阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364133_comment'></div>净施旁流。绮罗分解佩之因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364133_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>轩盖</span>得捐金之所。灵妃翳日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364133_comment'></div>舍翠幄于香筵。仙客停云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364133_comment'></div>落霓裳于宝地。自非冲姿密契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364133_comment'></div>景应潜周。岂能昭义祉于氤氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364133_comment'></div>动元机于肸蚃者也。爰有上座宏一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364133_comment'></div>节并沈研。性符隐括。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364133_comment'></div>凝妙律于神珠。肃灵椒于宝印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364133_comment'></div>大昊奉楫。截苦海而横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364133_comment'></div>风伯扶轮。历邪山而效驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364133_comment'></div>腾烛龙于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_88_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/176/Comments/0")'>慧炬</span>。俯镜重昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364133_comment'></div>奏鸣凤于天歌。下清群籁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364133_comment'></div>摩珍在握。遥临七宝之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364133_comment'></div>正觉为心。俯辟三乘之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364133_comment'></div>湛衢樽于忍地。品藻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/185/Comments/0")'>鸡园</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364133_comment'></div>推水砥于言河。扶持象化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364133_comment'></div>县令宇文某。河南人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364133_comment'></div>帝隋尚书之元孙。皇唐侍中之令子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364133_comment'></div>尔其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_96_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/192/Comments/0")'>虹旗</span>万里。御六气而鹏飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364133_comment'></div>霜戟千群。拥三州而鹗视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364133_comment'></div>帝叶皇枝之重。对越乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364133_comment'></div>金縢石匮之功。光华宇宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364133_comment'></div>公上流提庆。中和毓祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364133_comment'></div>见钟鼎于南邻。奉轩裳于北阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364133_comment'></div>云姿月步。下瑶泽而追风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364133_comment'></div>雪羽霞翎。丽珠田而矫雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364133_comment'></div>芳兰公子。即以地业高人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364133_comment'></div>幽桂王孙。即以琴樽待物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364133_comment'></div>叙徽猷于礼乐。则俎豆纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364133_comment'></div>谈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/214/Comments/0")'>赏契</span>于林泉。则烟霞咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364133_comment'></div>自裁声百里。揆化双川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364133_comment'></div>收武城之故事。择中牟之令典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364133_comment'></div>仁风易狎。候丹翟于春坰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364133_comment'></div>惠化难经。伫青鸾于晓队。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364133_comment'></div>山巨源之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/224/Comments/0")'>远量</span>。啸傲行藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364133_comment'></div>谢太傅之高风。从容语默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364133_comment'></div>县丞王敬。衣簪旧族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364133_comment'></div>孝友名家。白虹缄抵鹊之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364133_comment'></div>紫电蓄冲牛之气。七年<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_116_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/233/Comments/0")'>高秀</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364133_comment'></div>拂层汉以非遥。六月雄图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364133_comment'></div>击长波而未远。乡望等少承荣绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364133_comment'></div>中区胜族。门称东别之标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364133_comment'></div>地接西隅之向。严君平之履道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364133_comment'></div>盛德家传。秦子整之谈天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364133_comment'></div>风流代袭。咸以为妙图真谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364133_comment'></div>事出于无名。翠玉元碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364133_comment'></div>道凝于不朽。弇州北跨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364133_comment'></div>犹疏騄骥之名。文石东区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364133_comment'></div>尚勒元龟之颂。况乎玉衣流庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364133_comment'></div>事属于仙帏。金屋延祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364133_comment'></div>福缠于梵宇。爰求胜笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364133_comment'></div>载记芳谣。下官弱植少徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364133_comment'></div>薄游多暇。薜萝人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364133_comment'></div>空馀江海之心。笔札神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364133_comment'></div>尚有渊云之气。相如谢病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364133_comment'></div>访诗酒于临邛。邱也栖迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364133_comment'></div>听弦歌于单父。群公以道之存矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364133_comment'></div>思传记德之书。下官以文在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364133_comment'></div>愿展<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_136_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/272/Comments/0")'>当仁</span>之笔。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364133_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_137_1364133'>蜀岭东渐。岷山西积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364133_comment'></div>月峡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_138_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/276/Comments/0")'>星桥</span>。腾金孕碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364133_comment'></div>肸蚃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_139_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/278/Comments/0")'>灵兆</span>。邱墟梵迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364133_comment'></div>雁塔推基。鹿苑遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364133_comment'></div>肃肃黄运。英英文母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364133_comment'></div>配乾垂庆。仪坤握矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364133_comment'></div>宠照香城。仁沾净土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364133_comment'></div>爰光大壮。聿求多祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364133_comment'></div>青牛福地。白鹤禅林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364133_comment'></div>重扃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/292/Comments/0")'>雾敞</span>。复殿云深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364133_comment'></div>龛雕翠玉。刹树黄金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364133_comment'></div>龟镜夕照。凤铎晨吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364133_comment'></div>慧楼弥望。化台出没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364133_comment'></div>栋列长虹。窗虚明月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364133_comment'></div>果唇周映。莲眸间发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364133_comment'></div>雨霁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_152_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/304/Comments/0")'>猴池</span>。烟生龙窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364133_comment'></div>肃穆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_153_1364133", 1364133, "Clauses/306/Comments/0")'>禅众</span>。优游令宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364133_comment'></div>方驾康衢。连舟性海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364133_comment'></div>鹫岭增饰。鸡林润彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364133_comment'></div>藻绘相寻。丹青尽在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364133_comment'></div>我今怀矣。穷路何歧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364133_comment'></div>承风咏德。展义陈词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364133_comment'></div>百年心事。千载风期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364133_comment'></div>东西南北。栖遑几时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364133_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_161_1364133_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
什邡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5602b0a4acad4b569f919dc57d1240ec_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5602b0a4acad4b569f919dc57d1240ec");'><span id='5602b0a4acad4b569f919dc57d1240ec_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>，21岁</div><div id='5602b0a4acad4b569f919dc57d1240ec' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　秋晚,在什邡西池与九陇县令柳明（字太易）宴,作《秋晚什邡西池宴九陇柳明府序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版第634页。什邡时属益州,谭图标在汉州,张谱已言系垂拱二年后改。）</span><br /></div>

-----title
成都
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fb89f46aba0b45d787161eff52df3c75_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fb89f46aba0b45d787161eff52df3c75");'><span id='fb89f46aba0b45d787161eff52df3c75_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>，21岁</div><div id='fb89f46aba0b45d787161eff52df3c75' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　晚秋时节,与益州大都督府群官共游武担山,作《晚秋游武担山寺序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷7第212页。）</span><div id='poem_1364096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364096' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364096?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚秋游武担山寺序</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364096")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364096_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364096'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364096'>若夫武邱<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364096_comment'></div>下贲穷泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364096_comment'></div>而广岫长林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364096_comment'></div>终成胜境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364096_comment'></div>亦有霍将军之大隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364096_comment'></div>回写祁连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364096_comment'></div>樗里子之孤坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364096_comment'></div>竟开长乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364096_comment'></div>开明故地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364096_comment'></div>蜀夫人之葬迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364096_comment'></div>任文公之死所。<div id='poem_content_8786'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8786'>霜华净天末，雾色笼江际。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
