id='poem_sentence_2_8786_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　秋,作《为人与蜀城父老书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷6第176页;第183页。此书有两篇。）</span><div id='poem_1364052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人与蜀城父老书</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364052")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364052'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364052'>盖闻天地作极。不能迁否泰之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364052_comment'></div>川岳荐灵。不能改穷通之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364052_comment'></div>岂非圣贤同业。存乎我者所谓才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364052_comment'></div>荣辱异流。牵乎彼者所谓命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364052_comment'></div>是以龙骧凤峙。伊周成翊赞之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364052_comment'></div>含糗羹藜。颜冉困栖迟之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364052_comment'></div>或先号而后笑。或始吉而终凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364052_comment'></div>事不可量。功未必定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364052_comment'></div>则知洪涛未接。长鲸多陆死之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364052_comment'></div>层风未翔。大鹏有云倾之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364052_comment'></div>池䲡井鲋。亦将鼓鳞而轻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364052_comment'></div>田鸠野鴳。亦将鶱翮而侮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364052_comment'></div>及其衡溟渤。接扶摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364052_comment'></div>吹波则江汉倒流。腾气则虹霓掩彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364052_comment'></div>摩赤岸。负苍天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364052_comment'></div>然后知其力焉。吁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364052_comment'></div>韩信之无津也。昌亭之一饿夫耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364052_comment'></div>马卿之失路也。临邛之一食客耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364052_comment'></div>武不足以服众。文不足以动时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364052_comment'></div>长剑屈于无知。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>洪笔</span>沦于不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364052_comment'></div>洎乎雄图蹑运。至尊纳背水之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364052_comment'></div>丽藻升朝。天子赏淩云之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364052_comment'></div>威加海岳。声振廊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364052_comment'></div>彼淮阴之侠少。成都之遗老也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364052_comment'></div>又焉能知远近哉。是以鉴物于肇不于成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364052_comment'></div>赏士于穷不于达。是知卞和之得玉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364052_comment'></div>精存于岸谷之间。张华之得剑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364052_comment'></div>气发于星辰之际。夫岂琢磨成器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364052_comment'></div>然后知其宝。剸断为能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364052_comment'></div>然后知其用哉。仰惟乡耆等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364052_comment'></div>并玉山高族。金堤胜侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364052_comment'></div>列子弟于千城。耀衣冠于百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364052_comment'></div>或以风云去国。公孙跃马之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364052_comment'></div>钟鼎从王。诸葛攀龙之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364052_comment'></div>门庭相接。雕薨将绮栋连陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364052_comment'></div>机杼相和。凤镊将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>虬梭</span>交响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364052_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>金浆</span>玉馔。食客三千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364052_comment'></div>绿帻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>青裳</span>。家僮数百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364052_comment'></div>冲襟渺识。人多江汉之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364052_comment'></div>丽藻华文。代有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>云渊</span>之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364052_comment'></div>北斋开敞。南馆虚閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364052_comment'></div>诗酒同归。琴书合契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364052_comment'></div>忘机得意。耻嵇阮之交疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364052_comment'></div>虚席延宾。恨原尝之客少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364052_comment'></div>实烟霞之薮泽。风月之津梁者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364052_comment'></div>刘仲文之远识。不以乾没诣梁城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364052_comment'></div>闵仲叔之高风。不以口腹累安邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364052_comment'></div>虽其已没。生气犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364052_comment'></div>况乎属宇宙之明。当天下之泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364052_comment'></div>不能俯拾青紫。高视搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364052_comment'></div>攀北极而谒帝王。入南宫而取卿相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364052_comment'></div>胁肩侧足。求哀钟釜之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364052_comment'></div>低首俯眉。取济斗升之未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364052_comment'></div>嗟乎。诚下官所以仰天汉而郁拂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364052_comment'></div>临江山而慷慨者也。但时可以未遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364052_comment'></div>道可以未行。志愿可以未成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364052_comment'></div>功业可以未就。古之才足以辅王业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364052_comment'></div>蹑迹屠钓之门。功可以济巨川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364052_comment'></div>藏身版筑之下。百里奚之负贩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364052_comment'></div>陈汤之丐贷。而况于庸者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364052_comment'></div>此仆所以骏奔于顾盼之馀。自致于恩光之末也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364052_comment'></div>且夫精诚所感。尚动神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364052_comment'></div>意气相交。岂惭车马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364052_comment'></div>倘能投心季子。遥存素纻之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364052_comment'></div>援手应侯。先立绨袍之赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364052_comment'></div>岂人之情也。能无报乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364052_comment'></div>方今白藏绍序。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>朱律</span>谢期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364052_comment'></div>天高而林野疏。候肃而江山静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364052_comment'></div>轻蝉送夏。惊晚吹于风园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364052_comment'></div>旅雁乘秋。动宵吟于露渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364052_comment'></div>丝纩成于南亩。粳黍被于东阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364052_comment'></div>时计有储。愿履多福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364052_comment'></div>下官薄游绵载。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/145/Comments/0")'>飘寓</span>淹时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364052_comment'></div>欢踬相仍。忧虞自积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364052_comment'></div>陟梁鸿之峻岳。何暇长谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364052_comment'></div>临阮籍之长途。惟知恸哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364052_comment'></div>庶凭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>赒给</span>。以济飘危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364052_comment'></div>轻诉短怀。伫流<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364052", 1364052, "Clauses/155/Comments/0")'>嘉耗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364052_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1364052_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dafa2ca86d5e4362b983a5bcfd74c631_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dafa2ca86d5e4362b983a5bcfd74c631");'><span id='dafa2ca86d5e4362b983a5bcfd74c631_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>，22岁</div><div id='dafa2ca86d5e4362b983a5bcfd74c631' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　春初,居成都,赴王明府春游宴饮,作《春日序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版第631页。）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
彭州（九陇）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b29dd764393444aea2740477c83016ca_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b29dd764393444aea2740477c83016ca");'><span id='b29dd764393444aea2740477c83016ca_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>，21岁</div><div id='b29dd764393444aea2740477c83016ca' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　秋,应益州大都督府长史李崇义、司马宇文纯及九陇县令柳明之请,作《九陇县孔子庙堂碑文》（又名《益州夫子庙碑》）作品：《九陇县孔子庙堂碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷15第431页。《王子安集注》作《益州夫子庙碑》）</span><div id='poem_1364131' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364131' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364131?labeling=true' target='_blank'>益州夫子庙碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364131")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364131_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364131'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364131'>述夫帝车南指。遁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>七曜</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>中阶</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364131_comment'></div>华盖西临。藏五云于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>太甲</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364131_comment'></div>虽复星辰荡越。三元之轨躅可寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364131_comment'></div>雷雨沸腾。六气之经纶有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364131_comment'></div>然则抚铜浑而观变化。则万象之动不足多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364131_comment'></div>握瑶镜而临事业。则万机之凑不足大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364131_comment'></div>故知功有所服。龟龙不能谢鳞介之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364131_comment'></div>器有所归。江汉不能窃朝宗之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364131_comment'></div>是以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>朱阳</span>登而九有照。紫泉清而万物睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364131_comment'></div>粤若皇灵草昧。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>风骊</span>受河洛之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364131_comment'></div>帝象权舆。云凤锡乾坤之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364131_comment'></div>高辛尧舜氏没。大夏殷周氏作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364131_comment'></div>达其变遂成天下之文。极其数遂定天下之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364131_comment'></div>衣冠度律。随鼎器而重光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364131_comment'></div>玉帛讴歌。反宗禋而大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364131_comment'></div>洎乎三川失御。九服蒙尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364131_comment'></div>俎豆丧而王泽竭。钟鼓衰而颂声寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364131_comment'></div>召陵高会。诸侯轻汉水之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364131_comment'></div>践土同盟。天子窘河阳之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364131_comment'></div>三微制度。乘战道而横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364131_comment'></div>千载英华。与王风而扫地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364131_comment'></div>大业不可以终丧。彝伦不可以遂绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364131_comment'></div>由是山河眹兆。素王开受命之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364131_comment'></div>天地氤氲。元圣举乘时之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364131_comment'></div>兴九围之废典。振六合之颓纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364131_comment'></div>有道存焉。斯文备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364131_comment'></div>夫子姓孔氏。讳邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364131_comment'></div>字仲尼。鲁国邹人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364131_comment'></div>帝天乙之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>灵苗</span>。宋微子之洪绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364131_comment'></div>自元禽剪夏。俘宝玉于南巢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364131_comment'></div>白马朝周。载旌旗于北面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364131_comment'></div>五迁神器。琮璜高列帝之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364131_comment'></div>三命雄图。钟鼎冠承家之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364131_comment'></div>商邱诞睿。下属于防山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364131_comment'></div>泗水载灵。遥驰于汶上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364131_comment'></div>礼乐由其委输。人仪所以来苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364131_comment'></div>排祸乱而搆乾元。扫荒屯而树真宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364131_comment'></div>圣人之大业也。若乃承百王之丕运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364131_comment'></div>总千圣之殊姿。人灵昭有作之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364131_comment'></div>岳渎降非常之表。珠衡玉斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364131_comment'></div>徵象纬于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>天经</span>。虎踞龙蹲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364131_comment'></div>集风云于地纪。亦犹三阶瞰月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364131_comment'></div>恒星知太紫之宫。八柱冲霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364131_comment'></div>群岭辨中黄之宅。圣人之至象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364131_comment'></div>若乃顺时而动。用晦而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364131_comment'></div>纡圣哲于常师。混波流于下问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364131_comment'></div>太阳亭午。收爝火于丹衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364131_comment'></div>沧浪浮天。控涓涔于翠渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364131_comment'></div>西周捧袂。仙公留紫气之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364131_comment'></div>东海抠衣。郯子叙青云之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364131_comment'></div>接舆非圣。询去就于狂歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364131_comment'></div>童子何知。屈炎凉于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>诡问</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364131_comment'></div>圣人之降迹也。若乃参神揆训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364131_comment'></div>录道和倪。辱太白于中都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364131_comment'></div>绊乘黄于下邑。湛无为之迹而众务同并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364131_comment'></div>驰不言之化而群方取则。虽复霓旌羽旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364131_comment'></div>齐人张夹谷之威。八佾三雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364131_comment'></div>桓氏逼公宫之制。洎乎历阶而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364131_comment'></div>宣武备而斩俳优。推义而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364131_comment'></div>肃刑书而诛正卯。用能使四方知罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364131_comment'></div>争归旧好之田。三家变色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364131_comment'></div>愿执陪臣之礼。圣人之成务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364131_comment'></div>若乃乘机动用。历聘栖遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364131_comment'></div>神经幽显。志大宇宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364131_comment'></div>东西南北。推心于暴乱之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364131_comment'></div>恭俭温良。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>授手</span>于危亡之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364131_comment'></div>道之将行也命。道之将废也命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364131_comment'></div>归齐去鲁。发浩叹于衰周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364131_comment'></div>厄宋围陈。奏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>悲歌</span>于下蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364131_comment'></div>圣人之救时也。若乃筐篚六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364131_comment'></div>笙簧五典。折旋洙泗之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364131_comment'></div>探赜唐虞之际。三千弟子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364131_comment'></div>攀睿化而升堂。七十门人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364131_comment'></div>奉洪规而入室。从周定礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364131_comment'></div>宪章知损益之源。反鲁裁诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364131_comment'></div>雅颂得弦歌之旨。备物而存道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364131_comment'></div>下学而上达。援神叙教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364131_comment'></div>降赤制于南宫。运斗陈经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364131_comment'></div>动元符于北洛。圣人之立教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364131_comment'></div>若乃观象设教。法三百八十四爻四十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364131_comment'></div>穷神知化。应万一千二百五十策五十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364131_comment'></div>成变化而行鬼神。观阴阳而倚天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364131_comment'></div>以鼓天下之动。以定天下之疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364131_comment'></div>索众妙于重元。纂群微于太素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364131_comment'></div>圣人之赞易也。若乃灵襟不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364131_comment'></div>睿视无涯。石砮昭集隼之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364131_comment'></div>土缶验羵羊之井。稽山南望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364131_comment'></div>识皓骨于封禺。蠡泽东浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364131_comment'></div>考丹萍于梦渚。麟图鉴远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364131_comment'></div>金编题佐汉之符。凤德钩深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364131_comment'></div>玉策筮亡秦之兆。圣人之观化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364131_comment'></div>时义远矣。能事毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364131_comment'></div>然后拂衣方外。脱屣人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364131_comment'></div>奠楹兴夕梦之灾。负杖起晨歌之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364131_comment'></div>挠虹梁于大厦。物莫能宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364131_comment'></div>摧日观于鲁邱。吾将安仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364131_comment'></div>明均两曜。不能迁代谢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364131_comment'></div>序合四时。不能革盈虚之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364131_comment'></div>适来夫子时也。适去夫子顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364131_comment'></div>为而不有。用九五而长驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364131_comment'></div>成而勿居。抚云霓而高视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364131_comment'></div>圣人之应化也。自四教远而微言绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364131_comment'></div>十哲丧而大义乖。九师争大易之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364131_comment'></div>五传列春秋之辐。六体分于楚晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364131_comment'></div>四始派于齐韩。淹中之妙键不追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364131_comment'></div>稷下之高风代起。百家腾跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364131_comment'></div>攀户牖而同归。万匹驱驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364131_comment'></div>仰陶钧而共贯。犹使丝簧金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364131_comment'></div>长悬阙里之堂。荆棘蓬蒿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364131_comment'></div>不入昌平之墓。圣人之遗风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364131_comment'></div>导扬十圣。光被六虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364131_comment'></div>乘素履而保安贞。垂黄裳而获元吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364131_comment'></div>故能贵而无位。履端于太极之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364131_comment'></div>高而无名。布政于皇王之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364131_comment'></div>千秋所不能易。百代所不能移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364131_comment'></div>万乘资以兴衰。四海由其轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364131_comment'></div>虽复质文交映。瞻礿祀而长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364131_comment'></div>金火递迁。奉琴书而罔绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364131_comment'></div>盖易曰。观乎人文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364131_comment'></div>以化成天下。又云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364131_comment'></div>圣人以神道设教。而万物服焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364131_comment'></div>岂古之聪明睿智神武而不杀者夫。国家袭宇宙之淳精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364131_comment'></div>据明灵之宝位。高祖武皇帝以黄旗问罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364131_comment'></div>杖金策以劳华夷。太宗文皇帝以朱翟承天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364131_comment'></div>穆玉衡而正区宇。皇上宣祖宗之累洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364131_comment'></div>奉文武之重光。稽历数而坐明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364131_comment'></div>陈礼容而谒太庙。八神齐飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364131_comment'></div>停旒太史之宫。六辩同和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364131_comment'></div>驻跸华胥之野。文物隐地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364131_comment'></div>声名动天。乐繁九俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364131_comment'></div>礼盛三古。冠带混并之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364131_comment'></div>书轨八纮。闾阎兼匝之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364131_comment'></div>烟火四极。竭河<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_132_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/265/Comments/0")'>追日</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364131_comment'></div>夸父力尽于楹间。越海陵山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364131_comment'></div>竖亥涂穷于庑下。薰腴广被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364131_comment'></div>景贶潜周。乾象著而常文清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364131_comment'></div>坤灵滋而众宝用。溢金膏于紫洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364131_comment'></div>雨露均华。栖玉烛于元都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364131_comment'></div>风雷顺轨。丹蓂翠菌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364131_comment'></div>藻绘轩庭。凤彩龙姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364131_comment'></div>激扬池籞。殊徵肸蚃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364131_comment'></div>不召而自至。茂祉昭彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364131_comment'></div>无幽而不洽。虽复帝臣南面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364131_comment'></div>降衢室而无为。岱畎东临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364131_comment'></div>陟名山而有事。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_144_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/289/Comments/0")'>灵命</span>不可以辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364131_comment'></div>大典不可以推也。由是六戎宵警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364131_comment'></div>横紫殿而摐金。五校晨驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364131_comment'></div>蹴玄云而喷玉。星罗海运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364131_comment'></div>岳镇川渟。登碧墠而会神祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364131_comment'></div>御元坛而礼天地。金箱玉册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364131_comment'></div>益睿算于无疆。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_150_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/301/Comments/0")'>玳检</span>银绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364131_comment'></div>著<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_151_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/302/Comments/0")'>灵机</span>于不竭。功既成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364131_comment'></div>道既贞矣。历先王之旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364131_comment'></div>怀列圣之遗尘。翔赤骥而下云亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364131_comment'></div>吟翠虬而望邹鲁。泗滨休驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364131_comment'></div>杳疑汾水之阳。尼岫凝銮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364131_comment'></div>暂似峒山之典。乃下诏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364131_comment'></div>可追赠太师。托盐梅于异代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364131_comment'></div>鼎路生光。寄舟楫于同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364131_comment'></div>泉涂改照。咸亨元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364131_comment'></div>又下诏曰。宣尼有纵自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364131_comment'></div>体膺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_161_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/322/Comments/0")'>上哲</span>。合两仪之简易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364131_comment'></div>为亿载之师表。顾唯寝庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364131_comment'></div>义在钦崇。如闻诸州县孔子庙堂及学馆有破坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364131_comment'></div>并向来未造。生徒无肄业之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364131_comment'></div>先师阙奠祭之仪。久致飘零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364131_comment'></div>深非敬本。宜令诸州县官司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364131_comment'></div>速加营葺。成都县学庙堂者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364131_comment'></div>大唐龙朔三年乡人之所建也。尔其州分化鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364131_comment'></div>境属蹲鸱。萦锦室于中区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364131_comment'></div>托铜梁于古地。玉轮斜界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364131_comment'></div>神龙蟠沮泽之云。石镜遥临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364131_comment'></div>宝马蹀禺山之影。天帝会昌之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364131_comment'></div>上照乾维。英灵秀出之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364131_comment'></div>傍清地络。庠序由其纠合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364131_comment'></div>缨弁所以会同。文翁之景化不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364131_comment'></div>智士之风猷自远。于是双川旧老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364131_comment'></div>攀帝奖而翘心。三蜀名儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364131_comment'></div>想成均而变色。探周规于旧宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364131_comment'></div>询汉制于新都。开基于四会之躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364131_comment'></div>授矩于三农之隙。土阶无级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364131_comment'></div>就击壤于新欢。茅茨不剪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364131_comment'></div>易层巢于故事。庄坛文杏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364131_comment'></div>即架椽栾。夹谷幽兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364131_comment'></div>爰疏户牖。仪形莞尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364131_comment'></div>似闻沂水之歌。列侍訚如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364131_comment'></div>若奉农山之对。缁帷晓辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364131_comment'></div>横绀带于西河。绛帐宵悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364131_comment'></div>聚青衿于北海。虽秋礼冬诗之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364131_comment'></div>已洽于齐人。而宣风观俗之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364131_comment'></div>实归于上宰。银青光禄大夫谯国公讳崇义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364131_comment'></div>大武皇帝之支孙。河间大王之长子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364131_comment'></div>高秋九月。振玉贙于唐邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364131_comment'></div>宝算干龄。跃璇虬于太渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364131_comment'></div>我国家<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_194_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/388/Comments/0")'>灵命</span>。东朝抗裘冕之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364131_comment'></div>宗子维城。南面袭轩裳之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364131_comment'></div>析元元之允绪。拥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_196_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/393/Comments/0")'>朱虚</span>之禄位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364131_comment'></div>拜玉节于秦京。辉金章于蜀郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364131_comment'></div>元机应物。潜消水怪之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364131_comment'></div>丹笔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_199_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/398/Comments/0")'>申冤</span>。俯绝山精之讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364131_comment'></div>魏文侯之拥彗。道在而谦尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364131_comment'></div>董相国之垂帷。风行而俗易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364131_comment'></div>司马宇文公讳纯。河南洛阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364131_comment'></div>皇根帝绪。列五鼎于三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364131_comment'></div>青琐丹梯。跨千寻于十纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364131_comment'></div>仲举澄清之辔。未极夷涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364131_comment'></div>士元卿相之材。先登上佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364131_comment'></div>冰壶精鉴。遥清玉垒之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364131_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_208_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/416/Comments/0")'>霜镜</span>悬明。下映金城之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364131_comment'></div>县令柳公讳明。字太易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364131_comment'></div>河东人也。梁岳之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364131_comment'></div>长河之灵。沐云汉之精粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364131_comment'></div>荷天衢之元亨。旌旗赫奕于中古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364131_comment'></div>圭组陆离于下叶。凤岩抽律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364131_comment'></div>擢层秀于龙门。骊穴腾姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364131_comment'></div>吐荣光于贝阙。自朱丝就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364131_comment'></div>光膺令宰之荣。墨绶驰芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364131_comment'></div>高践郎官之右。仙凫旦举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364131_comment'></div>影入铜章。乳翟朝飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364131_comment'></div>声含玉轸。临邛客位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364131_comment'></div>自高文雅之庭。彭泽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_220_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/441/Comments/0")'>宾门</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364131_comment'></div>犹主壶觞之境。旷怀足以御物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364131_comment'></div>长策足以服人。重泉之惠训大行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364131_comment'></div>单父之讴谣遂远。犹为夏弦春诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364131_comment'></div>俗化之枢机。西序东胶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364131_comment'></div>政刑之根本。上只<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_225_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/451/Comments/0")'>朝宪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364131_comment'></div>下奉藩维。爰搜复庙之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364131_comment'></div>载阐重櫩之制。三门四表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364131_comment'></div>焕矣惟新。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_228_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/457/Comments/0")'>上哲</span>师宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364131_comment'></div>肃焉如在。将使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_229_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/459/Comments/0")'>圆冠方领</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364131_comment'></div>再行邹鲁之风。锐气英声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1364131_comment'></div>一变賨渝之俗。于是侍郎幽思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1364131_comment'></div>摛凤藻于瑰材。丞相高材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1364131_comment'></div>排龙姿于璧沼。遗荣处士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1364131_comment'></div>开帘诠孝悌之机。颂德贤臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1364131_comment'></div>持节听中和之乐。其为政也可久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1364131_comment'></div>其为志也可大。方当变化台极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1364131_comment'></div>仪刑万宇。岂徒偃仰听事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1364131_comment'></div>风教一同而已哉。勃幼乏逸才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1364131_comment'></div>少有奇志。虚舟独泛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1364131_comment'></div>乘学海之波澜。直辔高驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364131_comment'></div>践词场之阃阈。观质文之否泰众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364131_comment'></div>考圣贤之去就多矣。自生人以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1364131_comment'></div>未有如夫子者也。嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1364131_comment'></div>今古代绝。江湖路远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1364131_comment'></div>恨不亲承妙旨。摄齐于游夏之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1364131_comment'></div>躬奉德音。攘袂于天人之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1364131_comment'></div>抚声名而永悼。瞻栋宇而长怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1364131_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。敢为铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_249_1364131'>五帝既没。三王不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1364131_comment'></div>天地震动。阴阳乱飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1364131_comment'></div>山崩海竭。月缺星围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1364131_comment'></div>礼乐无主。宗禋遂微<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_253_1364131'>大哉神圣。与时回薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1364131_comment'></div>应运而生。继天而作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1364131_comment'></div>龙跃浩荡。鹏飞寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1364131_comment'></div>奄有人宗。遂荒天爵<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_257_1364131'>尼山降彩。泗滨腾气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1364131_comment'></div>志匡六合。神经万类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1364131_comment'></div>夹谷登庸。中都历试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1364131_comment'></div>睿情贯一。元猷绝四<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_261_1364131'>栖遑教迹。寂寞河图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1364131_comment'></div>违齐出宋。历楚辞吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1364131_comment'></div>风衰俗坏。礼去朝芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1364131_comment'></div>麟书巳卷。凤德终孤<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_265_1364131'>杳杳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_265_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/530/Comments/0")'>灵命</span>。茫茫天秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1364131_comment'></div>吾道难行。斯文易失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1364131_comment'></div>式宣六艺。裁成四术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1364131_comment'></div>虚往实归。外堂内室<span class='inlineComment2'>（其五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_269_1364131'>邈矣能仁。悠哉化主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1364131_comment'></div>力制群辟。权倾终古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1364131_comment'></div>陆离彩粲。蝉联茅土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1364131_comment'></div>涉海轻河。登山小鲁<span class='inlineComment2'>（其六）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_273_1364131'>皇家载造。神风四极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1364131_comment'></div>检玉题祥。绳金署德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1364131_comment'></div>聿怀圣迹。同享天则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1364131_comment'></div>乃眷台庭。爰升衮职<span class='inlineComment2'>（其七）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_277_1364131'>玉津同派。金堤茂版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1364131_comment'></div>智士高风。文翁泽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1364131_comment'></div>氓淳壤沃。声和俗愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1364131_comment'></div>载启仁祠。遂光儒苑<span class='inlineComment2'>（其八）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_281_1364131'>沈沈壶奥。肃肃扃除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1364131_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_282_1364131", 1364131, "Clauses/564/Comments/0")'>灵仪</span>若在。列配如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1364131_comment'></div>槐新市密。杏古坛疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1364131_comment'></div>楹疑置奠。壁似藏书<span class='inlineComment2'>（其九）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1364131_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_285_1364131'>泛泛寰中。悠悠天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1364131_comment'></div>徇名则众。知音盖寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1364131_comment'></div>碝石参琼。迷风乱雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1364131_comment'></div>仲尼既没。夫何为者<span class='inlineComment2'>（其十）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1364131_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_289_1364131_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0f04768d367741c8a5598b826d219e75_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0f04768d367741c8a5598b826d219e75");'><span id='0f04768d367741c8a5598b826d219e75_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>，22岁</div><div id='0f04768d367741c8a5598b826d219e75' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　春,于成都宴游后,复返九陇,旋有《春思赋》及诗歌《春游》、《羁春》等。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷1第1页。）</span>《春游》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第97页。）</span>《羁春》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第96页。）</span><div id='poem_1364031' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364031' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364031?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春思赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364031")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364031_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364031'>咸亨二年。余春秋二十有二。旅寓巴蜀。浮游岁序。殷忧明时。坎壈圣代。九陇县令河东柳太易。英达君子也。仆从游焉。高谈胸怀。颇泄愤懑。于时春也。风光依然。古人云。风景不殊。举目有山河之异。不其悲乎。仆不才。耿介之士也。窃禀宇宙独用之心。受天地不平之气。虽弱植一介。穷途千里。未尝下情于公侯。屈色于流俗。凛然以金石自匹。犹不能忘情于春。则知春之所及远矣。春之所感深矣。此仆所以抚穷贱而惜光阴。怀功名而悲岁月也。岂徒幽宫狭路。陌上桑间而已哉。屈平有言。目极千里伤春心。因作春思赋。庶几乎以极春之所至。析心之去就云尔。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364031'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364031'>若夫年临九域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364031_comment'></div>韶光四极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364031_comment'></div>解宇宙之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>严气</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364031_comment'></div>起亭皋之春色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364031_comment'></div>况风景兮同序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364031_comment'></div>复江山之异国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364031_comment'></div>感大运之盈虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364031_comment'></div>见长河之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>纡直</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364031_comment'></div>蜀川风候隔秦川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364031_comment'></div>今年节物异常年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364031_comment'></div>霜前柳叶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>衔霜</span>翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364031_comment'></div>雪里梅花犯雪妍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364031_comment'></div>霜前雪里知春早。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364031_comment'></div>看柳看梅觉春好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364031_comment'></div>思万里之佳期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364031_comment'></div>忆三秦之远道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364031_comment'></div>澹荡春色<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作风）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364031_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>悠扬</span>怀抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364031_comment'></div>野何树而无花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364031_comment'></div>水何堤而无草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364031_comment'></div>于是仆本<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>浪人</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364031_comment'></div>平生自沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364031_comment'></div>怀书去洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364031_comment'></div>抱剑辞秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364031_comment'></div>惜良会之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>遒迈</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364031_comment'></div>厌他乡之苦辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364031_comment'></div>忽逢边候改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364031_comment'></div>遥忆帝乡春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364031_comment'></div>帝乡迢递关河里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364031_comment'></div>神皋欲暮风烟起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364031_comment'></div>黄山半入上林园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364031_comment'></div>元灞斜分曲江水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364031_comment'></div>玉台金阙纷相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364031_comment'></div>千门万户遥相似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364031_comment'></div>昭阳殿里报春归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364031_comment'></div>未央台上看春晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364031_comment'></div>水精却挂鸳鸯幔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364031_comment'></div>云母斜开翡翠帏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364031_comment'></div>竞道西园梅色浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364031_comment'></div>争知北阙柳阴稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364031_comment'></div>敛态调歌扇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364031_comment'></div>回<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作端）</span>身整舞衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364031_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>银蚕</span>吐丝犹未暖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364031_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>金燕</span>衔泥试学飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364031_comment'></div>妾本幽闺学歌舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364031_comment'></div>宁知汉代多巡抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364031_comment'></div>前年斋祭谒甘泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364031_comment'></div>今岁笙箫祠后土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364031_comment'></div>桃花万骑喧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>长薄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364031_comment'></div>兰叶千旗照平浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364031_comment'></div>见原野之秀芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364031_comment'></div>忆山河之邃古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364031_comment'></div>长安路狭绕长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364031_comment'></div>公子春来不厌看。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364031_comment'></div>杏叶装金辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364031_comment'></div>蒲萄镂玉鞍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364031_comment'></div>耸盖临平乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364031_comment'></div>回笳出上兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364031_comment'></div>上兰经鄠杜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364031_comment'></div>挥鞭日将暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364031_comment'></div>白马新临御沟道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364031_comment'></div>青牛近出章台路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364031_comment'></div>章台接建章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364031_comment'></div>垂柳复垂杨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364031_comment'></div>草开驰马埒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364031_comment'></div>花满斗鸡场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364031_comment'></div>南邻少妇多妖婉<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作婉娩）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364031_comment'></div>北里王孙驻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>行幰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364031_comment'></div>乍怪前春节候迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364031_comment'></div>预道今年寒食晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364031_comment'></div>伤紫陌之<span id='poem_sentence_78_1364031_comment'></div>步步看花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364031_comment'></div>因狂夫之荡子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364031_comment'></div>成贱妾之倡家。<div id='poem_sentence_84_1364031_comment'></div>安知榆塞三千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364031_comment'></div>榆塞连延玉关侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364031_comment'></div>云间沈沈不可识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364031_comment'></div>葱山隐隐金河北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364031_comment'></div>雾里苍苍几重䵥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364031_comment'></div>忽有驿骑出幽并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364031_comment'></div>传道春衣万里程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364031_comment'></div>龙沙春草遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364031_comment'></div>瀚海春云生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364031_comment'></div>疏勒井泉寒尚竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364031_comment'></div>燕山烽火夜应明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364031_comment'></div>闻道河源路远远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364031_comment'></div>谁教夫婿苦行行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364031_comment'></div>君行塞外多霜露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364031_comment'></div>为想春台<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作园）</span>起烟雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364031_comment'></div>游丝空罥合欢枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364031_comment'></div>落花自绕相思树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364031_comment'></div>春望年年绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364031_comment'></div>幽闺离绪切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364031_comment'></div>春色朝朝异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364031_comment'></div>边庭羽书至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364031_comment'></div>都护新封<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_106_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>万里侯</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364031_comment'></div>将军稍定三边地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364031_comment'></div>长旆犹衔扫云色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364031_comment'></div>宝刀尚拥干星气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364031_comment'></div>昨夜祁连驿使还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364031_comment'></div>征夫犹在雁门关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364031_comment'></div>君度山川成白首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364031_comment'></div>应知岁序歇红颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364031_comment'></div>红颜一别成胡越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364031_comment'></div>夫婿连延限城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364031_comment'></div>羌笛横吹陇路风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364031_comment'></div>戎衣直照关山月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364031_comment'></div>春色徒盈望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364031_comment'></div>春悲殊未歇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364031_comment'></div>复闻天子幸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_120_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/120/Comments/0")'>关东</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364031_comment'></div>驰道烟尘万里红。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364031_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_122_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>析羽</span>摇初日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364031_comment'></div>繁笳思晓风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364031_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_124_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/124/Comments/0")'>后骑</span>犹分长乐馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364031_comment'></div>前旌已映洛阳宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364031_comment'></div>洛阳宫城纷合沓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364031_comment'></div>离房<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_127_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>别殿</span>花周匝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364031_comment'></div>河阳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/128/Comments/0")'>别舍</span>抵长河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364031_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_129_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>丹轮</span>绀幰相经过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364031_comment'></div>戚里繁珠翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364031_comment'></div>中闺盛绮罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364031_comment'></div>凤移金谷舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364031_comment'></div>莺引石城歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364031_comment'></div>向夕天津洛桥暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364031_comment'></div>争驱紫燕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_135_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>黄牛</span>度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364031_comment'></div>閒居伊水园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364031_comment'></div>旧宅邙山路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364031_comment'></div>武子新布金钱埒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364031_comment'></div>季伦欲碎珊瑚树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364031_comment'></div>复道西墉春雾寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364031_comment'></div>更值南津春望写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364031_comment'></div>入金市而乘羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364031_comment'></div>出铜街而试马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364031_comment'></div>叶抱露<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作草犯春）</span>而争密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364031_comment'></div>花牵风而乱下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364031_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/146/Comments/0")'>锦障</span>萦山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364031_comment'></div>罗帏照野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364031_comment'></div>司空令尹之博物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364031_comment'></div>二陆三张之文雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364031_comment'></div>新年柏叶之樽。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364031_comment'></div>年光几处新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364031_comment'></div>何年春不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364031_comment'></div>何地不宜春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364031_comment'></div>亦有当春逢远客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364031_comment'></div>亦有当春别故人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364031_comment'></div>风物虽同候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364031_comment'></div>悲欢各异伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364031_comment'></div>归去春山恣间放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364031_comment'></div><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_180_1364031_comment'></div>石镜岩前花屡密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364031_comment'></div>玉轮江上叶频浓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364031_comment'></div>自有春光煎别思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364031_comment'></div>无劳春镜照愁容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364031_comment'></div>盛年耿耿辞乡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364031_comment'></div>长路遥遥不可极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364031_comment'></div>形随朗月骤东西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364031_comment'></div>思逐浮云几南北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364031_comment'></div>春蝶参差命俦侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364031_comment'></div>春莺绵蛮思羽翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364031_comment'></div>余复何为此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364031_comment'></div>方春长叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364031_comment'></div>会当一举绝风尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364031_comment'></div>翠盖珠轩临上春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364031_comment'></div>朝升玉署调天纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364031_comment'></div>夕憩金闺奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_198_1364031", 1364031, "Clauses/198/Comments/0")'>帝纶</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364031_comment'></div>长卿未达终希达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364031_comment'></div>曲逆长贫岂剩贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364031_comment'></div>年年送春应未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364031_comment'></div>一旦逢春自有人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_202_1364031_comment'></div></div></div><div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8798", 8798, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>客念</span>纷无极，春泪倍成行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8798_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8798'>今朝花树下，不觉恋年光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8798_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8798'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8798_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_8809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>羁春</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_8809")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8809'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8809'>客心千里倦，春事一朝归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8809'>还伤北园里，重见落花飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8809'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8809_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　春,又应九陇县令柳明献（字太初,即前所称柳明）之请,作《九陇县龙怀寺碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷19第565页。《王子安集注》作《彭州九陇县龙怀寺碑》）</span><div id='poem_1364141' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364141' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364141?labeling=true' target='_blank'>彭州九陇县龙怀寺碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364141")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364141_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364141'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364141'>粤若真元混沌。抱一气于天门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364141_comment'></div>象化童蒙。构三灵于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>地户</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364141_comment'></div>由是金城逆顺。山河假成器之因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364141_comment'></div>玉烛沈浮。风火兆流形之蘖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364141_comment'></div>悬大明于日月。适滞泉宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364141_comment'></div>设巨浸于云雷。终迷燬宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364141_comment'></div>太极所以散而为两。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>洪飙</span>所以吹而为万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364141_comment'></div>虽复卑高异列。俱沈方内之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364141_comment'></div>坌集横流。共失环中之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364141_comment'></div>岂夫涅槃深视。不背色以求真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364141_comment'></div>般若长驱。每乘空而得静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364141_comment'></div>则知一名同出。阴阳为破道之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364141_comment'></div>万象皆空。天地即降魔之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364141_comment'></div>莫见其俯仰。不知其去就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364141_comment'></div>至自于太虚。复归于无物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364141_comment'></div>其建言立德。开业成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364141_comment'></div>握大柄而推造化。执洪炉而诘元始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364141_comment'></div>西门幽辟。顾非相而迟回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364141_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>三驾</span>晨严。临有为而出顿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364141_comment'></div>岂不知羁孤长路。终婴旅泊之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364141_comment'></div>舟楫中流。未释风涛之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364141_comment'></div>将以宅心者寂。虚室所以合符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364141_comment'></div>应物者神。明镜由其不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364141_comment'></div>故能商搉宇宙。指麾权实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364141_comment'></div>演群生而非其力。存庶品而非其有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364141_comment'></div>千峦闭景。似居蓬艾之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364141_comment'></div>双阙临空。若在江湖之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364141_comment'></div>其释迦之冲用乎。龙怀山者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364141_comment'></div>井络之所交会。岷隅之所控带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364141_comment'></div>攒峰北走。吐沓嶂于元霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364141_comment'></div>巨壑南驰。喷洪涛于赤岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364141_comment'></div>香城宝地。左右林泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364141_comment'></div>碧岫丹岑。往来烟雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364141_comment'></div>时有法会禅师者。俗姓褚氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364141_comment'></div>吴郡钱塘人也。金章钖美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364141_comment'></div>河阴传九命之尊。玉铉乘荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364141_comment'></div>江左受三台之贵。地灵人杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364141_comment'></div>自朔野而重光。学府文宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364141_comment'></div>冠南都而独秀。法师紫星降彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364141_comment'></div>红云受气。应积善于高门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364141_comment'></div>契冥缘于累世。果浮觞引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364141_comment'></div>潜图彼岸之功。聚砾延砂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364141_comment'></div>即揆为山之业。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>灵枢</span>密运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364141_comment'></div>辟仁路而长鸣。慧刃高挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364141_comment'></div>斩邪关而洞照。以为冥机体化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364141_comment'></div>毫发莫滞其真。执数逐微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364141_comment'></div>乾坤不容其算。于是四禅幽观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364141_comment'></div>破铜堞而出无明。三昧雄图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364141_comment'></div>排铁围而泯非相。法云自在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364141_comment'></div>吐纳龙宫。贤圣不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364141_comment'></div>奔驰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/100/Comments/0")'>象域</span>。将使三千塔庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364141_comment'></div>知真实之元津。万亿幡幢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364141_comment'></div>入空虚之秘藏。安心乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364141_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>遁影</span>灵关。以开皇元年憩于兹岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364141_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>灵墟</span>福地。已被神功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364141_comment'></div>玉榜金绳。未光朝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364141_comment'></div>蜀王秀以文昭建国。帝子专征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364141_comment'></div>仗巴服之尊名。裂邛荒之宝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364141_comment'></div>彤騑僭帝。跸万骑于铜梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364141_comment'></div>皂盖图王。警千乘于玉宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364141_comment'></div>镜山南望。志狭彭渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364141_comment'></div>锦水西浮。耻朝江汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364141_comment'></div>开实沈之壁垒。啸京叔之风尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364141_comment'></div>拥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>龟堞</span>而托殊方。凭爵堂而傲天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364141_comment'></div>威权所制。胜兵数十州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364141_comment'></div>雄视所临。经涂五千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364141_comment'></div>三英赋雪。瞻秋月于梁台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364141_comment'></div>八叟吟风。传朝云于楚馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364141_comment'></div>思宏正法。广召名僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364141_comment'></div>振锡云趋。乘杯雾合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364141_comment'></div>禅师括囊泉石。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/141/Comments/0")'>韬迹</span>烟霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364141_comment'></div>攀紫桂而同尘。守青莲而向晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364141_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/144/Comments/0")'>冲飙</span>荡岳。宁移忍地之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364141_comment'></div>烈火焚山。不挠坚林之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364141_comment'></div>王心有悟。时加优礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364141_comment'></div>顺风拜道。封山谢失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364141_comment'></div>发净财于广内。揆仙室于重幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364141_comment'></div>因嶂为壁。凭崖列户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364141_comment'></div>以开皇五年始赐额为龙怀寺。地邻绵左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364141_comment'></div>遂均绵上之恩。山似龙盘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364141_comment'></div>即建龙怀之刹。尔其崇峦经复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364141_comment'></div>复涧萦回。高邱泄云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364141_comment'></div>长林翳日。增琼垣于下麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364141_comment'></div>揆瑶构于中岩。香阙神行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364141_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_84_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/168/Comments/0")'>珍台</span>妙立。玉虬衔霭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364141_comment'></div>绝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/170/Comments/0")'>游气</span>而负苍天。金凤连甍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364141_comment'></div>排烈风而瞰元圃。延绿房于謺巘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364141_comment'></div>上拂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/174/Comments/0")'>霞庄</span>。蔓丹阙于重溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364141_comment'></div>下披泉户。阳开阴阖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364141_comment'></div>变霜露于旋回。蠖动螟飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364141_comment'></div>起雷霆于指顾。玉堂朝亘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364141_comment'></div>影袭长虹。珠殿宵浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364141_comment'></div>光含列宿。禅师殁后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364141_comment'></div>爰有孝恭法师智开法师宏向法师宝积阇黎四上人者。并禅师之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/187/Comments/0")'>上足</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364141_comment'></div>而法门之领袖也。五明衢路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364141_comment'></div>控引情宫。八解源流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364141_comment'></div>朝宗性海。其深为宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364141_comment'></div>拔白玉于崭岩。无碍居真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364141_comment'></div>得元珠于象罔。住持真界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364141_comment'></div>栖息妙涂。俱深寂灭之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364141_comment'></div>各證菩提之域。虽业定人境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364141_comment'></div>照已极于无方。而道寄生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364141_comment'></div>功遂覃于有相。演中乘之奥义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364141_comment'></div>增上栋之宏规。万栱不骞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364141_comment'></div>千门有闶。俄而帝隋<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_104_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/209/Comments/0")'>大去</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364141_comment'></div>皇家小往。天地闭而贤人隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364141_comment'></div>云雷屯而巨宝衰。毒龙横雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364141_comment'></div>四天沈暗逆之悲。醉象驱风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364141_comment'></div>三界溺崩离之酷。上人慧机幽晤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364141_comment'></div>定识潜融。知佛日之恒明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364141_comment'></div>审王风之尚静。芝歌商岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364141_comment'></div>揆鸡岭而同归。茅藉磻溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364141_comment'></div>与猴江而共致。遁俗无闷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364141_comment'></div>因时有待。洎丹陵启秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364141_comment'></div>赤县居尊。迦维授手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364141_comment'></div>波旬革面。十千天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364141_comment'></div>新朝帝释之宫。八万仙人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364141_comment'></div>始向毗耶之国。一音演而荒景服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364141_comment'></div>三圣澄而礼乐备。由是巴方旧彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364141_comment'></div>蜀城遗老。仰慈门而知户牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364141_comment'></div>升福田而喜耕凿。雕鞍绣辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364141_comment'></div>瞻燕㟧而驰魂。黼带綖裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364141_comment'></div>指<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_122_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/244/Comments/0")'>鹦林</span>而鹜款。宝瓶宵注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364141_comment'></div>润浃尧旬。玉尘晨麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364141_comment'></div>风调舜历。咸以为假沈其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364141_comment'></div>迷生安视听之功。动乱其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364141_comment'></div>穷子失肌肤之恋。江连巫峡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364141_comment'></div>始绊心猿。山对禺同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364141_comment'></div>终维意马。贞观年中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364141_comment'></div>积阇黎等乃宣昭遗址。发挥精舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364141_comment'></div>容成校历。揆日用于天经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364141_comment'></div>隶首陈章。算神功于地箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364141_comment'></div>回廊𥦖窱。自吐风飙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364141_comment'></div>列榭峥嵘。坐含云雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364141_comment'></div>图竭宫之妙质。俨卢舍之真容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364141_comment'></div>宝珠周映。银龛备色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364141_comment'></div>逸多垂足。似临兜率之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364141_comment'></div>师利分身。若赴维摩之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364141_comment'></div>灵仙可接。藻绘无施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364141_comment'></div>真应难徵。雕镌有寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364141_comment'></div>若乃巡积岨。历森沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364141_comment'></div>天花照而高月落。地籁惊而幽泉涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364141_comment'></div>紫兰花径。香侵柏叶之炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364141_comment'></div>绿草文茵。影入芙蓉之座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364141_comment'></div>真童凤策。即践金沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364141_comment'></div>仙女<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_145_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/290/Comments/0")'>鸾衣</span>。还窥石镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364141_comment'></div>岩庄转梵。杳冥松桂之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364141_comment'></div>涧户栖槔。寂寞藤萝之院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364141_comment'></div>法鼓奏而寒山旷。洪钟鸣而晓壑静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364141_comment'></div>赪苔翠藓。具不尽之灵衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364141_comment'></div>石乳琼浆。入无生之妙馔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364141_comment'></div>肃肃焉。遥遥焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364141_comment'></div>信调御之珠庭。而列真之甲第也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364141_comment'></div>爰有上座元鉴法师等。并六尘无我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364141_comment'></div>四谛非他。奉乾越之微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364141_comment'></div>守楞伽之奥府。法雷潜吼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364141_comment'></div>鼓动风烟。慧日扬明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364141_comment'></div>照临丘壑。青溪坐定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364141_comment'></div>见心宅之恒灵。丹洞行忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364141_comment'></div>觉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_159_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/318/Comments/0")'>身城</span>之每化。须弥不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364141_comment'></div>迥镇阎浮。阇崛安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364141_comment'></div>下观忍利。开四生之广路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364141_comment'></div>叙六趣之彝伦。足以导扬真绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364141_comment'></div>恭宣来命者矣。县令柳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364141_comment'></div>讳明献。字太初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364141_comment'></div>河东人也。太元降气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364141_comment'></div>中黄授彩。袭周鲁之荣基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364141_comment'></div>吐河汾之灵液。四科高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364141_comment'></div>振风翮于三冬。万室崇班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364141_comment'></div>跼云骖于百里。既而政成黎颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364141_comment'></div>道洽氓讴。假无上之幽筌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364141_comment'></div>毗不言之景化。弦歌在韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364141_comment'></div>将宝偈而齐归。铜墨成章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364141_comment'></div>与梵天而共贯。琼波湛淡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364141_comment'></div>沃荡云雷。珠灌萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364141_comment'></div>蔽亏烟雨。贞机罕应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364141_comment'></div>良谈放好事之游。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_176_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/353/Comments/0")'>朗调</span>多奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364141_comment'></div>高赏尽名山之曲。下走东皋事失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364141_comment'></div>南州涂穷。叹孔席之栖遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364141_comment'></div>笑阳歧之浩荡。薄游兹邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364141_comment'></div>喜见高人。三接而定琴樽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364141_comment'></div>七纵而擒风月。林宗有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364141_comment'></div>相期清浊之间。平叔能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364141_comment'></div>见许天人之际。从容宴语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364141_comment'></div>契阔胸怀。欣性情之同冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364141_comment'></div>感形骸之共遣。虽元都妙域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364141_comment'></div>已挂于忘言。而义塾文场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364141_comment'></div>窃申于知已。敢作颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364141_comment'></div>妙象无倪。神功有涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364141_comment'></div>湛淡名器。奔腾事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364141_comment'></div>慧路翘车。禅河<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_190_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/381/Comments/0")'>舣楫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364141_comment'></div>控引群品。轮回<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_191_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/383/Comments/0")'>庶劫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364141_comment'></div>纵横宇宙。反覆山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364141_comment'></div>言因境立。道寄形诠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364141_comment'></div>爰稽福地。式揆珍田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364141_comment'></div>丹溪漏日。碧洞栖烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364141_comment'></div>阇都玉槛。须弥石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364141_comment'></div>榛灌溟濛。风云萧瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364141_comment'></div>晬容乃眷。禅徒有谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364141_comment'></div>业磴三休。花岩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_199_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/399/Comments/0")'>四密</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364141_comment'></div>崇峦架殿。謺嶂营楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364141_comment'></div>千楣凤起。万栱鸾浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364141_comment'></div>星开绀发。月湛青眸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364141_comment'></div>神宫不夜。邃阁长秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364141_comment'></div>户临重㟧。窗分绝岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364141_comment'></div>半汉香浮。中天梵警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364141_comment'></div>鹤林圣迹。龙泉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_206_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/413/Comments/0")'>佛影</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364141_comment'></div>鸟思山空。猿悲峡静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364141_comment'></div>森森巨柏。落落长松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364141_comment'></div>月出东岫。霞生北峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364141_comment'></div>山人自狎。野老相逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364141_comment'></div>白云屡断。青溪几重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364141_comment'></div>彭泽之令。临邛之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364141_comment'></div>比德山薮。重规泉石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364141_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_214_1364141", 1364141, "Clauses/428/Comments/0")'>法宇</span>成言。慈门致役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364141_comment'></div>糠秕吏隐。薜萝心迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364141_comment'></div>吾生扰扰。与道遑遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364141_comment'></div>殷勤颂咏。惆怅津梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364141_comment'></div>投功翠碣。助化元场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364141_comment'></div>百年之后。苔藓苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364141_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_220_1364141_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年4月</a>　四月,同九陇县令柳明祷雨于九陇县白鹿山。作品：《祭白鹿山神文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（罗振玉《永丰乡人杂著续编·王子安集佚文》壬戌(1922)刊本。《罗振玉学术论著集》第五集《王子安集佚文》上海古籍出版社2010年版。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年4月</a>　祷雨之后,宴于仙居观。作品：《夏日仙居观宴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版第636页。）</span><div id='poem_1364083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏日宴宋五官宅观画障序</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364083")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364083'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364083'>宋五官芝庭袭誉。盛文史于三冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364083_comment'></div>桂幄凝欢。照绮罗于九夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364083_comment'></div>樽浮绿蚁。每披仙雾之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364083_comment'></div>障列青牛。更写行云之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364083_comment'></div>尔其龙编绣质。贝锦分花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364083_comment'></div>隐映楼台。比窗帘之在旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364083_comment'></div>参差花叶。若桃李之恒春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364083_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364083", 1364083, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>楚媛</span>调弦。韩娥对酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364083_comment'></div>虹桥度幔。鹊镜临妆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364083_comment'></div>佩引琅玕。讵动怀风之韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364083_comment'></div>鞍回玳瑁。唯奔逐日之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364083_comment'></div>鱼鸟冷而相亲。泉石纷而在玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364083_comment'></div>宋家斯近。难别谢于登垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364083_comment'></div>秦氏未遥。自堪留于驻马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364083_comment'></div>惊鸿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364083", 1364083, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>擅美</span>。丹青贵近质之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364083_comment'></div>吐凤标华。宫徵得缘情之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364083_comment'></div>递扬笔妙。式畅辞端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364083_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1364083_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绵竹
-----detail

class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>帝机</span>寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364132_comment'></div>云雷驱妙有之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364132_comment'></div>正气洪荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364132_comment'></div>清浊构乾元之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364132_comment'></div>融而为川渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364132_comment'></div>结而为山岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364132_comment'></div>五城韬海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364132_comment'></div>接昆阆于大都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364132_comment'></div>八洞藏云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364132_comment'></div>冠瀛洲于巨阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364132_comment'></div>造化之所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>偃薄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364132_comment'></div>灵谷之所启处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364132_comment'></div>极缇油而纵观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364132_comment'></div>咏颂宁殚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364132_comment'></div>出宇宙而高寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364132_comment'></div>风烟罕测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364132_comment'></div>是知玉卮无当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364132_comment'></div>遐荒非视听之津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364132_comment'></div>金榜所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364132_comment'></div>城阙尽江湖之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364132_comment'></div>何必九虬齐骛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364132_comment'></div>直访银宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364132_comment'></div>八骏长驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364132_comment'></div>遥临石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364132_comment'></div>武都山净慧寺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364132_comment'></div>梁太清年中之所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364132_comment'></div>名山列岳之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364132_comment'></div>仙都福地之凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364132_comment'></div>黄龙负匣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364132_comment'></div>著<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>宝籍</span>于山经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364132_comment'></div>紫凤衔书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364132_comment'></div>荫荣光于井络。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364132_comment'></div>须弥峰顶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364132_comment'></div>仍开梵帝之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364132_comment'></div>如意山中。<div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>盘基</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/36/Comments/1")'>跨险</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364132_comment'></div>列嶂凭霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364132_comment'></div>日月之所窜伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364132_comment'></div>飞泉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>瀑溜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364132_comment'></div>荡涤峰崖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364132_comment'></div>绿树元藤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364132_comment'></div>网罗丘壑。<div
