id='poem_sentence_49_1364132_comment'></div>桂庑松楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364132_comment'></div>寂寞风尘之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364132_comment'></div>是称英镇。<div id='poem_sentence_59_1364132_comment'></div>山川络绎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364132_comment'></div>崩腾宇宙之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364132_comment'></div>原隰纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364132_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>隐轸</span>亭皋之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364132_comment'></div>顷以黄旗夜徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364132_comment'></div>紫盖晨倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364132_comment'></div>九服失图。<div id='poem_sentence_68_1364132_comment'></div>据折坂而吟云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364132_comment'></div>壮士闻鸡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364132_comment'></div>拥阳关而啸雨。<div id='poem_sentence_73_1364132_comment'></div>江汉横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364132_comment'></div>非复朝宗之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364132_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>禅宇</span>由其覆没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364132_comment'></div><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_78_1364132_comment'></div>削平天衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364132_comment'></div>紫宸反照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364132_comment'></div>皇阶即叙。<div id='poem_sentence_83_1364132_comment'></div>幽显再立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364132_comment'></div>华戎一揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364132_comment'></div>烛龙韬景。<div id='poem_sentence_157_1364132_comment'></div>实杳冥之秘诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364132_comment'></div>托幽深之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_159_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/159/Comments/0")'>逸境</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364132_comment'></div>岂直淮南桂树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364132_comment'></div>暂得仙家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364132_comment'></div>江左桃源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364132_comment'></div>终迷故老而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364132_comment'></div>爰有宽阇黎者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364132_comment'></div>俗姓杨氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364132_comment'></div>其先华阴人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364132_comment'></div>因官徙地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364132_comment'></div>家于绵竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364132_comment'></div>山分太华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364132_comment'></div>水带长汾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364132_comment'></div>川岳会同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364132_comment'></div>风云感召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364132_comment'></div>元经素论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364132_comment'></div>侍郎居八俊之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364132_comment'></div>绿绶黄轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364132_comment'></div>太尉列三台之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364132_comment'></div>法师玉函降彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364132_comment'></div>金瓶探色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364132_comment'></div>振八解之遥源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364132_comment'></div>践三明之广路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364132_comment'></div>灵机入證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364132_comment'></div>穷象载于初髫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364132_comment'></div>妙谛因心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364132_comment'></div>释羊车于弱冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364132_comment'></div>三千法界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364132_comment'></div>由广位而出无明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364132_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_187_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/187/Comments/0")'>十二因缘</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364132_comment'></div>自普济而登彼岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364132_comment'></div>宏宣誓愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364132_comment'></div>大振沈黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364132_comment'></div>挥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_191_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/191/Comments/0")'>觉剑</span>而破邪山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364132_comment'></div>扬<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_192_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/192/Comments/0")'>智灯</span>而照昏室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364132_comment'></div>弥纶所被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364132_comment'></div>白马尽于禺同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364132_comment'></div>权渐所开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364132_comment'></div>黄牛至于嶓冢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364132_comment'></div>虔诚乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364132_comment'></div>憩影兹峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364132_comment'></div>乃以贞观九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364132_comment'></div>于寺西院立七佛堂一僧舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364132_comment'></div>星毫动牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364132_comment'></div>月面分阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364132_comment'></div>彩凤衔旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364132_comment'></div>神龙负塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364132_comment'></div>飞烟涌座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364132_comment'></div>龛龛忉利之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364132_comment'></div>香雾成台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364132_comment'></div>树树菩提之果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364132_comment'></div>朝散大夫行县令清河张楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364132_comment'></div>亲承妙业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364132_comment'></div>俯刊贞珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364132_comment'></div>林宗有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364132_comment'></div>伯喈无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364132_comment'></div>法师夙机少晤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364132_comment'></div>应变多奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364132_comment'></div>玉山中断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364132_comment'></div>琼林下杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364132_comment'></div>支道林之好事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364132_comment'></div>语默方融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364132_comment'></div>释慧远之高居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364132_comment'></div>风埃遂隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364132_comment'></div>洎乎坐忘遗照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364132_comment'></div>返寂归真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364132_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_224_1364132", 1364132, "Clauses/224/Comments/0")'>城肆</span>飒然若遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364132_comment'></div>空山黯而无色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364132_comment'></div>岂直岩枝泣血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364132_comment'></div>涧户摧梁而已哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364132_comment'></div>县令刘照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364132_comment'></div>彭城人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364132_comment'></div>自砀山仗剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1364132_comment'></div>绾凤历于云台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1364132_comment'></div>春郊授钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1364132_comment'></div>嗣龙图于白水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1364132_comment'></div>玉垒三分之冑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1364132_comment'></div>下杂公门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1364132_comment'></div>金陵一霸之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1364132_comment'></div>旁参帝绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1364132_comment'></div>翠緌丹绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1364132_comment'></div>历今古而先鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1364132_comment'></div>人杰地灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364132_comment'></div>冠山川而得隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364132_comment'></div>君膺岳渎之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1364132_comment'></div>挺风云之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1364132_comment'></div>昆溪剑锷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1364132_comment'></div>直照胸襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1364132_comment'></div>楚泽圭璋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1364132_comment'></div>爰命缉兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1364132_comment'></div>式光泉薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1364132_comment'></div>虎蹊龙涧。<div id='poem_sentence_266_1364132_comment'></div>更计瀛洲之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1364132_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1364132_comment'></div>武都仙镇。<div id='poem_sentence_272_1364132_comment'></div>涧流百道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1364132_comment'></div>峰云五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1364132_comment'></div>谷暗藤斜。<div id='poem_sentence_277_1364132_comment'></div>万栱星悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1364132_comment'></div>分林构址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1364132_comment'></div>接磴开廛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1364132_comment'></div>临阶竹树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1364132_comment'></div>绕栋风烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1364132_comment'></div>龛前怪石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1364132_comment'></div>塔下秋泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1364132_comment'></div>绿崖疏径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1364132_comment'></div>青岑拒室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1364132_comment'></div>雾道相萦。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1364132_comment'></div>鸟度难寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1364132_comment'></div>猿惊易失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1364132_comment'></div>檐分石窦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1364132_comment'></div>地络金沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1364132_comment'></div>丹邱抗月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1364132_comment'></div>砌因岩曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1364132_comment'></div>桥随峰返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1364132_comment'></div>果出天厨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1364132_comment'></div>香来仙苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1364132_comment'></div>玉钥启曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1364132_comment'></div>金铛照晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1364132_comment'></div>谷思钟张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1364132_comment'></div>山悲铎远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1364132_comment'></div>闾阎践胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1364132_comment'></div>铜墨高情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1364132_comment'></div>声飞别邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1364132_comment'></div>望动专城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1364132_comment'></div>悬金道肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1364132_comment'></div>刻石山楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1364132_comment'></div>千载之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1364132_comment'></div>吁嗟令名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_316_1364132_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
梓潼
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年6月</a>　六月,北归至梓潼,与梓潼县令韦君一同泛舟南江,作《梓潼南江泛舟序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷6第190页。）</span><div id='poem_1364067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梓潼南江泛舟序</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364067")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364067'>咸亨二年六月癸巳。梓潼县令韦君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364067_comment'></div>以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364067", 1364067, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>清湛</span>幽凝。镇流靖俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364067_comment'></div>境内无事。舣舟于江潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364067_comment'></div>纵观于丘壑。渺然有山林陂泽之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364067_comment'></div>遂长怀悠想。周览极睇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364067_comment'></div>思其人。则吕望藉茅于磻溪之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364067_comment'></div>屈平制芰于涔阳之浦。觉瀛洲方丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364067_comment'></div>森然在目。于是间以投壶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364067_comment'></div>酬以妙论。亦有嘉肴旨酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364067_comment'></div>鸣弦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364067", 1364067, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>朗笛</span>。以补寻幽之致焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364067_comment'></div>预于斯者。若干人尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364067_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1364067_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　秋,徘徊于绵州、梓潼间,作《山中》、《江亭夜月送别二首》、《临江二首》等诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第101页。）</span>《江亭夜月送别二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第99页。）</span>《临江二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷3第98页。）</span><div id='poem_8775' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8775' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8775?labeling=true' "poem_title_8775")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8775_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8775'><div class='poemSentence' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8782'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8782'>乱烟笼碧砌，飞月向南端。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8782'>寂寂离亭掩，江山此夜寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8782'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_8782'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(8782)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_8793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8793?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>别棹</span>，俱是倦游人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8793'></div><div id='poem_content_8794'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8794'>去骖嘶别路，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8794", 8794, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>归棹</span>隐寒洲。<div -----title
凤县（凤州）

-----title
宝鸡（散关）

-----title
灵宝（弘农）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fa7491bdf5374de6bd01a770e394e13c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fa7491bdf5374de6bd01a770e394e13c");'><span id='fa7491bdf5374de6bd01a770e394e13c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>，23岁</div><div id='fa7491bdf5374de6bd01a770e394e13c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>　在虢州参军任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7798922f966b4281938d9c7369d9a5f1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7798922f966b4281938d9c7369d9a5f1");'><span id='7798922f966b4281938d9c7369d9a5f1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=674')">672-674年</a>，23-25岁</div><div id='7798922f966b4281938d9c7369d9a5f1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>　本年或明年,撰《释迦如来成道记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷10第291页。）</span><div id='poem_1364108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>释迦如来成道记</a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364108")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364108'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364108'>观夫释迦如来之垂迹也。净法界身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364108_comment'></div>本无出没。大悲愿力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364108_comment'></div>示现受生。洎兜率陀天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364108_comment'></div>为护明菩萨。降迦毗罗国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364108_comment'></div>号一切义成。金团天子选其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364108_comment'></div>白净饭王为其父。玉象乘日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364108_comment'></div>示来于大术胎中。金轮作王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364108_comment'></div>创诞于无忧村下。八十种随形之妙好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364108_comment'></div>粲若芬花。三十二大士之相仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364108_comment'></div>皎如圆月。四方而各行七步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364108_comment'></div>九水而共沐一身。现优昙花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364108_comment'></div>作狮子吼。言胎分之已尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364108_comment'></div>早證常身。为度生以还来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364108_comment'></div>今垂化迹。于是还羁襁褓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364108_comment'></div>示貌婴儿。为占相也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364108_comment'></div>悲怅于阿私陀仙。往郊祀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364108_comment'></div>惊起于大自在庙。或为童子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364108_comment'></div>或学声名。为讲武也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364108_comment'></div>箭塔箭井犹存。为角力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364108_comment'></div>象迹象坑仍在。受欲乐于十岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364108_comment'></div>现游观于四门。乐沙门身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364108_comment'></div>厌老病死。于是作瓶天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364108_comment'></div>以警觉彰伎女之丑容。净居天王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364108_comment'></div>以捧持跃车匿而严驾。逾春城于八夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364108_comment'></div>栖雪岭于六年。人辞怆恋主之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364108_comment'></div>马舐落连珠之泪。挥宝刀而落绀发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364108_comment'></div>塔起天宫。将衮服以贸皮衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364108_comment'></div>形参山鹿。叩林仙之所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364108_comment'></div>了世定之非真。食麦食酥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364108_comment'></div>降苦降乐。且瑶琴奏曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364108_comment'></div>必自中而曲成。佛果圆因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364108_comment'></div>亦假中而果满。由是择其处也过龙窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364108_comment'></div>浴其身也入连河。示其食也受难陀之乳糜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364108_comment'></div>示其座也受吉祥之茅草。以最后之胜体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364108_comment'></div>诣菩提之道场。圆解脱之深因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364108_comment'></div>登金刚之宝座。一百四十功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364108_comment'></div>不共二乘。八万四千法门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364108_comment'></div>高超十地。由是魔军威慑于慈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364108_comment'></div>愁怖旋归。媚女败毒于定心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364108_comment'></div>媸羸变质。于是坚牢地神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364108_comment'></div>踊跃而作證。虚空天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364108_comment'></div>展转而报知。类莲花而出水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364108_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1364108", 1364108, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>赫焕</span>无方。若桂月以悬空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364108_comment'></div>光明洞彻。经七日受提谓之蜜麨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364108_comment'></div>警以少小之言。垂一音授贾客之代归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364108_comment'></div>赐与人天之福。既成佛已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364108_comment'></div>观所化缘。悲二仙而不遇雷音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364108_comment'></div>喜五人而堪从法化。然以尘根昧劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364108_comment'></div>圣智渊深。顺其法则法不应根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364108_comment'></div>顺其根则根不达法。莫不为爱河之长溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364108_comment'></div>缘痴乐之所盲。苟不利于当闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364108_comment'></div>仍假言于入灭。于是忉利帝释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364108_comment'></div>云驱于三十三天。堪忍界王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364108_comment'></div>雾拥于一十八梵。头面作礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364108_comment'></div>致敬专精。请转法轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364108_comment'></div>劝随宜说。如来寻念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364108_comment'></div>善逝通规。顺古佛之嘉谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364108_comment'></div>应群机之鄙欲。于是十方佛现。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364108_comment'></div>同兴赞美之辞。一法乘分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364108_comment'></div>共创尘劳之域。由是起道树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364108_comment'></div>诣鹿园。三月调根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364108_comment'></div>五人得度。憍陈如悟慈尊之首唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364108_comment'></div>创解标名。舍利弗逢马胜以传言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364108_comment'></div>于途见谛。探菽氏继踵以师事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364108_comment'></div>率门属以同归。迦叶氏汇迹以降心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364108_comment'></div>领火徒而回席。莫不甘露洪澍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364108_comment'></div>摩泥普应。天界人界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364108_comment'></div>鹦林尸林。或鹭池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364108_comment'></div>或鹫岭。或海殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364108_comment'></div>或庵园。或猕猴池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364108_comment'></div>或火龙窟。或住波罗奈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364108_comment'></div>或居摩竭提。或依坚固林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364108_comment'></div>或止音乐树。或海滨楞伽顶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364108_comment'></div>或山际补陀岩。或迦兰陁竹园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364108_comment'></div>或舍卫国金地。或应念而空现。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364108_comment'></div>或没山而出宫。或说法假于六方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364108_comment'></div>或化身变为三尺。或掌覆而指变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364108_comment'></div>或光流而佛来。或一身并普集于众身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364108_comment'></div>或此界便明于他界。或变净而以净覆秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364108_comment'></div>或随俗而即俗明真。若空谷之荅响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364108_comment'></div>洪钟之待扣矣。其间所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364108_comment'></div>阿含四有。般若八空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364108_comment'></div>密严华严。佛藏地藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364108_comment'></div>思益天之请问。楞伽山之语心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364108_comment'></div>万行首楞严。一乘无量义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364108_comment'></div>大悲芬陁利。法炬陁罗尼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364108_comment'></div>无垢称之说经。须达拿之瑞应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364108_comment'></div>本事本生之别。讽颂重颂之殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364108_comment'></div>象马兔之三兽渡河。羊鹿牛之三车出宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364108_comment'></div>或谓之有空守中也。或谓之无转照持也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364108_comment'></div>或谓之顿也渐也。或谓之半也满也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364108_comment'></div>或无说而常说。或不闻而恒闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364108_comment'></div>或保任而可凭。或加被而不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364108_comment'></div>无小而不大。无边而不中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364108_comment'></div>三乘同入一佛乘。三性同归一法性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364108_comment'></div>真可谓父母孩孺。导师险夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364108_comment'></div>悬日月于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_96_1364108", 1364108, "Clauses/192/Comments/0")'>幽宵</span>。布舟航于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_96_1364108", 1364108, "Clauses/193/Comments/0")'>幻海</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364108_comment'></div>为云为雨。使枯槁以还滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364108_comment'></div>为救为归。指穷途于寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364108_comment'></div>暨乎所作已办。功成不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364108_comment'></div>将返本以还源。类薪尽而火灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364108_comment'></div>由是指力地。诣金河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364108_comment'></div>光流面门。相惊尘刹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364108_comment'></div>山摇地动。俱兴苦痛之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364108_comment'></div>异类变容。同现奢花之血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364108_comment'></div>受纯陀之后供。纳毗夜之密言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364108_comment'></div>唱四德以显三伊。指万有而归一性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364108_comment'></div>酬多罗迦叶四十二。请问已周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364108_comment'></div>度须跂陁罗八十一。化缘将毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364108_comment'></div>破十仙之横计。使获朝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364108_comment'></div>建四塔之崇规。遐滋末叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364108_comment'></div>将欲明有为之有灭。表无相以无生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364108_comment'></div>上升金刚身。往复虚空界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364108_comment'></div>日月其犹坠落。萤光如何久留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364108_comment'></div>诫有常身。使无放逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364108_comment'></div>于是还登玉座。首卧鹤林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364108_comment'></div>遍游三昧之门。将复一真之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364108_comment'></div>逆入顺入。全超半超。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364108_comment'></div>依四禅之等持。湛三点之圆寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364108_comment'></div>是时也。人天叫躄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364108_comment'></div>鸟兽哀号。飘风骤云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364108_comment'></div>山吼波逆。案轮王之古式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364108_comment'></div>方俟葬仪。命力士以捧持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364108_comment'></div>竟无能动。由是金棺自举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364108_comment'></div>绕拘尸之大城。宝炬不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364108_comment'></div>驻阇维之盛礼。莫不生怨在于王舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364108_comment'></div>创结梦于十号。慈尊大迦叶远下鸡峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364108_comment'></div>获瞻礼于千辐轮足毕。以兜罗致氎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364108_comment'></div>圣火自焚。爇王众旃檀之薪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364108_comment'></div>注帝释全瓶之水。彼愿力犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364108_comment'></div>悲心尚熏。碎金刚之胜身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364108_comment'></div>为舍利之遗骨。于是八国严卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364108_comment'></div>四岳肃容。各自持于金坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364108_comment'></div>竞归兴于宝塔。于是若牙若发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364108_comment'></div>迦叶婆礼于忉利天宫。或炭或灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364108_comment'></div>无忧王建于赡部洲界。若乃金言道在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364108_comment'></div>尘劫法存。象王去而象子随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364108_comment'></div>一灯灭而一灯续。莫不大迦叶云迎千众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364108_comment'></div>阿难陀雷吼三轮。商那表定于未来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364108_comment'></div>鞠多化筹而盈室。始自坏梁之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364108_comment'></div>终乎流乳之徵。瓶器异而水必同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364108_comment'></div>灯点殊而光终一。是以大乘之真空妙有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364108_comment'></div>文殊弥勒异其宗。小乘而分氎㭊金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364108_comment'></div>上座大众元其部。或十支宏阐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364108_comment'></div>或千部郁兴。马鸣龙树继其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364108_comment'></div>无著天亲播其美。或提婆凿眸而作器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364108_comment'></div>陈那吼石以飞声。或百偈齐祛于外宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364108_comment'></div>或十师翊赞于遗颂。或闻经而夜升兜率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364108_comment'></div>或待佛而窟寄修罗。或剑誓首以要期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364108_comment'></div>或象驮金而请释。或赏能而食邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364108_comment'></div>或得胜而建幢。或论般若之理也名灯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364108_comment'></div>或究俱舍之非也名雹。莫不殊途异辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364108_comment'></div>终会一源。自有及空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364108_comment'></div>咸归万液。自商周见虹贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364108_comment'></div>炎汉梦金人。教及神州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364108_comment'></div>声流华夏。勃叨生季世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364108_comment'></div>获奉真谭。维陆续而以叙金言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364108_comment'></div>在飘零而不逢玉相。见闻尽尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364108_comment'></div>宗致昭然。盖委遗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364108_comment'></div>不复备而言也。乃为铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364108_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_160_1364108'>化起从本源。功成应贤劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364108_comment'></div>万行显真宗。三祇积鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364108_comment'></div>为法出于世。降灵示分胁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364108_comment'></div>眉横天帝弓。目带青莲叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364108_comment'></div>仙师相垂泪。天神争捧接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364108_comment'></div>灌顶当在宫。飞轮化弥帖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364108_comment'></div>宗承天日贵。象贯师子颊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364108_comment'></div>善教谁与传。抨弹独豪侠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364108_comment'></div>游观惊老死。逾城弃臣妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364108_comment'></div>落发亲宝刀。贸衣遇群猎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364108_comment'></div>寄迹狎麋鹿。苦身示羸怯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364108_comment'></div>食糜人尽知。坐草魔方慑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364108_comment'></div>洁若莲出水。明逾镜开匣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364108_comment'></div>山海类高深。云雷等辞捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364108_comment'></div>三时教弥阐。万类根自惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364108_comment'></div>四问聊欲酬。十仙度相蹑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364108_comment'></div>补处记慈氏。遗文嘱迦叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364108_comment'></div>卧树徒再春。香薪已焚氎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364108_comment'></div>悲心及绵远。舍利光郁烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364108_comment'></div>独我生后时。馀渡幸沾涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364108_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_180_1364108_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　在虢州参军任.夏旱,虢州长史王嶷祈雨,为作《祭石堤山神文》、《祭石堤女郎神文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（罗振玉《永丰乡人杂著续编·王子安集佚文》壬戌(1922)刊本。《罗振玉学术论著集》第五集《王子安集佚文》上海古籍出版社2010年版。）</span>《祭石堤女郎神文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（罗振玉《永丰乡人杂著续编·王子安集佚文》壬戌(1922)刊本。《罗振玉学术论著集》第五集《王子安集佚文》上海古籍出版社2010年版。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　夏,宴于宋之问宅,作《夏日宴宋五官宅观画障序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷6第194页。）</span><div id='poem_1364083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏日宴宋五官宅观画障序</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364083")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364083'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364083'>宋五官芝庭袭誉。盛文史于三冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364083_comment'></div>桂幄凝欢。照绮罗于九夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364083_comment'></div>樽浮绿蚁。每披仙雾之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364083_comment'></div>障列青牛。更写行云之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364083_comment'></div>尔其龙编绣质。贝锦分花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364083_comment'></div>隐映楼台。比窗帘之在旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364083_comment'></div>参差花叶。若桃李之恒春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364083_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364083", 1364083, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>楚媛</span>调弦。韩娥对酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364083_comment'></div>虹桥度幔。鹊镜临妆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364083_comment'></div>佩引琅玕。讵动怀风之韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364083_comment'></div>鞍回玳瑁。唯奔逐日之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364083_comment'></div>鱼鸟冷而相亲。泉石纷而在玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364083_comment'></div>宋家斯近。难别谢于登垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364083_comment'></div>秦氏未遥。自堪留于驻马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364083_comment'></div>惊鸿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364083", 1364083, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>擅美</span>。丹青贵近质之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364083_comment'></div>吐凤标华。宫徵得缘情之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364083_comment'></div>递扬笔妙。式畅辞端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364083_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1364083_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　冬,因杀官奴曹达被拘审。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>　在狱整理《周易发挥》、《次论语》、《合论》、《百里昌言》等书稿,诸书皆佚。作品：《续书序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷9第279页。王勃入狱地,权系于虢州。）</span><div id='poem_1364066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>续书序</a><span class='authorDate'>（674年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364066")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364066'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364066'>叙曰。书以记言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364066_comment'></div>其来尚矣。越在三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364066_comment'></div>左史职之。百官以理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364066_comment'></div>万人以察。扬于王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364066_comment'></div>用实大焉。苟非可以燮理情性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364066_comment'></div>平章邦国。敷彝伦而叙要道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364066_comment'></div>察时变而经王猷。树皇极之纲维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364066_comment'></div>资生灵之视听。皆可略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364066_comment'></div>昔者仲尼之述书也。将以究事业之通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364066_comment'></div>而正性命之理。故曰吾欲托之空言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364066_comment'></div>不如附之行事。道德仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364066_comment'></div>于是乎明。刑政礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364066_comment'></div>于是乎出。非先王之德行不敢传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364066_comment'></div>非先王之法言不敢道。纪千数百岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364066_comment'></div>断自唐虞。迄于商周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364066_comment'></div>风流所存。百篇而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364066_comment'></div>以此见圣人言约理举。神明不劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364066_comment'></div>而体时务之撰矣。故能法象天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364066_comment'></div>同符易。借前箸于筌蹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364066_comment'></div>驱后生于轨物。密而显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364066_comment'></div>宏而奥。久而弥新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364066_comment'></div>用而不竭。非古之聪明圣智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364066_comment'></div>元览博达。孰能为此哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364066_comment'></div>孔安国曰。帝王之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364066_comment'></div>坦然明白。可举而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364066_comment'></div>嗟乎。其言甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364066_comment'></div>可使南面称圣人之后矣。自时以降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364066_comment'></div>史述陵迟。人自为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364066_comment'></div>标指失中。陈事乱而无当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364066_comment'></div>制理参而不一。由是大典散而人文乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364066_comment'></div>是非繁而取舍谬。与夫古先哲人制述之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364066_comment'></div>不其疏乎。我先君文中子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364066_comment'></div>实秉睿懿。生于隋末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364066_comment'></div>睹后作之违方。忧异端之害正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364066_comment'></div>乃喟然曰。宣尼既没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364066_comment'></div>文不在兹乎。遂约大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364066_comment'></div>删旧章。续诗为三百六十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364066_comment'></div>考伪乱而修元经。正礼乐以旌后王之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364066_comment'></div>述易赞以申先师之旨。经始汉魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364066_comment'></div>迄于有晋。择其典物宜于教者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364066_comment'></div>续书为百二十篇。而广大悉备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364066_comment'></div>嗟乎。贤圣之述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364066_comment'></div>岂多为哉。噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364066_comment'></div>亦足垂训作则。冒天下之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364066_comment'></div>如斯而已矣。当时门人百千数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364066_comment'></div>董薛之徒。并受其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364066_comment'></div>遭代丧乱。未行于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364066_comment'></div>年永久。稍见残缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364066_comment'></div>贞观中。太原府君考诸六经之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364066_comment'></div>则忘其小序。其有录而无篇者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364066_comment'></div>又十六焉。呜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364066_comment'></div>兹不可复见矣。家君钦若丕烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364066_comment'></div>图终休绪。乃例六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364066_comment'></div>次礼乐。叙中说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364066_comment'></div>明易赞。永惟保守前训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364066_comment'></div>大克敷遗后人。勃兄弟五六冠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364066_comment'></div>童子六七。祇祇怡怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364066_comment'></div>讲问伏渐之日久矣。躬奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1364066", 1364066, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>成训</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364066_comment'></div>家传异闻。犹恐不得门而入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364066_comment'></div>才之不逮至远也。是用励精激愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364066_comment'></div>宵吟昼咏。庶几乎学而知之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364066_comment'></div>其修身慎行。恐辱先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364066_comment'></div>岂声禄是殉。前人之不继是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364066_comment'></div>间者承命为百二十篇作序。而兼当补修其阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364066_comment'></div>爰考众籍。共参<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1364066", 1364066, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>奥旨</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364066_comment'></div>泉源浩然。罔识攸济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364066_comment'></div>呜乎小子。何敢以当之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364066_comment'></div>其尽心力乎。始自总章二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364066_comment'></div>洎乎咸亨五年。刊写文就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364066_comment'></div>定成百二十篇。勒成二十五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364066_comment'></div>昔者文中子曰。汉魏之礼乐未足称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364066_comment'></div>其书不可废也。尚有近古之对议存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364066_comment'></div>制诏册则几乎典诰矣。后之达悟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364066_comment'></div>将有得于斯文乎。于时龙集阉茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364066_comment'></div>勉踵前修。在大唐御天下之五十七祀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364066_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_75_1364066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年8月</a>　八月,遇赦,出狱,除名.向其父呈《上百里昌言疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷6第187页。）</span><div id='poem_1364048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上百里昌言疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（674年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364048")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364048'>勃言。乡人奉五月一日诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364048_comment'></div>子弟各陈百里之术宣于政者。承命惶灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364048_comment'></div>伏增悲悚。勃闻古人有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364048_comment'></div>明君不能畜无用之臣。慈父不能爱无用之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364048_comment'></div>何则。以其无益于国而累于家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364048_comment'></div>呜呼。如勃尚何言哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364048_comment'></div>辱亲可谓深矣。诚宜灰身粉骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364048_comment'></div>以谢君父。复何面目以谈天下之事哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364048_comment'></div>所以迟回忍耻而已者。徒以虚死不如立节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364048_comment'></div>苟殒不如成名。悔过傥存于已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364048_comment'></div>为仁不假于物。是以孟明不屑三奔之诮而罢匡秦之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364048_comment'></div>冯异不耻一败之失而摧辅汉之气。故其志卒行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364048_comment'></div>其功卒就也。此言虽小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364048_comment'></div>可以喻大。此勃所以怀既往而不咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364048_comment'></div>指将来而骏奔。割万恨于生涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364048_comment'></div>进一篑于平地者。今大人上延国谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364048_comment'></div>远宰边邑。出三江而浮五湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364048_comment'></div>越东瓯而度南海。嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364048_comment'></div>此皆勃之罪也。无所逃于天地之间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364048_comment'></div>然勃尝闻之大易曰。人之所助者信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364048_comment'></div>天之所助者顺也。是以君子不以否屈而易方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364048_comment'></div>故屈而终泰。忠臣不以困穷而丧志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364048_comment'></div>故穷而必亨。今交趾虽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364048_comment'></div>还珠者尝用之矣。书不云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364048_comment'></div>弗虑胡获。弗为胡成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364048_comment'></div>不胜愤激之至。谨上百里昌言一部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364048_comment'></div>列为十八篇。分为上下卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364048_comment'></div>庶竭私款。少裨公政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364048_comment'></div>追思罪戾。若投冰谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364048_comment'></div>谨奉言疏不备。勃再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364048_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1364048_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>　为西京太原寺范姓律师作《四分律宗记序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷9第279页。）</span><div id='poem_1364068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四分律宗记序</a><span class='authorDate'>（674年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364068")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364068'>昔在调御。利见迦维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364068_comment'></div>光宅<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>净都</span>。抚临法界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364068_comment'></div>抑扬垢路之业。以疆理情田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364068_comment'></div>阐导毗尼之藏。以堤防性海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364068_comment'></div>二边云彻。方知实相之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364068_comment'></div>十刹风行。乃识真如之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364068_comment'></div>将使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>龙象</span>缁服。维明克允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364068_comment'></div>鹙鹭元盟。有耻且格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364068_comment'></div>五篇垂范。岂同训夏之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364068_comment'></div>七聚分宗。宁比歌虞之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364068_comment'></div>功存离欲。道在降魔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364068_comment'></div>仙苑创基。因善果以调物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364068_comment'></div>提河灭迹。凭净戒以为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364068_comment'></div>诚拯溺之舟航。而御黠之衔策者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364068_comment'></div>故能庄严百福。粉绘三身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364068_comment'></div>摧憍慢山。拔生死树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364068_comment'></div>覆篑菩萨之道。滥觞正觉之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364068_comment'></div>除<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>惑箭</span>而断爱枝。销<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>恚刀</span>而解<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/35/Comments/1")'>疑网</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364068_comment'></div>自银棺掩耀。金杖殊珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364068_comment'></div>五师烟腾。四分云谲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364068_comment'></div>波离睿旨。明而更明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364068_comment'></div>饮光妙迹。盛而愈盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364068_comment'></div>其后卑摩覃思。犹沈赤水之辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364068_comment'></div>惠远研精。尚玷元岩之彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364068_comment'></div>遂使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>琼编</span>浩汗。利涉迷于要津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364068_comment'></div>瑶轴纷纶。登高暗于飞陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364068_comment'></div>熟习者博而寡用。志学者劳而少功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364068_comment'></div>七众所以迟回。八部由其太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364068_comment'></div>丕应冥发。睿感潜融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364068_comment'></div>爰挺异才。式扶象训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364068_comment'></div>有西京太原寺索律师。俗姓范氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364068_comment'></div>其先南阳人也。殷霸洪允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364068_comment'></div>周藩茂族。八鸾与四牡竞驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364068_comment'></div>紫绘与青緺叠照。六军卿冑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364068_comment'></div>绩著于钟彝。三传儒门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364068_comment'></div>业流于训诂。律师冲襟霞映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364068_comment'></div>峻局霜凄。筠抱显于髫龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364068_comment'></div>兰芬凝于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>丱齿</span>。由是糠秕礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364068_comment'></div>锱铢名教。以尧舜为尘劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364068_comment'></div>以周孔为桎梏。爰依白法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364068_comment'></div>遂托元徒。探鹫岭之微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364068_comment'></div>得龙宫之秘藏。咸亨之祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364068_comment'></div>椒房谅阴。舍槐里而构庵园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364068_comment'></div>因金穴而开银地。伽蓝肇建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364068_comment'></div>号曰太原。明阳所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364068_comment'></div>咸收时望。自价隆康会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364068_comment'></div>誉重摩腾。竺法猷之苦节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364068_comment'></div>支道林之远致。将何以发明禅宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364068_comment'></div>光应纶言。律师乃以道众羽仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364068_comment'></div>释门栋干。粤自宏济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364068_comment'></div>来游太原。经行德人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364068_comment'></div>于兹为盛。既而惧六和之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>紊绪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364068_comment'></div>悼三聚之乖宗。稽法令之遗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364068_comment'></div>讨惠猷之旧业。网罗近护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364068_comment'></div>吞含觉明。原始要终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364068_comment'></div>探赜索隐。芟夷疣赘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364068_comment'></div>剪截<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>骈枝</span>。收<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>绝代</span>之精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364068_comment'></div>诘往圣之纰缪。葭灰屡变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364068_comment'></div>槐燧骤迁。开遮持犯之异同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364068_comment'></div>废立止作之轻重。故以该<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1364068", 1364068, "Clauses/119/Comments/0")'>象牙</span>之扇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364068_comment'></div>穷贝叶之图。钻研刊削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364068_comment'></div>五载而就。名曰开四分律宗记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364068_comment'></div>凡十卷三十七万六百三十言。律师又以为仲尼述易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364068_comment'></div>申妙典于系辞。元凯谈经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364068_comment'></div>托馀文于释例。爰因多暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364068_comment'></div>更辑旧章。牢笼秘察之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364068_comment'></div>发挥沈郁之旨。名曰开四分律宗拾遗钞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364068_comment'></div>凡十卷四十万馀言。所以裨助三明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364068_comment'></div>抑扬四谛。宏八正之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364068_comment'></div>成一家之言。庶使众善雷奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364068_comment'></div>群疑雾敛。照欢戚之两镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364068_comment'></div>荡欣忧之二瓶。凭此戒田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364068_comment'></div>方跻定境。岂直功周沙甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364068_comment'></div>道制铁围而已哉。弟子才非元度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364068_comment'></div>识劣真长。本乏淩云之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364068_comment'></div>虚荷弥天之眷。揄扬盛烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364068_comment'></div>顾孙绰而多惭。归依胜侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364068_comment'></div>仰郤愔而自励。辄牵庸陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364068_comment'></div>轻序德音。岂比夫公理昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364068_comment'></div>资缪袭之引。太冲作赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364068_comment'></div>假士安之谈。盖所谓观豹而识班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364068_comment'></div>闻乐而窃抃者矣。故曰四分律宗记序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364068_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1364068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>　为父亲筹集南行赴任经费,并作《上郎都督启》以日后呈于交州都督郎馀庆。<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷4第143页。）</span><div id='poem_1364063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上郎都督启</a><span class='authorDate'>（674年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364063")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364063'>某启。某闻古之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364063_comment'></div>重神交而贵道合者。以其得披心胸而尽志义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364063_comment'></div>是以叔牙苟在。管仲分多而不贪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364063_comment'></div>无知尚存。陈平受谤而非罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364063_comment'></div>何则。达其趣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364063_comment'></div>能申其迹。收其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364063_comment'></div>能让其细也。今某东鄙之一书生耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364063_comment'></div>少怀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364063", 1364063, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>耿亮</span>。颇慕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364063", 1364063, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>高烈</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364063_comment'></div>俯仰相得。则屠博可游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364063_comment'></div>造次不谐。则轩冕异路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364063_comment'></div>蒙君侯国士之遇。受君侯长者之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364063_comment'></div>缱绻谈谑。殷勤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364063", 1364063, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>诲诱</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364063_comment'></div>今有情而不告。是不尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364063_comment'></div>有窘而不托。是有疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364063_comment'></div>将恐季布无侣于后叶。孙膑独称于前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364063_comment'></div>嗟乎。可以竭诚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364063_comment'></div>敢不尽言乎。勃家大人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364063_comment'></div>天下独行者也。性恶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364063", 1364063, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>储敛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364063_comment'></div>家无儋石。自延国谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364063_comment'></div>远宰边隅。常愿全雅志于暮齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364063_comment'></div>扬素风于下邑。而道里夐遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364063_comment'></div>资粮窘鲜。秩寡钟釜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364063_comment'></div>债盈数万。此勃所以侧目扼腕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364063_comment'></div>临深履薄。庶逢知已之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364063_comment'></div>以成大人之峻节也。古人有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364063_comment'></div>富观其所与。贫观其所取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364063_comment'></div>又曰。损有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364063_comment'></div>补不足。于君侯何如哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364063_comment'></div>然则定其交而后求。敢无愧已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364063_comment'></div>易其心而后语。夫何饰焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364063_comment'></div>赈给之义。既惟其常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364063_comment'></div>厚薄之差。伏希俯访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364063_comment'></div>轻尘视听。伏增兢惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364063_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1364063_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='abbea58be5ef4b6484f49d811a7ef55b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("abbea58be5ef4b6484f49d811a7ef55b");'><span id='abbea58be5ef4b6484f49d811a7ef55b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>，23岁</div><div id='abbea58be5ef4b6484f49d811a7ef55b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>　时高宗在洛阳.秋,曾到洛阳,至毕国公宅参预饯别道王李诱的宴席,有《秋晚入洛于毕公宅别道王宴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷8第255页。）</span><div id='poem_1364103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364103?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋晚入洛于毕公宅别道王宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364103")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364103'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364103'>下官才不旷俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364103_comment'></div>宠不动时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364103_comment'></div>充帝王之万姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364103_comment'></div>预乾坤之一物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364103_comment'></div>早师周礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364103_comment'></div>偶爱儒宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364103_comment'></div>晚读老庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364103_comment'></div>动谐真性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364103_comment'></div>进非干物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364103_comment'></div>自疏朝市之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364103_comment'></div>退不邀荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364103_comment'></div>谁识王侯之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364103_comment'></div>散琴樽于北阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364103_comment'></div>喜耕凿于东陂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364103_comment'></div>野老披荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364103_comment'></div>暂辞幽涧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364103_comment'></div>山人卖药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364103_comment'></div>忽至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364103", 1364103, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>神州</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364103_comment'></div>惊帝室之威灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364103_comment'></div>伟皇居之壮丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364103_comment'></div>朝游魏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364103_comment'></div>见轩冕于南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364103_comment'></div>暮宿灵台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364103_comment'></div>闻弦歌于北里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364103_comment'></div>交情独放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364103_comment'></div>已厌人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364103_comment'></div>野性时违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364103_comment'></div>少留都下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364103_comment'></div>道王以天孙之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364103_comment'></div>分曲阜之新基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364103_comment'></div>毕公以帝室之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364103_comment'></div>拥平阳之旧馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364103_comment'></div>迹尘钟鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364103_comment'></div>思在江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364103_comment'></div>居荣命于中朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364103_comment'></div>接风期于下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364103_comment'></div>绿縢朱绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364103_comment'></div>且混以萝裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364103_comment'></div>列榭崇轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364103_comment'></div>坐均于蓬户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364103_comment'></div>宾主由其莫辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364103_comment'></div>语默于是同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364103_comment'></div>终大王之乐善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364103_comment'></div>备将军之揖客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364103_comment'></div>是日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364103_comment'></div>云繁雨骤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364103_comment'></div>气爽风驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364103_comment'></div>高秋九月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364103_comment'></div>王畿千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364103_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364103", 1364103, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>高扃</span>向术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364103_comment'></div>似元礼之龙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364103_comment'></div>甲第临衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364103_comment'></div>有当时之驿骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364103_comment'></div>英王入座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364103_comment'></div>牢醴还陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364103_comment'></div>高士临筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364103_comment'></div>樵苏不爨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364103_comment'></div>是非双遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364103_comment'></div>自然天地之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364103_comment'></div>荣贱两忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364103_comment'></div>何必山林之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364103_comment'></div>元谈清论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364103_comment'></div>泉石纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364103_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1364103", 1364103, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>雄笔</span>壮词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364103_comment'></div>烟霞照灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364103_comment'></div>既而神驰象外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364103_comment'></div>宴洽寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364103_comment'></div>白露下而南亭虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364103_comment'></div>苍烟生而北林晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364103_comment'></div>鶢鶋始望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364103_comment'></div>不及牲牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364103_comment'></div>麋鹿长怀。<div id='poem_sentence_73_1364103_comment'></div>倦城市之尘埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364103_comment'></div>游子横琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364103_comment'></div>忆汀洲之杜若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364103_comment'></div>况乎迹不皆遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364103_comment'></div>时不再来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364103_comment'></div>属<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1364103", 1364103, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>宸驾</span>之方旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364103_comment'></div>值群公之毕从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364103_comment'></div>洛城风景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364103_comment'></div>此会无期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364103_comment'></div>敢抒重襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364103_comment'></div>爰疏短引。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364103_comment'></div>其辞云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_134_1364103_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年</a>　夏,经洛阳,随即沿大运河南下。<br /></div>

-----title
万荣（万泉）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fcb7f345a12643c2811669edf437efc1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fcb7f345a12643c2811669edf437efc1");'><span id='fcb7f345a12643c2811669edf437efc1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>，25岁</div><div id='fcb7f345a12643c2811669edf437efc1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>　冬,曾至汾阴县送友人韦少府,作《冬日羁游汾阴送韦少府入洛序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷8第239页。张谱作"河中府汾阴县",据谭图改为"绛州万泉"）</span><div id='poem_1364106' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364106' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364106?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬日羁游汾阴送韦少府入洛序</a><span class='authorDate'>（667年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364106")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364106_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364106'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364106'>游汾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364106", 1364106, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>胜壤</span>。楼船高汉帝之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364106_comment'></div>卜洛名都。城邑辨周公之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364106_comment'></div>仰天文而窥日月。虽共光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364106_comment'></div>凭地理而考山川。即殊南北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364106_comment'></div>韦少府玉山四照。珠胎一色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364106_comment'></div>纵横振<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364106", 1364106, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>锋颖</span>之才。吐纳积江湖之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364106_comment'></div>子云笔札。拥鸾凤于行间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364106_comment'></div>孙楚文词。列宫商于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364106", 1364106, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>调下</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364106_comment'></div>牵丝一命。披林野而随班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364106_comment'></div>考绩三年。指兰台而赴选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364106_comment'></div>移征驾。背长亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364106_comment'></div>地隔风烟。人离岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364106_comment'></div>寒原冠盖。既同斟桂之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364106_comment'></div>歧路风尘。即断惊蓬之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364106_comment'></div>下官诗书<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364106", 1364106, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>拓落</span>。羽翮摧颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364106_comment'></div>朝廷无立锥之处。丘园有括囊之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364106_comment'></div>山中事业。暂到渔樵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364106_comment'></div>天下栖迟。少留城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364106_comment'></div>忽逢萍水。对云雨以无聊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364106_comment'></div>倍切穷途。抚形骸而何托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364106_comment'></div>于时冰霜裂地。星象回天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364106_comment'></div>朔风动而关塞寒。明月下而楼台曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364106_comment'></div>各题一字。传之两乡云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364106_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1364106_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临猗（桑泉）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a76f92570e05427885f8ff410f95c429_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a76f92570e05427885f8ff410f95c429");'><span id='a76f92570e05427885f8ff410f95c429_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年</a>，26岁</div><div id='a76f92570e05427885f8ff410f95c429' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年</a>　春,由龙门出发,随父赴交趾.（按,两唐书均作“省父”）至桑泉,作《春夜桑泉别王少府序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷9第262页。）</span><div id='poem_1364080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364080?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春日桑泉别王少府序</a><span class='authorDate'>（675年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364080")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364080_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364080'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364080'>下官以穷途万里。动脂辖以长驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364080_comment'></div>王公以倾饯百壶。别芳筵而促兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364080_comment'></div>是以青阳半序。明月中宵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364080_comment'></div>离亭拥花草之芳。别馆积琴歌之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364080_comment'></div>去留欢尽。动息悲来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364080_comment'></div>惜投分之几何。恨知音之忽间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364080_comment'></div>他乡握手。自伤关塞之春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364080_comment'></div>异县<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364080", 1364080, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>分襟</span>。意切悽惶之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364080_comment'></div>既而星河渐落。烟雾仍开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364080_comment'></div>高林静而霜鸟飞。长路晓而征骖动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364080_comment'></div>含情不拜。空伫听于南昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364080_comment'></div>挥涕无言。请投文于西候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364080_comment'></div>因探一字。四韵成篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364080_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1364080_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_sentence_0_1364099_comment'></div>星分<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>翼轸</span>。地接<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>龙光</span>射牛斗之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364099_comment'></div><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_5_1364099_comment'></div>台隍枕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>夷夏</span>之交。宾主尽<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_13_1364099_comment'></div>童子何知。躬逢胜饯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364099_comment'></div>时维九月。序属三秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364099_comment'></div><span onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>二难</span>并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364099_comment'></div>穷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>睇盼</span>于中天。极娱游于暇日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364099_comment'></div>天高地迥。觉宇宙之无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364099_comment'></div>兴尽悲来。识盈虚之有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364099_comment'></div>望长安于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>日下</span>。指吴会于云间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364099_comment'></div>地势极而南溟深。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>天柱</span>高而北辰远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364099_comment'></div>关山难越。谁悲失路之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364099_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>萍水相逢</span>。尽是他乡之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364099_comment'></div>怀帝阍而不见。奉宣室以何年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364099_comment'></div>嗟乎。时运不齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364099_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>命途</span>多舛。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>冯唐易老</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364099_comment'></div>李广难封。屈贾谊于长沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364099_comment'></div>非无圣主。窜梁鸿于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>海曲</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364099_comment'></div>岂乏明时。所赖君子安贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364099_comment'></div>达人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>知命</span>。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>老当益壮</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364099_comment'></div>宁知白首之心。穷且益坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364099_comment'></div>不坠青云之志。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>酌贪泉</span>而觉爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364099_comment'></div>处涸辙而犹欢。北海虽赊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364099_comment'></div>扶摇可接。东隅已逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364099_comment'></div>桑榆非晚。孟尝高洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364099_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/110/Comments/0")'>空怀</span>报国之情。阮籍猖狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364099_comment'></div>岂效<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>穷途之哭</span>。勃三尺微命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364099_comment'></div>一介书生。无路<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>请缨</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364099_comment'></div>等终军之弱冠。有怀投笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364099_comment'></div>慕宗悫之长风。舍簪笏于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/119/Comments/0")'>百龄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364099_comment'></div>奉晨昏于万里。非谢家之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>宝树</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364099_comment'></div>接孟氏之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>芳邻</span>。他日<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/123/Comments/0")'>趋庭</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364099_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/124/Comments/0")'>叨陪</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/124/Comments/1")'>鲤对</span>。今辰捧袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364099_comment'></div>喜托龙门。杨意不逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364099_comment'></div>抚淩云而自惜。钟期既遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364099_comment'></div>奏流水以何惭。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364099_comment'></div>胜地不常。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>盛筵难再</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364099_comment'></div>兰亭已矣。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>梓泽</span>邱墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364099_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/136/Comments/0")'>临别赠言</span>。幸承恩于伟饯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364099_comment'></div>登高作赋。是所望于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>群公</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364099_comment'></div>敢竭鄙怀。恭疏短引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364099_comment'></div>一言均赋。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/143/Comments/0")'>四韵</span>俱成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364099_comment'></div>请洒潘江。各倾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364099", 1364099, "Clauses/145/Comments/0")'>陆海</span>云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364099_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1364099_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_8863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8863?labeling=true' "poem_title_8863")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_8863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8863'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8863'>滕王<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8863", 8863, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>高阁</span>临江渚，佩玉鸣鸾罢歌舞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8863'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8863", 8863, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>画栋</span>朝飞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8863", 8863, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>南浦</span>云，珠帘暮捲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8863", 8863, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>西山</span>雨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8863'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8863", 8863, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>闲云</span>潭影日悠悠，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8863", 8863, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>物换星移</span>几度秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8863'>阁中<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8863", 8863, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>帝子</span>今何在，槛外长江空<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8863", 8863, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>自流</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8863'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8863_comment'></div></div><div -----end



-----title
赣州（虔州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8397ce2c9b0d47bfaca63a0eec8105ca_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8397ce2c9b0d47bfaca63a0eec8105ca");'><span id='8397ce2c9b0d47bfaca63a0eec8105ca_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年</a>，26岁</div><div id='8397ce2c9b0d47bfaca63a0eec8105ca' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年10月</a>　十月,过虔州,作《为虔州诸官祭故长史文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（罗振玉《永丰乡人杂著续编·王子安集佚文》壬戌(1922)刊本。《罗振玉学术论著集》第五集《王子安集佚文》上海古籍出版社2010年版。）</span><br /></div>
