-----title
广州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d6769a2c08eb451ca446ea21302e0914_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d6769a2c08eb451ca446ea21302e0914");'><span id='d6769a2c08eb451ca446ea21302e0914_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年</a>，26岁</div><div id='d6769a2c08eb451ca446ea21302e0914' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>十一月,到广州,作《鞶鉴图铭序》、《广州宝庄严寺舍利塔碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷9第288页。张谱云广州故治在南海县,在今广州市.谭图所示今广州仍为广州,据谭图改。）</span>《广州宝庄严寺舍利塔碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪贤度校点《王子安集注》上海古籍出版社1995年版卷18第521页。）</span><div id='poem_1364070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364070?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鞶鉴图铭序</a><span class='authorDate'>（675年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364070")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364070_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364070'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364070'>上元二年岁次乙亥十有一月庚午朔七日丙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364070_comment'></div>子将之交阯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364070_comment'></div>旅次南海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364070_comment'></div>有好事者以转轮钩枝八花鉴铭示子云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364070_comment'></div>当今之才妇人作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364070_comment'></div>观其藻丽反覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364070_comment'></div>文字荣回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364070_comment'></div>句读曲屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364070_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364070", 1364070, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>韵调</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364070", 1364070, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>高雅</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364070_comment'></div>有陈规起讽之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364070_comment'></div>可以作鉴前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364070_comment'></div>辉映将来者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364070_comment'></div>昔孔诗十兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364070_comment'></div>不遗卫姜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364070_comment'></div>江篇拟古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364070_comment'></div>无隔班媛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364070_comment'></div>盖以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364070", 1364070, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>超俊</span>颖拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364070_comment'></div>同符君子者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364070_comment'></div>呜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364070_comment'></div>何勤非戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364070_comment'></div>何述非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364070_comment'></div>风律句存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364070_comment'></div>士女何算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364070_comment'></div>聊抚镜以长想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364070_comment'></div>遂援笔而作叙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364070_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364135?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广州宝庄严寺舍利塔碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（675年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18262, "初唐", "王勃", "poem_title_1364135")'>王勃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364135'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364135'>昔者万人疾疫。神农<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>鞭草</span>而救之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364135_comment'></div>四维<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>凋瘵</span>。夏禹刊木以除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364135_comment'></div>岂非物外其性。则道功出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364135_comment'></div>事愆其和。则任迹著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364135_comment'></div>傍稽素篆。仰叩元扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364135_comment'></div>即时义而规大觉。因彝伦而伫真谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364135_comment'></div>向使三灾克殄。八正咸修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364135_comment'></div>人握<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>戒珠</span>。家藏宝印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364135_comment'></div>则三十二相不可得而视也。八万四千法不可得而闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364135_comment'></div>然则圣人以运否而生。神机以道丧而显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364135_comment'></div>况迦维授手。摩竭推心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364135_comment'></div>高张妙用之功。自拯横流之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364135_comment'></div>盖不获已。岂徒然哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364135_comment'></div>故能业拥大千。化形真一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364135_comment'></div>由乐推而起七觉。因来苏而坐三昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364135_comment'></div>发挥五演。以寂灭为身常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364135_comment'></div>提挈四流。用慈悲为化迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364135_comment'></div>黑风宵遁。波旬忘反噬之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364135_comment'></div>绿沼晨开。天常识问津之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364135_comment'></div>括夷涂于九相。蹇步其安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364135_comment'></div>纳慧晷于重昏。迷方自晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364135_comment'></div>大矣哉。应物而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364135_comment'></div>兴运而终。至自于昆冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364135_comment'></div>复归于无物。虽金沙宴驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364135_comment'></div>双林无可作之期。而玉牒遗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364135_comment'></div>六尘有经行之俗。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>象法</span>不可以无主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364135_comment'></div>微言不可以遂丧。六千罗汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364135_comment'></div>竞结香缘。五百仙人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364135_comment'></div>分开<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>讲肆</span>。星龛月殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364135_comment'></div>俄盈震旦之墟。凤刹蜺旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364135_comment'></div>坐遍阎浮之域。屈伸阖辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364135_comment'></div>其道矣哉。夫宝庄严寺舍利塔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364135_comment'></div>梁大同三年内道场沙门昙俗法师所立也。其琅邪贵族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364135_comment'></div>则汉庭峻节。祖德犹传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364135_comment'></div>梁甫高吟。嘉声未远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364135_comment'></div>法师夙登真地。深入慧门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364135_comment'></div>照果业于三明。拂尘劳于八解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364135_comment'></div>羊车绮岁。悬欣半月之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364135_comment'></div>凤阁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>觿年</span>。已振弥天之响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364135_comment'></div>道惟坚固。行乃头陀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364135_comment'></div>百结斯安。斥罗绡而不御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364135_comment'></div>十珍虽贵。对藜藿而甘心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364135_comment'></div>于时以丕应天人。大宏缁侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364135_comment'></div>法师至诚幽感。独步元宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364135_comment'></div>岂直王公钦振锡之风。固亦天子降同舆之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364135_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>宝瓶</span>宵注。则雨露随轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364135_comment'></div>玉柄朝撝。则风霜满席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364135_comment'></div>既而素怀有在。潜营摈俗之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364135_comment'></div>爰定我居。首托栖霞之寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364135_comment'></div>尔乃岩开石霤。邑跨金陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364135_comment'></div>鱼峰多赞呗之欢。虎溪有送迎之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364135_comment'></div>紫萝山径。居藏胜缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364135_comment'></div>青松涧户。坐谐幽致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364135_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>枕石漱流</span>者久之。原夫见化有缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364135_comment'></div>应身欲谢。昊天罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364135_comment'></div>追怀自远。故有诸天会聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364135_comment'></div>共位神光。列国交兵□□□译求其致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364135_comment'></div>岂不深哉。然则麟凤下灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364135_comment'></div>犹称瑞贶。玉石微玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364135_comment'></div>尚腾精彩。亦有楚铎沦照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364135_comment'></div>擢紫霭以冲星。周鼎沈华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364135_comment'></div>吐黄云而喷景。诚浩作者之述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364135_comment'></div>足称希代之贵。况乎释迦妙相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364135_comment'></div>如来真骨。虽八万四千之宝塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364135_comment'></div>散在群方。而九十二道之灵虹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364135_comment'></div>终闻间出。立诚斯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364135_comment'></div>瞻庭庑而时逢。非德不邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364135_comment'></div>历山川而罕致。是以忧填顿颡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364135_comment'></div>思存电下之光。波匿投身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364135_comment'></div>愿奉岩间之影。粤在梁武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364135_comment'></div>精求不暇。以为秦登碣石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364135_comment'></div>而事止寻仙。汉索瀛洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364135_comment'></div>而心非好善。于是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/145/Comments/0")'>斋筵</span>凤设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364135_comment'></div>上祈忉利之宫。讲帐星随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364135_comment'></div>下请龙王之藏。轻赍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/149/Comments/0")'>棹海</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364135_comment'></div>重赏梯山。庶玉匣之全移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364135_comment'></div>幸金棺之半启。以法师智遗人我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364135_comment'></div>识洞幽明。思假妙因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364135_comment'></div>冀通<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>灵感</span>。爰承纶綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364135_comment'></div>载践沧溟。过石门而右指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364135_comment'></div>历铜标而左顾。乘桴月沂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364135_comment'></div>戒楫星沼。相彼遐陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364135_comment'></div>实维荒裔。一音<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/165/Comments/0")'>演说</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364135_comment'></div>本承听受之乡。五日继明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364135_comment'></div>素隔照临之域。珍奇乃萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364135_comment'></div>圣德攸传。则知有感必臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364135_comment'></div>信覃幽境。不行而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364135_comment'></div>岂隔殊方。法师既达国城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364135_comment'></div>式敷朝命。受铣筐而顶礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364135_comment'></div>抚瑶缄而跪发。尽收其宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364135_comment'></div>重载而归。亦犹珠匿弊衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364135_comment'></div>须马鸣而后用。金藏陋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364135_comment'></div>待龙树而方开。梁氏之都妙算而仰神光家之繇也<span class='inlineComment2'>（十四字疑有脱误）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364135_comment'></div>炎凉可质。往返九十旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364135_comment'></div>楫柂不辍。风潮八千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364135_comment'></div>以大同三岁。届于兹邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364135_comment'></div>法师性丰幽澹。质固虚羸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364135_comment'></div>绵历是淹。疲疴屡积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364135_comment'></div>维摩见病。益伸方便之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364135_comment'></div>道安谢归。思远朝廷之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364135_comment'></div>愿居此刹。有诏许焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364135_comment'></div>仍分舍利。俾宏真福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364135_comment'></div>国惟瓯络。郡实番禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364135_comment'></div>尔其封疆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/206/Comments/0")'>跨蹑</span>之壮。海陆会同之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364135_comment'></div>上当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_104_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/208/Comments/0")'>星纪</span>。下裂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_104_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/209/Comments/0")'>坤维</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364135_comment'></div>阶百越而邻三吴。轵雕题而陬交趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364135_comment'></div>神仙气色。汀洲建不死之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364135_comment'></div>舜禹精灵。原隰现行宫之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364135_comment'></div>闾阎雾扑。士女云流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364135_comment'></div>讴歌有霸道之馀。毗俗得华风之杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364135_comment'></div>蜃楼高峙。犹埋夕帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364135_comment'></div>螺台峻积。尚识朝基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364135_comment'></div>信夷夏之奥区。而仙灵之窟宅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364135_comment'></div>此寺乃曩在宋朝。早延题目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364135_comment'></div>法师聿提神足。愿启规模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364135_comment'></div>爰于殿前。更须弥之塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364135_comment'></div>因缘盛力。人以子来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364135_comment'></div>徵日官而正墨。集风师而举草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364135_comment'></div>育王奔命。扫地户而献神兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364135_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_119_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/238/Comments/0")'>梵事</span>驰心。感天官而下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_119_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/239/Comments/0")'>灵匠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364135_comment'></div>崇阶遽积。宝树俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364135_comment'></div>不殊仙造。还如涌出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364135_comment'></div>故其粉画之妙。丹青之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364135_comment'></div>璿基岌其六峙。雕关纷其四照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364135_comment'></div>仙楹架雨。若披<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_124_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/249/Comments/0")'>云翳</span>之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364135_comment'></div>䌽槛临风。似遏扶摇之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364135_comment'></div>散<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_126_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/252/Comments/0")'>华珰</span>于月径。璧合非遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364135_comment'></div>拨罾网于星浔。珠连可验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364135_comment'></div>玉虬承霤。傃云窦而将骞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364135_comment'></div>金爵提甍。拂烟衢而待翥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364135_comment'></div>瑶窗绣户。洞达交辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364135_comment'></div>方井圆泉。参差倒景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364135_comment'></div>雕镌备勒。飞禽走兽之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364135_comment'></div>藻绘争开。复地<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_133_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/267/Comments/0")'>重天</span>之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364135_comment'></div>悬梁九息。良马踆走而未穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364135_comment'></div>謺磴三休。的卢骋犍而知倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364135_comment'></div>是栖银椁。用府琼函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364135_comment'></div>采舍卫之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_137_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/274/Comments/0")'>遗模</span>。得浮图之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364135_comment'></div>爰自梁末。以迄皇初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364135_comment'></div>城邑屡新。轩墀若旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364135_comment'></div>虽复百魔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_140_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/280/Comments/0")'>蜩沸</span>。听鼓铎而怀音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364135_comment'></div>六贼蜂屯。仰椽栾而革面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364135_comment'></div>多回净施。罕犯仁宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364135_comment'></div>则知遐吹所会。斯同偃草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364135_comment'></div>慈云所润。岂直流根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364135_comment'></div>故能比蜀守之祠堂。长为典制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364135_comment'></div>均鲁王之秘殿。若有明徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364135_comment'></div>宜其作镇一隅。俯炎荒而独秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364135_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_148_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/296/Comments/0")'>盘基</span>有地。冠终古而长存者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364135_comment'></div>国家业拥太初。事用皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364135_comment'></div>高祖以援危拨乱。伏紫气以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_150_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/301/Comments/0")'>登三</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364135_comment'></div>太宗以端拱继明。自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_151_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/303/Comments/0")'>黄离</span>而用九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364135_comment'></div>皇上缵乾坤之令业。振文武之英风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364135_comment'></div>太阶平而百度理。中国定而兆人乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364135_comment'></div>时和岁阜。邑颂涂歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364135_comment'></div>以五刑不用。六械徒设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364135_comment'></div>舟车四达。难论贡赋之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364135_comment'></div>襟带八荒。非复华夷之隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364135_comment'></div>天宝降。地符升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364135_comment'></div>木石甄祉。飞沈效庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364135_comment'></div>虽叶和制变。实赖文思之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364135_comment'></div>而持盈守成。亦资连帅之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364135_comment'></div>大中大夫使持节广韶等州都督李某。早登清贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364135_comment'></div>夙践崇轩。嘉猷迥发于天朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364135_comment'></div>善政果行于期月。越溪仙锷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364135_comment'></div>吐光芒而骇人。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_165_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/331/Comments/0")'>岱岭</span>寒松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364135_comment'></div>排风飙以成性。美哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364135_comment'></div>称由功著。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_167_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/335/Comments/0")'>鹘响</span>彻于云霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364135_comment'></div>方为时须。熊轼疲于道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364135_comment'></div>广陵单毂。如送张纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364135_comment'></div>浡海乱绳。复思龚遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364135_comment'></div>王尊皂盖。欣临折坂之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364135_comment'></div>吴隐朱軿。更集贪泉之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364135_comment'></div>高名夙著。佛化横飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364135_comment'></div>群盗屏迹而归农。奸吏闻风而去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364135_comment'></div>京坻坐积。圄犴潜回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364135_comment'></div>汲黯之卧淮扬。直闻清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364135_comment'></div>王堂之居汝郡。但举贤良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364135_comment'></div>用能使槛阱不施。猛兽巡江而远窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364135_comment'></div>市廛无扰。商旅倍道而相欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364135_comment'></div>飓风寝毒。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_180_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/361/Comments/0")'>炎埃</span>罢厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364135_comment'></div>人称有道。家实无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364135_comment'></div>加以援翰写心。自契真廉之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364135_comment'></div>高谈见意。不踰元默之津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364135_comment'></div>学究儒林。真穷释部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364135_comment'></div>知通人事。且味禅宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364135_comment'></div>道可以知归。物繇其显会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364135_comment'></div>是岁也。忽于此塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364135_comment'></div>重睹神光。玉林照灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364135_comment'></div>金山具足。倏来忽往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364135_comment'></div>类奔电之含云。吐燄流精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364135_comment'></div>若繁星之转汉。倾都共仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364135_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_192_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/384/Comments/0")'>溢郭</span>周窥。士女几乎数里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364135_comment'></div>光景动乎七重。实孟冬之日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364135_comment'></div>观夫至道不私。瑞生必由乎乐国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364135_comment'></div>庆基有会。福至必依于善人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364135_comment'></div>自非化足动微。教非饰迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364135_comment'></div>何以发真如之盛契。壮实相之辉华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364135_comment'></div>在昔凤集颍川。宣后归功于良守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364135_comment'></div>龙游湘浦。章帝布德于贤臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364135_comment'></div>历选前猷。兹为故实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364135_comment'></div>然后上和下睦。主圣臣良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364135_comment'></div>灭火返风。虽有辞于进壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364135_comment'></div>母修子应。亦何愧于当仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364135_comment'></div>至于百越衣缨。三阙耆老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364135_comment'></div>或代传篁竹。气推丹桂之城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364135_comment'></div>家擅芝兰。名动苍梧之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364135_comment'></div>出平原而袪甲。拥崇闼以鸣钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364135_comment'></div>并为蕃部之恩。亲睹招提之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364135_comment'></div>同祈介福。共洁斋坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364135_comment'></div>罄龙象于南州。尽衣钵于西竺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364135_comment'></div>会吞方仗。供备盂兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364135_comment'></div>法鼓振而沙界肃。洪钟锵而铁围净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364135_comment'></div>妙财爰舍。法施争流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364135_comment'></div>华毂牣于香城。文驷填于宝厩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364135_comment'></div>镪藏巨亿。更入僧田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364135_comment'></div>价直百千。还登佛座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364135_comment'></div>岂徒照车十乘。列隋氏之明珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364135_comment'></div>盈篚万金。积大颠之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_218_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/437/Comments/0")'>宝具</span>而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364135_comment'></div>朝散大夫守长史某。地乘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_219_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/439/Comments/0")'>华绪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364135_comment'></div>价偃名流。豫章擢而成干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364135_comment'></div>骐骥生而蹑影。山涛天骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364135_comment'></div>无情吏隐之间。王衍风神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364135_comment'></div>自出尘埃之表。自忝荣岭海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364135_comment'></div>作式瀛幽。略其小术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364135_comment'></div>包其大体。振温良之逸步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364135_comment'></div>得毗赞之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_226_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/452/Comments/0")'>宏纲</span>。布道移风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364135_comment'></div>善宠邦政。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_227_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/455/Comments/0")'>归休</span>置驿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364135_comment'></div>独守家声。然则野老行歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364135_comment'></div>虽致功于露冕。藩君坐啸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364135_comment'></div>固藉美于题舆。化成异壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1364135_comment'></div>抑由同德。故能道扬法教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1364135_comment'></div>挥斥盖缠。家怀方广之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1364135_comment'></div>人慕韦陀之学。传灯继爌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1364135_comment'></div>曳组成阴。下逮府寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1364135_comment'></div>旁周县寀。并志薰修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1364135_comment'></div>同希福慧。时有明威将军行禺府折冲都尉李公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1364135_comment'></div>天子之旧属。朝廷之夙将也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1364135_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_238_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/476/Comments/0")'>灵根</span>自远。圣族多奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1364135_comment'></div>受<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_239_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/478/Comments/0")'>睇盼</span>于甘泉。奉衣缨于平乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1364135_comment'></div>青龙带剑。先超殿阁之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364135_comment'></div>白虎衔珠。早陟斋坛之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364135_comment'></div>自招皇诞。作镇边城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1364135_comment'></div>湟水楼船。遂劳都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1364135_comment'></div>灞陵车马。尚识将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1364135_comment'></div>魂惊断雁之峰。恩尽沈鸢之浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1364135_comment'></div>濡鳞涸辙。处定水而弥勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1364135_comment'></div>抚翼香林。在穷途而更切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1364135_comment'></div>频光法会。荐委殊珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1364135_comment'></div>护持攸仰。招提是属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1364135_comment'></div>其兆基也如此。经纶黼藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1364135_comment'></div>其大矣哉。爰有上座宝轮等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1364135_comment'></div>并妙根宿值。胜果将圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1364135_comment'></div>翰飞般若之林。高步檀那之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1364135_comment'></div>慈衿密洞。散明月于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_254_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/509/Comments/0")'>谈筵</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1364135_comment'></div>智锷相辉。化繁霜于宝刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1364135_comment'></div>思雕琬璧。式播徽猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1364135_comment'></div>弟子家嗣太邱。忝闺门之薄宦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1364135_comment'></div>地连睢涣。窃藻绘之馀工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1364135_comment'></div>爰托下才。用旌高躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1364135_comment'></div>岂知仲宣旅泊。方衔深井之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1364135_comment'></div>长卿罢归。空负淩云之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1364135_comment'></div>我之怀矣。乃作铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1364135_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_263_1364135'>太息颓运。嗟乎失道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1364135_comment'></div>德弊为仁。物壮则老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1364135_comment'></div>絷猿情暗。求鸮计早。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1364135_comment'></div>赤水沈珠。元邱坠宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1364135_comment'></div>皇矣妙觉。蒸然应期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1364135_comment'></div>宗深微妙。业奥慈悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1364135_comment'></div>燃灯匡俗。舍筏济时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1364135_comment'></div>涅槃不住。般若无思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1364135_comment'></div>俯迹见生。和光不灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1364135_comment'></div>色音虽昧。规模尚切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1364135_comment'></div>猗欤上人。穆彼惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1364135_comment'></div>智倾八藏。心超六尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1364135_comment'></div>凄凉燬宅。解脱迷津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1364135_comment'></div>鸿冥伫想。龙蛰存身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1364135_comment'></div>青盖遗邦。黄旗故服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1364135_comment'></div>原隰形势。江山重复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1364135_comment'></div>涧户秋明。岩盘夜烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1364135_comment'></div>鼓钟于宫。声闻于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1364135_comment'></div>聿求紫闼。言寻丹濑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1364135_comment'></div>绝域栖遑。惊涛颠沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1364135_comment'></div>至诚冥感。神珍显会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1364135_comment'></div>甄陶设险。翼轸疏源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1364135_comment'></div>尉陀馀国。卢循旧边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1364135_comment'></div>邑居<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_286_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/572/Comments/0")'>雄盛</span>。人物殷全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1364135_comment'></div>是维乐土。实曰龙川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1364135_comment'></div>护持灵刹。庄严宝塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1364135_comment'></div>基构<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_289_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/578/Comments/0")'>鼎新</span>。亭栾栌嶪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1364135_comment'></div>奔日宵排。归云晓纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1364135_comment'></div>架壁三休。连甍四合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1364135_comment'></div>分惟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_292_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/584/Comments/0")'>星纪</span>。境控天池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1364135_comment'></div>栋宇绵邈。衡津推移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1364135_comment'></div>神机丕应。瑞景潜仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1364135_comment'></div>光合玉庑。彩动金枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1364135_comment'></div>凡我寮庶。同嗟权实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1364135_comment'></div>周顗情勤。王濛思逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1364135_comment'></div>咫尺幽键。往来<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_298_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/597/Comments/0")'>灵室</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1364135_comment'></div>共荫法堂。俱归慧日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1364135_comment'></div>四维信受。三明宏益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1364135_comment'></div>贝叶纷纶。龙华舄奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1364135_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_302_1364135", 1364135, "Clauses/604/Comments/0")'>讲肆</span>宏敞。齐筵巨翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1364135_comment'></div>供引纯陀。饭回香积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1364135_comment'></div>天人合契。幽显同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1364135_comment'></div>倾家奉贿。破产移琛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1364135_comment'></div>轩裳夐骛。缨佩交临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1364135_comment'></div>兰薰习远。檀那意深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1364135_comment'></div>伟哉连率。冲乎德化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1364135_comment'></div>职重隼裳。秩遵熊驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1364135_comment'></div>酌贪贻则。还淳息诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1364135_comment'></div>道济香城。祯凝宝舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1364135_comment'></div>琳琅什种。梓缁徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1364135_comment'></div>调轻僧会。辨析文殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1364135_comment'></div>奔螭易失。令鼠难拘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1364135_comment'></div>愿刊贞珉。永冠康衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1364135_comment'></div>伊我穷途。欣兹胜谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1364135_comment'></div>文休泛海。仲翔游越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1364135_comment'></div>倘想知音。有怀明发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1364135_comment'></div>谬惟雅顾。叨陪天骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1364135_comment'></div>爰抽弱翰。式叙高踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1364135_comment'></div>孤音易竭。独赏难逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1364135_comment'></div>思起王粲。悲生蔡邕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1364135_comment'></div>岂无章甫。谁适为容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1364135_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_324_1364135_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
